# 1987宇宙组曲 - 1987 Cosmic Overture

## 目录

- CO-01 避雨指南 / How to Find Shelter
- CO-02 旅行者们 / The Voyagers
- CO-03 意义的意义 / The Meaning of Meaning
- CO-04 崭新的，美丽的 / Beautiful New Things
- CO-05 时间简谱 / A Score of Time
- CO-06 比旅程更险恶的 / What's Worse than the Journey
- CO-07 园圃与花园 / The Wilds and the Garden
- CO-08 当日子往前 / When We Move Forward
- CO-09 致陌生人 / To Former Strangers
- CO-10 冻雨天 / A Freezing Rain
- CO-11 偶然的诗 / Poems Come By Chance
- CO-12 《协奏曲》 / Concerto
- CO-13 永恒春天的地方 / Where Ever Spring Stays
- CO-14 追星星的人 / We Who Chase the Stars
- CO-15 告别时刻 / Time to Say Goodbye
- CO-16 奶油饺子汤 / What's About Time
- CO-17 蛇靠星星证明 / The Measure of a Melusine
- CO-18 墓志铭 / Epitaph
- CO-19 你并不孤单 / You Are Not Alone
- CO-20 宇宙无事发生 / As If Nothing Happened up There

## CO-01 避雨指南 / How to Find Shelter

**？？？**：呼……再来一次深呼吸，然后……放轻松……\
**???**: *breathing* Take a deep breath, and relax.

**？？？**：第一场演出最不能失败。这关系着我的、科兹洛夫的、大家的荣誉……\
**???**: This is my debut. I can't fail, not now. I have to do this for Mr. and Mrs. Kozlov and everyone in the circus. I must make them proud.

**？？？**：娜塔莉亚女士教过，重点是让吸进的气流在身体里找到平衡。\
**???**: Mrs. Kozlov told me that I must guide the air through my body until it finds its balance.

**？？？**：左脚，右脚——好。接下来，适当地伸手和观众打招呼。\
**???**: Left, right. Good. Now, wave to the audience and say hello.

**？？？**：啊，糟糕。\
**???**: Oh, no!

**？？？**：不，别着急，我能做到……\
**???**: I can do this. I'm almost there.

先站稳。在一根纤细的钢丝上找到立足之地。\
Steady yourself. Find your footing on a strand-thin wire.

它真的存在吗？\
Is it even there?

**？？？**：我能应对一切……只要先……\
**???**: I can have this handled. First, I need to ...

**？？？**：我——\
**???**: I ...

**？？？**：宇宙中没有绝对的方向之分，下落同时也能是上升。这取决于你使用的参照体系。\
**???**: There's no absolute direction up there. Up or down depends on the reference you choose.

**？？？**：她有权知道“暴雨”意味着什么。\
**???**: I think she has the right to know what the "Storm" really is.

**？？？**：我们要先抵达九九年之后的世界。\
**???**: We will still need to cross the year 1999.

**？？？**：阿涅娅。回家。\
**???**: Alia. Come home.

**？？？**：库珀花环。\
**???**: Kiperina.

**？？？**：生命体征，平稳。各项指标均有回升。\
**???**: Vitals are stable. Biometrics returning to normal.

病床前的拉普拉斯研究员尚未褪去奔波的疲惫。医疗职员揣摩着她的心情，斟酌词句说明目前的状况。\
The Laplace researcher still hasn't shaken off the weariness of her journey. The medic examines her closely, weighing her emotions as she explains the current situation.

**医疗职员**：我听说您之前不在发射基地，没想到还是第一时间赶回了这里……\
**Medical Staff Member**: I'd heard you'd already left. Never thought you'd be back so quickly.

**医疗职员**：既然您这样关心他们，我想您应该能明白我接下来这些话的意思，指针女士。\
**Medical Staff Member**: It's obvious you care about them. So, I'm sure you know what to do when they wake up, Ms. Pointer.

指针点了点头，目光依然落在床边那些医疗仪器闪烁的屏幕上。\
Pointer gives a nod, her eyes fixed, scanning the blinking screens beside the bed.

**医疗职员**：实验事故造成的外伤并不严重，库珀花环小姐只是需要休息。\
**Medical Staff Member**: She hasn't suffered any serious trauma. All that Ms. Kiperina here needs is rest.

**医疗职员**：考虑到她的身体状况，我不建议她立刻离开病房。\
**Medical Staff Member**: But considering her condition, I recommend she stays here a few days longer for observation.

指针没有回应这句话。在几秒钟的停顿后，她开口询问。\
Pointer doesn't respond. After a long silence, she speaks.

**指针**：辛苦了。其他人的情况怎么样？\
**Pointer**: Thank you. What's the status of the others?

**医疗职员**：冷周六小姐要好些，之前还醒来了十五分钟。\
**Medical Staff Member**: Ms. Hissabeth is fine. She was awake earlier, for a few minutes anyway.

**医疗职员**：利用这点儿时间，她迅速要求签署了遗体捐献协议书。甚至没忘记让她的兄弟姐妹们也签字。\
**Medical Staff Member**: She signed a donor card. Managed to get all her other siblings to sign it too. Not sure what we'd even do with them.

**医疗职员**：……另外两位先生和她做了差不多的事。\
**Medical Staff Member**: That gentleman and that little salamander guy did the same thing when they woke up.

**医疗职员**：这倒都没什么，疯子我见得够多了。麻烦的是决定治疗方案。太多细节都要注意，特殊剂量、抗药性……而且我没有任何动物医疗经验，只能申请协助。\
**Medical Staff Member**: Anyway, it's no cause for concern. I've seen my share of lunatics just like them. The real problem is determining treatment. There are so many details to pay attention to when dealing with these special patients: the dosage, their drug resistance ... And I'm not a vet, you know. I had to seek out some professional consultation.

**医疗职员**：虽然这么说不太合适，但还好您没有参与这次……勇敢的尝试。不然我连一个帮手也找不着了。\
**Medical Staff Member**: No offense, but I'm glad you weren't part of this ... attempt; otherwise, I might have had to face all of this by myself.

指针的目光从病床上收回。她直视着职员的眼睛。\
Pointer faces away from the bed and looks the staff member straight in the eye.

**指针**：我不赞成他们，但他们毕竟也算是我的组员。\
**Pointer**: I may not have approved of their taking on this project, but I'm still on the team.

**指针**：如果哪天有了规制法案，教会这群家伙重视生命，我一定双手双脚赞成。\
**Pointer**: *sigh* If only the Foundation could devise regulations sufficient to control our staff's recklessness with their own lives.

**医疗职员**：举个例子，首先限制苦目糖的使用？\
**Medical Staff Member**: Hmm. Maybe they should consider controlling access to Picrasma Candy?

**指针**：噢，这就算了吧。我自己偶尔也会多来两颗。\
**Pointer**: Ugh, forget that. Even I can't help exceeding the recommended dosage sometimes.

**医疗职员**：下个月我就要调任去康复中心总部了，我会帮你问问那儿的苦目糖平均用量。\
**Medical Staff Member**: I'll be reporting to the headquarters of the Rehab Center next month. I'll let you know their average dosage by then.

**医疗职员**：但现在，比起这个，我看得先给来探病的人排张时间表……\
**Medical Staff Member**: Anyway, I need to write up a visitors' schedule. We have to make sure our patients get enough rest.

第二位来访者很好地说明了时间表之必要。\
The second visitor proves just how necessary a proper schedule can be.

**？？？**：她的情况还好吗？我刚从另一边的病房过来。\
**???**: How's she doing? I just left the other ward and thought I might drop by.

突然响起的声音礼貌而亲切，但依旧让两位职员吃了一惊。\
The new voice is polite and warm but still startles them.

**指针**：您好，北方哨歌女士。\
**Pointer**: Hello, Ms. Windsong.

**医疗职员**：根据今天的检查结果来看，库珀花环小姐的身体情况已经基本稳定。\
**Medical Staff Member**: Her vitals have stabilized. We're monitoring her recovery, but the initial results are positive.

**医疗职员**：我们无法确保她何时苏醒。但好消息是，预期时间为这周内。\
**Medical Staff Member**: We can't say precisely when she'll wake up, but it shouldn't take more than a week.

**北方哨歌**：辛苦了。我会常来探望——严格按照规定行动，尽量少添麻烦，我记着呢。\
**Windsong**: Good to hear. I'll be by to visit them from time to time, following the schedule, of course. Let me know if it's too much trouble.

**医疗职员**：这间病房还好，隔离室几乎静音。在常规病房内的确需要保持安静。\
**Medical Staff Member**: You're welcome to drop by here anytime. The isolation room is soundproof, but do keep it down when you visit the other wards.

**北方哨歌**：我理解，我理解。我只是有些担心，而且维拉女士和阿夫西维总是在信里问起大家的近况。\
**Windsong**: Of course. I'm just worried about them, you know. Besides, Vila and Avgust have drowned me in letters asking about the project.

**北方哨歌**：老师和学生多少都会挂念对方，这也没办法。\
**Windsong**: More importantly, there's a bond between a teacher and her student.

**医疗职员**：明白。我正好也该去忙其他事了。如果碰上什么问题，就用那边的呼叫按钮找我。\
**Medical Staff Member**: I understand. I'll check in on the others. If you need any help, press that button to call me.

**医疗职员**：顺带一提，指针女士——祝您的组员一切顺利！\
**Medical Staff Member**: By the way, Ms. Pointer, Godspeed to you and your team!

**医疗职员**：一群打算上太空的疯子，我觉得还挺酷的。\
**Medical Staff Member**: A bunch of lunatics working together to reach space. Pretty damn cool, I'd say.

这是句意料外的称赞，指针的脸上明明白白地写满了惊讶。\
It's an unexpected and unorthodox compliment. The surprise is written all over Pointer's face.

**北方哨歌**：我也希望一切顺利。\
**Windsong**: Ditto.

**指针**：……您真的认为我们能成功？\
**Pointer**: Are you being serious? Do you think it's possible we could succeed?

**北方哨歌**：您瞧，“我们”。您不是已经打算退出这个小组了吗？\
**Windsong**: Listen to yourself, "we." Weren't you quitting the team?

短暂的沉默之后，她们默契地略过了对方的反问。\
After a short silence, they decide not to answer either question.

北方哨歌率先迈开步子，指针跟着她来到走廊，回手带上了房门。\
Windsong takes the first step, and Pointer follows her into the hallway, pulling the door shut behind them.

**北方哨歌**：看来您并没有像声称的那样，坚持认为冷周六的想法不切实际。\
**Windsong**: Your comment on Hissabeth's project, you said it was "unrealistic." I don't think you really meant that.

**北方哨歌**：干脆回来搭把手？我觉得利用传送软盘是个很不错的主意，而且实验失败本就是常事。\
**Windsong**: But, even if you do, why not stay and give them a hand? Their latest ideas for the teleportation disk sound solid to me. This one failure shouldn't be enough to walk away.

**北方哨歌**：你和冷周六合作过这么久，理应比我更清楚她是不是在做无用功。\
**Windsong**: You've worked with Hissabeth long enough. I'm sure you'd already know if she's pursuing a fool's errand.

指针又一次选择了沉默。但北方哨歌并没有再次与她达成默契。\
Pointer chooses silence again. But this time, Windsong presses her concern.

**北方哨歌**：你到底怎么想？\
**Windsong**: So, what do you really think?

**指针**：我怎么想不重要。我劝过他们很多次，停下吧，到这里就可以了。\
但他们听得越多就越打算坚持。\
**Pointer**: My thoughts are unimportant. All attempts to talk them out of it have failed, and what's worse, the more forcefully I attempt to dissuade them, the more determined they become.

**北方哨歌**：我只想知道你是否认为冷周六他们必定失败。\
**Windsong**: Alright, so lay it on me: why are they doomed to fail?

**指针**：难道我必须站在这里一五一十地向你剖析我的想法？\
**Pointer**: I see no reason to expend any energy explaining it.

北方哨歌指向她的身后，那间她们刚刚离开的医务室。\
Windsong gestures at the ward behind her.

**北方哨歌**：我有自己的判断。\
**Windsong**: Whatever. I'll just have to make my own judgments on the matter.

**指针**：……\
**Pointer**: ...

**指针**：冷周六是一位很好的研究员，足够敏锐，也向来果断。我从来没有不信任她。\
**Pointer**: Hissabeth is an excellent researcher, sharp and decisive. On those merits alone, she's earned my trust.

**指针**：但谁来保证计划百分百成功，谁来面对失败的后果？不是进医务室躺几个月、几年，而是——\
**Pointer**: My analysis points to a dangerous level of uncertainty in this project. The price of failure, even optimistically, could be much worse than a few days in recovery. There could be more permanent injuries. They could even ...

她的肩膀在发颤，但她的声音异常的平静和稳定。\
Her shoulders shrink in, but her voice remains calm.

**指针**：这是我的个人想法，我希望自己的同事们能……活下去。\
**Pointer**: My nature compels me to do whatever I can to reduce the danger to our staff, and I want to keep my friends alive.

**指针**：就算真到了太空，拿到了数据，明白了宇宙是否会被“暴雨”冲刷……\
**Pointer**: What does it matter if we make it into space and discover whether the "Storm" affects the whole universe?

**指针**：即使宇宙不受影响，我们又能怎么办？逃去一颗新的星球？\
**Pointer**: Say that we determine this phenomenon only affects Earth, then what? We can't leave. We don't have the technology to fly off somewhere else.

**指针**：如果“暴雨”连我们头顶的群星都会带走，那知道这样的结果又有什么意义？\
**Pointer**: And if instead we determine the "Storm" is indeed universal, and that it will inevitably swallow up the stars, well, then wouldn't it all be pointless?

**指针**：这个答案并不值得如此追求。\
**Pointer**: Either way, my calculations are clear: the answer is not worth our lives.

**北方哨歌**：如果你真的这样想，应该把刚刚的话说给他们听。\
**Windsong**: That's how you feel, I get it, so why not tell them?

**指针**：我在等一个合适的机会。\
**Pointer**: I've been attempting to find the right time to say it.

理线学者耸了耸肩，她已经得知了自己需要的答案。\
The ley lines scholar shrugs. She has the answer she came for.

**北方哨歌**：总之，我这里有个新消息。虽然你很快也会知道。\
**Windsong**: Maybe so. Speaking of things to say, I've got some news, and I thought it was better you hear it from me.

**北方哨歌**：发射基地将逐步开始清空撤离，最迟半个月后，至少拉普拉斯的所有职员都必须离开。\
**Windsong**: Laplace has decided to evacuate the spaceport. All staff on-site are to be relocated before the end of the month.

**指针**：撤离？有不少难以搬运的设备，要去哪里？而且你应该清楚这里的很多项目和国家合作开发……\
**Pointer**: Evacuate? Where to? There is critical equipment here that can't be moved in that time frame. Besides, this spaceport was a part of our active partnership with the local government.

她猛然抬起头，北方哨歌没有回避她的视线。\
She lifts her head, and Windsong doesn't shy away from her gaze.

**指针**：……回真正的、不受影响的普列谢茨克分部，北极圈边缘，对不对？\
**Pointer**: Ah, we're moving to our real branch in Plesetsk, aren't we? The one on the edge of the Arctic Circle that's proven immune to the "Storm."

**指针**：这是“暴雨”应急预案！\
**Pointer**: This is our "Storm" Emergency Plan!

**北方哨歌**：是的。\
**Windsong**: You've got it.

**北方哨歌**：拉普拉斯职员回去报到后，可以在休养中心度过一周。那些不属于科算中心管辖的员工，他们将从今天起迎来带薪假期。\
**Windsong**: All Laplace employees are to spend a week in the care center after reporting to Plesetsk. The local staff will be put on paid vacation as is usual.

她们都清楚这场“带薪假期”将何时中止。\
They both know exactly when this "paid vacation" will come to an end.

**北方哨歌**：冷周六也在等合适的时机。现在她等到了。\
**Windsong**: Hissabeth was also waiting for the right time, and I guess this is it.

**北方哨歌**：帮她签名吧。放心，这份不是捐献协议。\
**Windsong**: Sign this for her, will you? Don't worry. It's not a donor card.

一张纸被递到面前。\
A sheet of paper is held out to her.

**指针**：你要我向路德维希先生提交申请，叫他特批我的组员留下送死？\
**Pointer**: You're asking me to sign this so that my teammates can stay here and die in the "Storm"?

**北方哨歌**：不，我只是帮忙转交它。\
**Windsong**: I'm not asking. I'm only delivering it to you.

**北方哨歌**：他们相当清楚自己要面对的困难。这不是一次徒有勇气的赌博。\
**Windsong**: But they know what they're doing here.

**北方哨歌**：所以我愿意尽举手之劳。\
**Windsong**: That's why I want to help.

**指针**：……我现在没心情考虑。之后再说。\
**Pointer**: I need some time. My analysis won't be objective right now.

**北方哨歌**：别让你的组员等得太久，这很可能是最后的机会。\
**Windsong**: Sure. Just don't keep your teammates waiting. Our time is short.

**指针**：……\
**Pointer**: ...

她把那张纸用力塞进了外套口袋，隔着玻璃看向病床上静静沉睡的女孩。\
She places the paper neatly into her pocket, then returns to the glass to watch over the sleeping girl in the hospital bed.

在几个月前，她们还未曾料想到事情会发展到如此境地。\
A few months ago, none of them could have imagined it would come to this.

## CO-02 旅行者们 / The Voyagers

**电台节目**：“不久前，旅行者二号已顺利抵达天王星，完成了人类历史上首次对这颗星球进行的探测活动，并按计划对天王星环系统进行了考察……”\
**Radio**: "Not long ago, Voyager 2 successfully reached Uranus, marking the first-ever exploration of this planet in human history. It conducted an examination of Uranus's ring system as planned ..."

**电台节目**：“由于探访土卫六造成的临时轨道变动，旅行者一号仍在飞往太阳系边缘……”\
**Radio**: "After a temporary orbital adjustment caused by its earlier visit to Titan, Voyager 1 continues its journey towards the edge of the solar system ..."

**电台节目**：“它们今后的旅程……”\
**Radio**: "Their future ..."

冷静的新闻播报声骤然中断。\
The staticky but steady voice of the news cuts out.

**冷周六**：它们接下来要去哪里，做了什么，都是已经确认的结果，不用听过时的消息啦。\
**Hissabeth**: We already know where they're going and what they're gonna do. Why are you wasting time on old news?

**冷周六**：我记得拉普拉斯的资料库里还收藏过1990年旅行者一号拍的照片。\
**Hissabeth**: As I recall, we've even got a photo from Voyager 1 taken in 1990. It's stored somewhere in the Laplace archives.

**指针**：也有三进制计算机和流星余迹通信技术的研发报告。\
**Pointer**: That's correct. They even have the development reports from Setun and the work done on meteor burst communication tech.

**指针**：但资料库里没有记载过那张金唱片的下落，对不对？\
**Pointer**: But none of the archives mention the whereabouts of the Golden Records, do they?

**指针**：说不定在哪次播报里就会提到，“根据旅行者一号骤然减少的质量，我们判断，其上搭载的唱片已经被不知名的存在截获……”\
**Pointer**: So there is a chance we'll hear some new clue this time around, like "According to the sudden decrease in Voyager 1's mass, it's been speculated that the Golden Records were intercepted by an unknown entity ..."

**冷周六**：“截获”听起来像星际海盗。\
**Hissabeth**: "Intercepted," you make it sound like it was stolen by aliens, or space pirates!

**指针**：我想海盗应该对一张小小的金唱片不感兴趣。\
**Pointer**: A space pirate? I doubt they would have any interest in some ordinary records.

**指针**：说吧，按掉我的收音机是为了什么要紧事？\
**Pointer**: Now why don't you get to the point? What's so urgent that you had to switch off the radio?

**冷周六**：简单小事。他们说录像最好不要有太多杂音。\
**Hissabeth**: Oh, I'm making a video. I didn't want the sound drowning out the recording.

**冷周六**：现在差不多够安静了——\
**Hissabeth**: Should be quiet enough now.

1986 4月 普列谢茨克发射基地\
April 1986, Plesetsk Cosmodrome

Hissabeth, Laplace Researcher.

**冷周六**：冷周六，拉普拉斯研究中心职员。

加入计划的原因？爱好而已。\
So, why was I mad enough to join this project? Call it a matter of personal interest.

Правда? “真的吗？”\
Правда? "Really"?

为了避免你太惊讶，我会做个更详细点的介绍。\
Let me introduce myself in a little more detail, in case you're shocked when you get your first look at me.

**小蛇Ⅰ**：到地方没有？该死，我讨厌一切爬行以外的交通方式！\
**Snake I**: Are we there yet? Drats! This is no way to travel! Let me just slither please.

**小蛇Ⅴ**：但你绝大多数时间都在“搭乘交通工具”。\
**Snake V**: We don't have a choice. We're stuck with this most unfortunate mode of transportation.

迪布瓦家族兄弟姐妹中的九分之二。以聒噪为美德。\
Introducing two of the nine siblings of the Dubois family, always loudly at odds and proud of it.

或许是天气太冷，其他家伙将所有时间都用来睡觉。感谢他们的沉默，让我还能保留点耐心。\
Thanks to the cold weather, the others're still brumating, so they haven't yet tested my patience.

由远及近的脚步声促使他们抬头张望。\
Footsteps grow nearer, prompting them to look around for their source.

**接待员**：您好，我来接您前往办公室。\
**Receptionist**: Welcome. Let me walk you to your office.

**接待员**：请先出示您的工牌……\
**Receptionist**: Your ID card, please.

**小蛇Ⅰ**：嘶嘶。\
**Snake I**: Hiss.

**接待员**：啊，抱歉——！\
**Receptionist**: Oh, my apologies!

My patience just ran out.

**冷周六**：我的耐心耗尽了。

小蛇灵活地偏开身子，但它躲得不够快，只能被迫闭紧嘴巴。\
The snake twists its body away with agility, but not fast enough. It is forced to clamp its mouth shut.

**冷周六**：多谢您为我领路。\
**Hissabeth**: Thank you for showing me the way.

**冷周六**：再走快些怎么样？这地方的温度连开口说句话都够呛。\
**Hissabeth**: Why don't we speed up a bit? This place feels as cold as a goddamn morgue. I can barely talk without shivering.

到了目的地，我会再次、再次、再次教他们不要随便吓唬同事。\
When we get to the office, I'll warn them not to scare our colleagues for the fourth time.

**接待员**：您放心，办公室内的暖气二十四小时开启。拉普拉斯不会忽略这种细节。\
**Receptionist**: Of course. We'll ensure the heat is kept on 24/7 inside your office. Laplace never neglects the little details.

In truth, as a reptile enthusiast, she's just trying to hide the rudeness of her surprise at seeing the cute snakes.

**接待员**：就是这里。您直接敲门就好，指针女士应该正在里面等您。\
**Receptionist**: Here we are. Go ahead and knock on the door. Ms. Pointer should be expecting you.

**接待员**：对了，刚才您提到了气候问题，请问您可爱的宠物是否需要恒温箱？\
**Receptionist**: By the way, since you mentioned the cold weather, do you need a thermostat for your lovely pets?

**接待员**：我们会在合理范围内尽量满足每位研究员的需求。\
**Receptionist**: We try our best to meet all of our researchers' needs.

**冷周六**：噢，没事。我的外套参考了一些类似原理，完全够用。\
**Hissabeth**: Oh, we're all good. My coat works as a kind of thermo-regulated insulator. It should be fine.

**接待员**：好的。另外，发射基地的这处办公场地专为合作研究建设。如果您有事前往拉普拉斯专用办公楼，记得提前提交访问申请。\
**Receptionist**: Understood. And please note that the spaceport here is just a part of our local research collaboration. Laplace's official branch in Plesetsk is actually further north, right on the edge of the Arctic Circle.

**接待员**：那儿在极圈附近，过去有些远，来往管控也很严格。为避免耽误日程，希望您记住这一流程。\
**Receptionist**: It has a strict security policy. So, you'll need to file an application before visiting. There's no guarantee it will be approved either.

**接待员**：普列谢茨克发射基地研究所，欢迎您的加入。\
**Receptionist**: Welcome to the Plesetsk Cosmodrome.

接待员刚走出几步，又被细微的声响吸引着回过头。\
Just a few steps out, the receptionist turns back, drawn by a faint sound.

鳞片金黄的小蛇朝她吐着信子，似乎还瞧得见它眨了眨眼。\
The little golden-scaled snake flicks its tongue at her, and—was that a wink?

**接待员**：再见，小家伙。\
**Receptionist**: Goodbye, little hissie.

研究员的背影消失在走廊尽头，愉快的说话声再次响起。\
The researcher disappears down the hall, and cheerful voices ring out again.

**小蛇Ⅰ**：你知道吗，二号？我觉得这地方的人对我们更友好。\
**Snake I**: You know what, Two, I think the staff here are more accommodating than most types we meet.

**冷周六**：你的素质简直越来越差了。\
**Hissabeth**: Or, are you just being more of a jerk than usual?

**冷周六**：不准用编号叫我。还有，别惹太多麻烦。\
**Hissabeth**: Now stay out of trouble, and don't call me by my number again.

**冷周六**：再收到任何关于“实验动物被偷吃”的投诉，我就给你打结。\
**Hissabeth**: Just so you know, I'm perfectly willing to tie you up by the tails if I start hearing about any "missing lab rats."

在家族辩论赛正式打响前，房门及时地敞开了。\
The door swings open, preventing the escalation of their family feud.

**冷周六**：——？\
**Hissabeth**: ...?

**指针**：我听到外面有动静，原来真有人。\
**Pointer**: I knew I heard someone talking behind the door. Glad my ears don't need tuning.

**指针**：别杵在门口。你就是那个主动申请调来这里的研究员？\
**Pointer**: Please, come in. Are you the new researcher on this project?

**冷周六**：看样子，你是我的新同事？\
**Hissabeth**: You've got it. So, I take it you're one of my new colleagues?

新同事的态度谈不上欢迎。\
The new colleague's attitude seems cold to the touch.

但踏进房间，看清楚所有陈设后，她意识到这点细节已经是最不重要的。\
But once she steps inside and takes in the whole setup, she realizes that details like that won't matter too much.

**冷周六**：两台设备，两把椅子……两张制式办公桌。\
**Hissabeth**: Two devices, two chairs, and two standard-issue desks.

**冷周六**：整个组就只有我们两个？\
**Hissabeth**: Is it just the two of us?

**指针**：当然不，记得保持严谨！组里有足足三个人。不过第三个人从来没在公示名单以外的地方出现。\
**Pointer**: I expected you to be more rigorous as a fellow Laplace researcher! According to official records, we have a third researcher on the team, an attache from the local government. In theory anyway, no one has ever seen or heard of them. It's just a name on the noticeboard.

**指针**：暂时别算上那位政府派来的协作者——我用这个词完全是出于尊重——这里确实只有两位员工。\
**Pointer**: However, if you insist on ignoring our esteemed coworker—who I mention out of deep respect for our local partners—then correct, it's just the two of us.

**指针**：怎么样，也算是个惊喜吧？至少项目经费怎么用只需要我俩做决定。\
**Pointer**: So, what do you think of our setup? It's not so bad. At least, we're in full control of our budget.

**指针**：当然也别指望能有多少。\
**Pointer**: Although, I recommend setting those budget expectations low.

**冷周六**：行，和我预想中也挺接近，特殊时期的边缘项目……\
**Hissabeth**: Cool, cool. Everything's more or less as I expected—an undervalued project in extraordinary times.

**冷周六**：到底是谁想到要用传送术式往航天器上送补给？我真佩服那家伙的想象力。\
**Hissabeth**: What kind of bizarre mind hatched up the idea of teleporting supplies directly into space?

**指针**：你觉得这是异想天开？\
**Pointer**: Do you believe our goals are unrealistic?

**冷周六**：当然不，充分利用一切知识才是科学研究的秘诀，我一向赞成神秘学与科技的结合。\
**Hissabeth**: Not at all. Only eclectic, let's say. And I've always been a fan of eclectic theories. They are often a stepping stone to true discovery.

**冷周六**：这一定会是科学发展的主流趋势，尽管现在还不是，但……\
**Hissabeth**: I'm certain that the combination of arcanum and science will one day make up the core of our civilization. We're not there yet, but ...

**指针**：但未来一定会的。或许改变的第一步就是从这个项目开始。\
**Pointer**: It's only a matter of time. Perhaps this project will be the next leap forward.

**指针**：要是能改进传送术式的缺陷，解决它单程、不稳定、距离过短的问题，这就不会再是边缘项目。\
**Pointer**: So far, the teleport disk we've developed is functional but unstable. It's a one-way ticket capable of travel only within a short distance. But if we can improve its range and stability, I calculate its value to society to be potentially earth-shaking.

**冷周六**：看来我们的合作会很顺利。\
**Hissabeth**: Looks like we'll make for quite a team.

她拿起桌面上堆叠的材料，给自己腾出一小块便于倚靠的空间。\
She picks up the stack of files from the desk, clearing a small spot to lean against.

**冷周六**：为了我们共同的目标，当务之急是先做出些值得填上报告书的东西。\
**Hissabeth**: But before that, we'll have to make sure our project isn't shut down before it can begin, which means we need to cook up something worthwhile to put in our report.

**指针**：我知道你擅长的是空间材料科学。需要什么，这位专家？我来帮您想办法。\
**Pointer**: To that end, I know you're an expert in aerospace materials. Are there any specific specimens you need? I'll do what I can to source them for you.

**指针**：考虑到审批流程、运输时间，还有其他一系列影响因素，我今天得提交新的领用单。\
**Pointer**: Oh, but be quick. Our resource applications must be submitted today. The evaluation process and all other little details mean it will take some time to arrive.

**冷周六**：我想想，也没什么特别的……你怕不怕鱼？\
**Hissabeth**: Let me see. Hmm, no, I don't have any particular needs for now. How do you feel about fish?

这次话题实在转折得太快，即使是惯于处理信息的大脑也无法立刻做出反应。\
Even Pointer's keen analytical mind struggles to keep up with the rapid topic change.

指针停顿了足足三秒，还是决定回答这个荒谬的问题。\
She pauses a full three seconds before answering.

**指针**：……不怕。我对你养在头上的小宠物也没有意见。\
**Pointer**: They're fine, as are those pets you've got dangling in your hair.

**冷周六**：好，看来我的确来对了地方，没人会反对我关于鱼类养殖的这点儿爱好。\
**Hissabeth**: Cool. Looks like I've come to exactly the right place. No nosy layabouts around to moan about my hobbies.

**冷周六**：至于我头上的生物——这是另一件事，虽然我是没把身份背景贴在脸上，但好歹在档案里……你没看。\
**Hissabeth**: Speaking of those "pets," they're not really pets. I remember mentioning them in my profile. You didn't read it, hmm?

**冷周六**：“能多个帮手就不错，管他是谁呢！”然后把文件随手摞在废纸堆顶层。我猜对了？\
**Hissabeth**: "Whatever, so long as they can hold their own!" Then you threw the file into the trash. Am I right?

**指针**：真聪明。我扫了两眼，记得你的研究方向和过往经验。其他东西不重要。\
**Pointer**: It wasn't quite so dramatic, but yes. I briefly scanned it for your field of expertise and experience. Nothing else mattered to me.

**冷周六**：但也得解释清楚嘛。蛇发女妖和蛇打从出生起就在一块儿，比起宠物，更像同胞的兄弟姐妹。\
**Hissabeth**: Still, you should get to know your new colleagues. I'm a Melusine. We have snakes for hair. So, they're not pets. They're my siblings.

**冷周六**：——所以你其实多了九位同事，算上我在内。够不够惊喜？\
**Hissabeth**: Technically, you've got yourself a grand total of nine new coworkers. Surprise!

**指针**：很新奇的知识。可惜我们恐怕发不出九份补贴。\
**Pointer**: That is certainly new information. It's unfortunate that Laplace doesn't pay out their Sharpodonties by head.

**冷周六**：五份？\
**Hissabeth**: Maybe I can convince them to go in for every two heads?

**指针**：正常发放，可以在常规份额上额外增加饮食津贴。\
**Pointer**: I wouldn't predict your chances to be high, but a larger food allowance seems appropriate, given your additional mouths to feed.

**冷周六**：加上单间办公室，我需要地方放我的生态缸。鱼类和绿植有助于放松心情。\
**Hissabeth**: Mind requesting me a corner office? I need a lot of space for my fish tank. Pets and plants help me cool off.

**指针**：那就推进进度，把报告书写完，申请新办公室——一人一间，怎么样？\
**Pointer**: Whatever you want, let's just finish the report as soon as possible. Then we can apply for additional office space—one room for each of us. Deal?

**冷周六**：成交。\
**Hissabeth**: Deal.

协议达成。指针顺势抬起右手，打算来个友善的击掌。\
Agreement reached. Pointer lifts her right hand.

小蛇抢先一步探出身子，用头顶轻轻碰了碰指针的掌心。\
A snake stretches forward to gently tap her palm with its head.

**指针**：合作愉快。\
**Pointer**: Nice working with you.

## CO-03 意义的意义 / The Meaning of Meaning

1987 5月 普列谢茨克发射基地\
May 1987, Plesetsk Cosmodrome

我们的合作的确很愉快，一切都按照计划顺利进行。\
Everything from there on went smoothly and according to schedule. It was a genuine pleasure working with Pointer.

至少那时候还是这么回事。\
Well, those first days at least.

**指针**：冷周六，你有没有听昨天的理线学讲座？\
**Pointer**: Hissabeth, did you go to that ley lines lecture yesterday?

**指针**：我连着检查了十几个小时的数据，根本没空……\
**Pointer**: I couldn't make it. I've been reviewing this data for the last 10 hours.

**指针**：有可能是原本的术式转写后漏了些字符，也可能是航天系统编译器有问题。天知道到底是什么让模型一塌糊涂。\
**Pointer**: The model is a mess. Something's off. I can't isolate the issue. It could be the system compiler, or the incantation. Or, maybe we missed some characters when we transcoded it.

**冷周六**：嗯？噢，我前几天在食堂碰到北方哨歌，她的确提过讲座的事，你等等。\
**Hissabeth**: Hmm? Oh, the lecture? Yeah, Windsong mentioned it when we met her at the canteen a few days ago. Hold on.

椅子转了小半圈，窝在里面的研究员站起身伸了个懒腰，放下手里的面包。\
The chair swivels halfway, and Hissabeth stands, stretching before setting her bread aside.

一条叼着数据卡的小蛇出现在指针的脚边。\
A snake holding a data card slithers up to Pointer's feet.

**冷周六**：这是海伦娜，她难得睡醒，正好让她跟你打个招呼。\
**Hissabeth**: This is Hélène. She woke up just a while ago. Hélène, meet Pointer.

**冷周六**：虽然没空自己去听讲座，但我想了个办法，拜托其他人把海伦娜放进口袋捎过去。刚抽空整理过笔记，给你。\
**Hissabeth**: We couldn't all attend the lecture, but I asked someone to take Hélène there to observe. Here are the notes.

**指针**：每次到这时候我都想感叹意识共享的便捷性！\
**Pointer**: I still haven't stopped being amazed by your siblings' telepathic connection.

**指针**：就没有什么效果相似的神秘术吗？真不敢想象它会让研究效率提升多少倍。\
**Pointer**: I wonder if there is an arcane skill that might approximate the same effect. Imagine how much faster we'd be able to share information with it.

**冷周六**：你会先被各种啰嗦的声音吵得睡不着啦。\
**Hissabeth**: It's got its advantages, if you're willing to accept eight different voices oscillating between a party and a brawl every day in your mind.

冷周六耸了耸肩膀，弯腰拾起完成任务的小蛇。\
Hissabeth shrugs and scoops up the little snake.

它用比其他兄弟姐妹更快的速度消失在那头蓝发之间。\
It shoots up her sleeve, vanishing into her blue hair to rejoin her siblings.

**冷周六**：别介意，她还是幼崽的时候就容易害羞。\
**Hissabeth**: Hope you don't mind. She's been a bit shy ever since we were little.

**指针**：早习惯了。笔记过两天还你，我想看看理线学知识是否能应用于航天材料外壳的受力计算。\
**Pointer**: That won't be a problem. I'll get it back to you in a few days. I just want to check if the study of ley lines can help with our aeroshell's force analysis.

**冷周六**：特地过来就为了这份笔记？留言给我也行的事，应该没那么着急吧。\
**Hissabeth**: Is that all? You could've left a message. No need to go out of your way.

**指针**：啊哈，我正找人和我分享物资申领单被搁置几个月毫无动静的“惊喜”。\
**Pointer**: Well, and I needed someone to unload a bit on. It's been months since I submitted our resupply application, and there doesn't appear to be any progress.

**指针**：我看他们不如把“无法直接应用于当下”的项目一锅端掉。\
**Pointer**: This slow starvation for all of us is a waste of effort. They should just cut the cord and scrap all these projects they feel "show no value in the short term."

**冷周六**：往好处想，至少这两间办公室我们实打实地用上了。\
**Hissabeth**: Look at the silver lining. We're sure to get our new offices.

**指针**：那是因为这地方的空房间实在够多。\
**Pointer**: Office space, the one thing we have in abundance here.

她烦躁地挥了挥胳膊，找回了平时的语气。\
She waves her arms in irritation before slipping back into her usual tone.

**指针**：先不管那些，你这边怎么样？我能抽空搭把手。\
**Pointer**: *sigh* Anyway, how are things on your side? I'm free for the moment.

**冷周六**：进度照常，符合预期。你瞧。\
**Hissabeth**: I'm progressing just fine. Take a look.

她走近那张办公桌，冷周六侧身让出道路，摊开桌上的设计稿。\
She steps closer to the desk. Hissabeth shifts some space and lays out the blueprints.

**指针**：那就好，遇见麻烦就随时找我。\
**Pointer**: Excellent. Feel free to let me know if you require any help.

**指针**：好像一直没有正式聊过——你为什么选了这个项目？\
**Pointer**: You know, for all the time we've worked together, there are still many questions left unanswered between us. I'm curious: why did you choose this project?

和刚见面时不同，这不是某种检验或质疑，只是真正出于关心的询问。\
The tenor of their conversation has changed since their first meeting. This isn't a test. It's genuine concern.

这段时间来的共事让她能够，也愿意发问。\
Time has built enough trust between them to ask.

**指针**：我知道也有几个小组在解决清扫术式和植物类神秘术的生活应用问题。大方向而言，他们做的也是“神秘术与科技的兼容”。\
**Pointer**: There are many other teams pursuing the "combination of arcanum and science." I think one of them is presently working on cleaning incantations and plant-related rituals.

**指针**：最后决定来偏远的普列谢茨克，只是因为你更熟悉空间材料学，更想为航天工程出力？\
**Pointer**: Why choose Plesetsk? Is it that you feel your expertise in material science will be of most benefit here? Or do you have a particular interest in the aerospace industry?

**指针**：当然，你做得很好，不然我们也没法这么快就申请到单间。\
**Pointer**: Don't mistake my intentions. I'm happy you chose to join our little team. You've performed exceptionally well so far.

**冷周六**：一定要找个理由的话……我也想知道旅行者号的金唱片会送到哪儿。\
**Hissabeth**: If I had to put a finger on it, I'd say it was curiosity. I really want to know where those Golden Records will end up.

她将设计稿卷了起来，腾开桌面，找到更适合聊天的舒适站姿。\
She rolls up the blueprint before settling into a relaxed posture.

**冷周六**：我提过父母的事，第一次“暴雨”发生前他们在拉普拉斯研究信息技术。\
**Hissabeth**: Remember what I told you about my parents? They were studying information technology at Laplace before the first "Storm" struck.

冷周六的思维时常会过于跳跃，但现在指针已经能跟上这种节奏。她耐心地等待着下文。\
Hissabeth's mind has always jumped around, but now Pointer can keep up. She knows to wait for the point to come back around.

**冷周六**：我不擅长那个，或者说我早就厌倦了处理太多信息，脑子里有人开会可够烦的。\
**Hissabeth**: I can't wrap my head around that stuff. My whole life has been a constant stream of information. You wouldn't believe how distracting it is to have eight voices in your brain, bothering you night and day.

**冷周六**：但网络依旧很有趣。我们九个都喜欢家里的电脑，九双眼睛同时读一篇文章，关注的内容会完全不同。\
**Hissabeth**: Still, all nine of us enjoyed reading. Whenever we found a particularly compelling article, we'd divide it up and each focus on a different part.

**冷周六**：看见，记住，就此展开激烈讨论。我们当时热衷于玩这种游戏，简直爱死它了。\
**Hissabeth**: We'd always have a huge brainstorm after we finished. It was a lot of fun actually. *sigh* I miss those times.

**冷周六**：我记得那篇关于流星的报道。\
**Hissabeth**: I still remember the day that meteor fell to Earth.

**电台节目**：“最新数据表明，旅行者一号已成为距离太阳最远的航天器……”\
**Radio**: "Our latest reports are that Voyager 1 has officially traveled the furthest through our solar system of any man-made spacecraft ..."

**电台节目**：“它以大约69.419个天文单位的距离，将先驱者十号抛在了身后……”\
**Radio**: "Surpassing Pioneer 10 by a distance of approximately 69.419 astronomical units ..."

**冷周六**：是电视还是收音机里？总之那个声音正说着旅行者探测器的消息。\
**Hissabeth**: I don't remember where I was or what I was doing, but I remember the broadcast was talking about the Voyager 1.

**冷周六**：而我们注视屏幕里发光的小点，所有视线都集中在它身上。\
**Hissabeth**: And that all nine of us were staring at the twinkling dot on the screen.

**小冷周六**：就连月亮离我们都有快四十万千米远，这颗流星到底是从多远的地方来的？\
**Little Hissabeth**: If the moon is almost 400,000 kilometers away from us, how much further away was this little rock from Earth when it started on its journey?

**小冷周六**：这真是不可思议——\
**Little Hissabeth**: Unbelievable ...

Невероятно？“不可思议的？”\
Невероятно？"Unbelievable"?

**冷周六**：在地球之外，在我们头顶闪烁的星星，它竟然也会来到地面的世界。\
**Hissabeth**: We never knew the stars above our heads could actually fall into our world.

**冷周六**：宇宙中在发生什么？我们没讨论出结果。\
**Hissabeth**: What was happening up there? For all our brainstorms, we never reached the solid conclusion.

**冷周六**：旅行者会到达哪儿，金唱片会送往哪里，群星会何时熄灭？\
**Hissabeth**: Where will Voyager 1 go? Who, if anyone, will find its Golden Records? When will the stars stop shining?

**冷周六**：某颗星球上有没有像你和我这样的研究员，在致力于弄清相似的问题？\
**Hissabeth**: Are there researchers out there just like us living on another planet, looking for the same answers?

**冷周六**：那颗流星带给我们很多疑问，而我喜欢刨根问底，得到答案。\
**Hissabeth**: One little meteor brought us so many questions, and we could never leave a stone unturned.

**指针**：所以你加入了这个缺少实际意义的项目。\
**Pointer**: I see. That's why you joined this project, despite its lack of immediate contributions to society.

**冷周六**：航天工程当然有它的意义。\
**Hissabeth**: Nonsense! Our work is critical to the future of aerospace engineering. We've got plenty of contributions to offer.

这回换她抬起手等待一次击掌。\
This time, she's the one holding up a hand, waiting for a high five.

**指针**：……怎么开始安慰我了？我可没对这份工作泄气。\
**Pointer**: Was that an attempt to cheer me up? There's no need. I'm not easily discouraged.

掌心贴着掌心，两只手短暂地重叠。\
Palm to palm, their hands meet for just a moment.

**指针**：你的体温没之前那么低了。\
**Pointer**: Hmm. You've warmed up a bit.

**冷周六**：这要得益于发射基地贴心的暖气供应，当然还有我对于能量摄入的重视。\
**Hissabeth**: Yeah, thanks to the 24/7 heating, and because I keep all of us well fed.

**冷周六**：说起来我昨天在镇上找到几家不错的餐馆，要不要去尝尝？\
**Hissabeth**: Speaking of, I'm headed to town to find a restaurant. Care to join me?

**冷周六**：多亏了新的福利政策，这里值得一吃的东西的确越来越多了。\
**Hissabeth**: There's some decent food in Plesetsk now, thanks to the new policies. Do you want anything in particular?

**指针**：听你的。\
**Pointer**: Your call.

当时我们都没有仔细想过，物资申领为何会这么艰难。\
Back then, we never thought to ask why our supply application had been put on ice for so long.

1987 5月 普列谢茨克发射基地\
May 1987, Plesetsk Cosmodrome

**冷周六**：——中止项目？！\
**Hissabeth**: They're terminating the project?!

过大的动静让小蛇们都探出头来，冷周六瞧上去像一朵炸开的向日葵。\
The noise startles the snakes. One by one, they poke their heads out to join the shock.

可惜这幅画面转瞬即逝，指针甚至来不及启动留影设备。\
Too bad the moment's already passed. Pointer doesn't even have time to snap a picture.

**拉普拉斯研究员**：完全能理解您的心情，女士。但您也应该清楚，“暴雨”过后，基金会和科算中心的首要任务是重建和恢复。\
**Laplace Researcher**: I understand, ma'am, but you should know that our top priority after each "Storm" is to restore the Foundation and the LSCC to full function as soon as possible.

**拉普拉斯研究员**：在资源和人手都相当紧缺的情况下，中止一些相对不那么紧急的研究项目，这是难免的。\
**Laplace Researcher**: With our current shortages of resources and manpower, that means cutting all non-essential projects.

**冷周六**：哪一部分能算是“紧急”？是谁在决定它们的重要性？\
**Hissabeth**: Non-essential? Then what is it that counts as "essential"? Who decided on our priority?!

在小蛇们再次发出愤怒的嘶嘶声之前，有人及时地拉住了冷周六。\
Before the snakes can hiss again in protest, Pointer reaches out and grabs Hissabeth.

**指针**：我们能做到现在还得感谢路德维希先生，他并没有立刻叫停普列谢茨克的大多数研究。\
**Pointer**: Calm down, Hissabeth. I understand that Mr. Ludwig did his best to keep as many projects running in Plesetsk as he could. We couldn't have stayed here this long if it weren't for him.

**指针**：但他也只是这个小小分部的管理者，能做的有限。\
**Pointer**: But he's only a branch leader. He doesn't get to make the top-level decisions.

**冷周六**：……所谓的“基础的”“有应用价值”的技术又不会凭空出现。\
**Hissabeth**: They act as if all of their essential and valuable consumer technology just popped up out of nowhere!

**冷周六**：航天工程没有用？随便说个简单的——他们吃泡面会没有蔬菜包！\
**Hissabeth**: To think that aerospace engineering has less to contribute than their other projects?! S**t! They wouldn't even have vegetable packets in their instant noodles without us!

**拉普拉斯研究员**：无论这个消息让您的心情多糟糕，女士，它就是既有事实。\
**Laplace Researcher**: I'm sorry, but our decision is final.

**拉普拉斯研究员**：您还是让我把通知说完吧，我还得去下一个研究室。\
**Laplace Researcher**: Please allow me to finish. As you can imagine, I have several other meetings lined up after this.

**指针**：好的，请您继续。\
**Pointer**: Sure. Please continue.

**拉普拉斯研究员**：露西女士并不完全赞同这个决定。她希望向普列谢茨克航天基地的研究员们确认一件事。\
**Laplace Researcher**: Madam Lucy has expressed that she is not in favor of this decision. To that end, she asked me to deliver a "lifeline" for your work here.

**拉普拉斯研究员**：对于“暴雨”，我们的了解还极其有限。如果能收集更多相关数据，能确认它的影响范围，就能更好地应对它。\
**Laplace Researcher**: As you know, our knowledge about the "Storm" remains extremely limited. Madam Lucy believes we could better manage our circumstances if we could observe it in greater detail, particularly its extent.

**拉普拉斯研究员**：——是否有人愿意尝试将监测器送往太空，回收“暴雨”落下时的宇宙数据？\
**Laplace Researcher**: She's seeking volunteers from Plesetsk for a project, one that aims to send a monitor into space in order to collect data as the "Storm" arrives.

**指针＆冷周六**：……！\
**Hissabeth & Pointer**: ...!

两种截然不同的反应。\
Two completely different reactions.

**冷周六**：那些项目被中止的研究员，他们要去哪里？\
**Hissabeth**: What about the other projects? Where will the researchers be assigned if their projects have all been terminated?

指针飞快地看了她一眼，试图给出提醒。但冷周六并没有注意到她在摇头。\
Pointer shoots her another look, trying to signal her. But Hissabeth either doesn't notice or doesn't care.

**拉普拉斯研究员**：等待调任通知，去支援其他小组。不过和航天应该没太大关系了。\
**Laplace Researcher**: Most will be reassigned to other teams. I'm afraid there isn't much manpower to spare on our work here.

**拉普拉斯研究员**：如果你不打算就这么离开，那只有接下任务。普列谢茨克剩下的研究资源都会留给你。\
**Laplace Researcher**: That's the deal. If you want to stay on this project, then this mission must become your full focus. On the bright side, you'll have full access to all the resources left in Plesetsk.

他转头确认过走廊上没有别人，紧接着凑近一步，压低了声音。\
He makes a quick glance down the hallway to check no one else is around, then steps closer and lowers his voice.

**拉普拉斯研究员**：我知道你们都打算整出点像样的东西，也一直是普列谢茨克最认真的那部分人……\
**Laplace Researcher**: I believe you two to be the most talented researchers in Plesetsk, and I know you want to achieve something with your work here.

**拉普拉斯研究员**：但这真的不是好差事。你想想，假如有谁成功了，大伙儿的确会敬佩他——然后呢？没这份敬佩也能活着嘛。\
**Laplace Researcher**: Still, I think I should caution you against accepting this task. Sure, if you pull this off, you'd become a legend throughout our organization, but there's only so much value in fame and admiration.

**冷周六**：如果失败呢？\
**Hissabeth**: And what would happen if we were to fail?

**拉普拉斯研究员**：我觉得最普通的结果是死。更坏点的结果就很难预料了。毕竟现在谁都不清楚“暴雨”的原理。\
**Laplace Researcher**: I'm afraid your best hope would be instant death, and it may be much worse than that. No one knows for certain what the "Storm" can do, after all.

**拉普拉斯研究员**：要押上性命不值得。\
**Laplace Researcher**: I'm not sure this is worth your lives.

看见有正提着行李的研究员从走廊另一侧走来，他再度拉开了距离。\
Noticing another researcher approaching from the far end of the hall with luggage in hand, he steps back, readopting his cool professional tone.

**拉普拉斯研究员**：那么我的通知就到这里。请确认相关事项，并在24小时内提交回复。\
**Laplace Researcher**: Alright, that's all. I just need you to confirm that you've been informed. You'll have 24 hours to respond to our request.

收下通知材料，指针和冷周六回到只有二人的研究室。\
After receiving the official documents, Pointer and Hissabeth return to their office.

在难捱的沉默中犹豫良久后，指针艰难开口。\
They say nothing for a long time. The weight of the decision before them deserves their silent consideration. Finishing her deliberations, Pointer clears the air.

**指针**：冷周六，我知道你一向认同露西女士的观点。但这次毕竟情况特殊，这也并不是专门指定给谁的强制要求。\
**Pointer**: Hissabeth, I know you're a big supporter of Madam Lucy, but I'm sure you agree this mission is a statistical death sentence.

**指针**：如果你觉得不好拒绝，我……\
**Pointer**: If you're struggling for a way to say no, I'll ...

这些字眼并没能顺利抵达研究员的耳朵。几秒钟后，她才疑惑地抬起头来。\
Her words don't seem to have any purchase on her fellow researcher. Hissabeth looks up at her with a puzzled expression.

**冷周六**：你说什么？——对了，跟你说个好消息。\
**Hissabeth**: Sorry, what? Never mind. I've got good news.

**冷周六**：我刚才联络了北方哨歌，她能为我们解决一个大问题。\
**Hissabeth**: I just talked to Windsong. She's got a solution to one of our major issues.

冷周六扬了扬手，回答的同时还不忘继续手头的工作。\
Hissabeth waves a hand as she answers, continuing her work.

**指针**：你……你不打算拒绝？\
**Pointer**: Wait. Don't tell me you want to volunteer?

**冷周六**：为什么？当然不！这可不是能轻易得到的机会。\
**Hissabeth**: Why shouldn't we? This is a once-in-a-lifetime opportunity.

**指针**：但你知道那会遇到多少困难，面对多大的风险。就像刚才说的……\
**Pointer**: But have you even considered the risk we'd be taking? Like the liaison said.

**冷周六**：我们有可用的设备，有正在进行中的研究，有共同确认过的目标。\
**Hissabeth**: We'll have all the equipment we need, with a project that's progressing smoothly, working towards an achievable goal for the common good.

**冷周六**：宇宙真的如此遥不可及吗？如果传送术式能派上用场——\
**Hissabeth**: It is almost like the universe is within our grasp. All we must do is make our teleport disk work.

**指针**：但我们没有合适的人选能安放监测器。你要上哪去找能在短期训练后适应失重、高压和高温环境的人？\
**Pointer**: It's not that simple. We'd still need an astronaut capable of launching the monitor. Who could we find that would be capable of acclimatizing to a zero-gravity environment under high heat and pressure in such a short time?

**冷周六**：我正要将好消息的详情分享给你，关于北方哨歌发现的理线学好苗子，一位空中飞人小姑娘。\
**Hissabeth**: That's the good news! Windsong already found us an ideal candidate—an acrobat.

冷周六终于完成了手头的工作——她将稿纸展示给指针，那是后续的工作计划表。\
Hissabeth finishes her task and holds out the sheet to Pointer: a follow-up work schedule.

**冷周六**：我列出了之后要解决的问题——当然，前提是我们接下露西女士的任务。\
**Hissabeth**: Here, I made a list of issues we'll need to tackle. Of course, that's only assuming you'll accept Madam Lucy's mission too.

**冷周六**：刚到普列谢茨克的时候，我们聊过关于航天探索的话题，你说也想知道宇宙里在发生什么。\
**Hissabeth**: I remember we talked about space exploration when I first arrived in Plesetsk. You said you wanted to know what's going on up there, too.

**冷周六**：为了那个答案，你愿意面对多大的风险？\
**Hissabeth**: So tell me, what price are you willing to pay for that answer?

**？？？**：深呼吸，找到那个平衡点。\
**???**: Breathe. Let the air find its balance within.

**？？？**：科兹洛夫先生说过，不用害怕风险。想象自己漂浮在宇宙中——\
**???**: Remember what Mr. Kozlov said: "You must never be afraid of falling." I just have to imagine myself floating in space.

**？？？**：——没错。我绝不会再从钢丝上跌落了。\
**???**: That's right. I will not fall from the wire again.

主持人的介绍、热烈的欢呼与掌声从耀眼的光线处传来。\
The circus barker's introduction booms above the blinding lights, followed by a wave of cheers and applause.

**马戏团员**：接下来登场的是我们乌特恩亚亚马戏团最年轻的空中飞人、钢丝上的舞者——\
**Circus Barker**: Ladies and gentlemen, introducing our fabulous wire dancer, the youngest acrobat of the Utrennyaya Circus—

**马戏团员**：——库珀花环！\
**Circus Barker**: Kiperina!

## CO-04 崭新的，美丽的 / Beautiful New Things

1987 6月 乌特恩亚亚马戏团\
June 1987, Utrennyaya Circus

库珀花环，乌特恩亚亚马戏团的空中飞人。\
Kiperina, Star Acrobat of the Utrennyaya Circus.

加入计划的原因……像平时一样，做我力所能及的事。\
Why did I join this project? Well, I guess I'm trying to help in any way I can, like I always do.

马戏团就像一个小小的宇宙。\
The circus is a lot like outer space.

我们在其中演出，塑造接近无重力的、充满想象的、不可捉摸的世界。\
It is a performance that exists within an almost weightless world of imagination. Close to reality but, at the same time, unreachable.

我非常喜欢团长描述的生活，也从没想象过它会结束。\
I've come to love the life that Mr. and Mrs. Kozlov provided for us there, and I never thought it might end.

**库珀花环**：我来了，团长。您有什么事？\
**Kiperina**: Here I am, Ringmaster. How can I help you?

科兹洛夫正擦拭着座椅上的一小撮烟灰，听到库珀花环的声音，他立刻抬起头来。\
Mr. Kozlov brushes a little ash off his seat, but when he hears Kiperina's voice, he bolts up immediately.

**科兹洛夫**：平时就不用叫我团长了。阿涅娅，你今天感觉怎么样？\
**Mr. Kozlov**: Oh, Alia. No need to be so formal outside of work. Anyways, how is it you are feeling today?

**科兹洛夫**：可别把一切想得太麻烦，你多休息休息，我们大伙儿也不会吃不起饭饿肚子。\
**Mr. Kozlov**: I don't want you to be overwhelmed. Take time for a little rest. Old Kozlov can manage things from here.

**库珀花环**：上次摔下钢丝只是非常罕见的意外，我完全可以保证！\
**Kiperina**: Please, it was just a thoughtless accident, and I won't let it happen again, I promise!

**库珀花环**：最近我都很有精神，很健康，娜塔莉亚女士她们也知道，您可以问问大家我是不是每天都活蹦乱跳。\
**Kiperina**: I've fully recovered. I know you're worried about me, but just ask anyone and you'll know I'm not lying. Even Mrs. Kozlov agreed.

**库珀花环**：您看，我甚至能给您来场小小的烟花表演。\
**Kiperina**: See. I can even put on my firework show again.

光点在伸出的指尖炸开，短暂地将周围映亮，如同白昼。\
Light bursts out from her outstretched fingertip, briefly illuminating the space like it's midday.

像一株进行光合作用的植物那样，捕捉光粒子，储存它们，释放它们。\
Like a plant drawing in sunlight, absorbing it, storing it, and then releasing it again.

美丽但缺乏作用的神秘术。\
A beautiful, if useless, arcane skill.

**科兹洛夫**：多漂亮！看来北方哨歌女士教你的神秘术技巧你都记得很牢。\
**Mr. Kozlov**: Oh! More beautiful than ever! It seems you've mastered the techniques that Ms. Windsong taught you.

**科兹洛夫**：我们的阿涅娅的确是理线学的好苗子！\
**Mr. Kozlov**: There's no doubt our Alia has a budding talent for these ley line things!

**库珀花环**：您又在提那件事了，我当时已经和那位女士好好说过，我暂时不打算离开马戏团。\
**Kiperina**: Please don't start that again. I already told Ms. Windsong that I had no plans to leave the circus.

**科兹洛夫**：我知道了，我知道了。喔，对了，有件事我要告诉你。\
**Mr. Kozlov**: I know, I know. Such a loyal star you are. Oh, but there's something I should tell you.

中年人清了清嗓子，想尽力以自然的方式带过这个略显突兀的话题。\
He clears his throat, trying to smooth over the sudden topic shift.

**科兹洛夫**：是这样，我们要去米尔内演出。\
听说那个镇子能看到极光，风景相当不错。\
**Mr. Kozlov**: Ahem, um, it's ... we're going to hold a show up near Mirny. They say the night sky is beautiful that far north. Perhaps you might even see the aurora.

**库珀花环**：突然去那么远的新地方？我们碰上了麻烦吗？\
**Kiperina**: All of a sudden? But it's so far from here. Are we in trouble?

**科兹洛夫**：都挺好的……不是麻烦，其实……\
**Mr. Kozlov**: No, everything's fine. I-It's just ...

科兹洛夫略显局促地搓着手，他实在不擅长拐着弯说话。\
Mr. Kozlov wrings his hands. Subtlety is not his strong suit.

**科兹洛夫**：其实——阿涅娅，北方哨歌女士联系了我，她的一位朋友想邀请你去米尔内。\
**Mr. Kozlov**: Actually, Alia, Ms. Windsong called me. A friend of hers would like to meet you in Mirny.

**科兹洛夫**：那位朋友是拉普拉斯的人……我打听过，他们在神秘学交易市场口碑非常好。\
**Mr. Kozlov**: They work for an organization called Laplace. I made inquiries at the arcane market. They have a good reputation.

**科兹洛夫**：还有人提到他们和圣洛夫基金会的关系，听说基金会正在从外面招揽神秘学家。\
**Mr. Kozlov**: Someone even told me that they were related to the St. Pavlov Foundation—that big organization that recruits all kinds of arcanists.

**科兹洛夫**：我的年纪可不行啦，但你还年轻。假如——万一你能加入拉普拉斯或者基金会，绝对比跟着马戏团东奔西跑要好得多——\
**Mr. Kozlov**: We are old, Alia, but you, your life has just begun. If you were to join Laplace or the Foundation, you'd live a much better life than any you could have in our little circus.

**库珀花环**：……您还是想把我送走，是不是？\
**Kiperina**: Do you want me to leave?

**科兹洛夫**：我们只是去看看。你可能要参加一些训练，但如果不开心，不想继续，可以退出。\
**Mr. Kozlov**: No. No, Alia. We just want to let you have another try. There may be some training involved, but we will not force you to stay. You can quit anytime you like.

**科兹洛夫**：我希望你能平安、开心地过日子。你摔下去那次，把我和娜塔莉亚都吓坏了，我实在不愿意——\
**Mr. Kozlov**: Natalya and I, we hope you will have a safe and happy life. After that last time when you fell from the wire, we-we just can't bear to—

**库珀花环**：……如果您希望我去，我会去的。科兹洛夫先生。\
**Kiperina**: Then I'll go, Mr. Kozlov, if that's what you want for me.

感知到眼前孩子话语里的妥协，中年人叹了口气，像往常一样用宽厚的手掌轻轻摸了摸她的脑袋。\
Sensing the compromise in the girl's words, the man sighs and pats her head with a broad, fatherly hand.

**科兹洛夫**：我们不是要赶你走，阿涅娅。这样稳定、安全、舒适的地方，不是什么时候都能遇到。你才十五岁，没有尝过从雪堆里刨土豆填肚子的滋味……\
**Mr. Kozlov**: We don't want you to leave, Alia. But this is an opportunity for you to live in comfort and safety. You're just 15. We don't want you to have to learn what it feels like to scrounge for food in the freezing wild.

他没继续说下去，那并不是美好的回忆，不需要讲给一个孩子。\
He leaves it there. Some memories aren't worth retelling—not to a child.

**科兹洛夫**：我们至少去试一试。你也随时可以回乌特恩亚亚，这里是你长大的地方，当然也永远是你的家。\
**Mr. Kozlov**: Let's just give it a try. What do you say? You will always be welcome to come back to the Utrennyaya when you want. We will never turn you away from your home.

**库珀花环**：我一直这么想。\
**Kiperina**: I've always known that.

她露出了一个微笑，但并不足以遮掩那份觉得自己无足轻重的失落。\
She smiles, but it's not enough to hide the quiet weight of her insecurity.

**科兹洛夫**：……北方哨歌女士给过你名片，你记得吗？\
**Mr. Kozlov**: Ms. Windsong gave you her card, remember?

**库珀花环**：那张名片早就不知道去哪里啦。我本来以为他们不会需要照明灯泡。\
**Kiperina**: I forgot where I put it. I figured they wouldn't ever find a need for a living light bulb.

**科兹洛夫**：阿涅娅——\
**Mr. Kozlov**: Alia ...

**库珀花环**：科兹洛夫先生，我们做好计划了吗？要带哪些东西去，什么时候动身？还有，从陆地走吗？\
**Kiperina**: So, then have you already planned the route, Mr. Kozlov? Are we traveling overland? When do we set off? And what are we taking with us?

**库珀花环**：那边的气候怎么样，需不需要另外添衣服？\
**Kiperina**: What's the weather like in Mirny? Should I pack some warmer clothes?

**库珀花环**：药箱里的药品也很久没补充了，我待会就去检查。您记得规划动物们的运输……\
**Kiperina**: Oh, it's been a while since the last time we restocked the medical kit. I'll check it later. We need to prepare for the animals' transportation.

**科兹洛夫**：好，我都记着。你这孩子，总是很有主意……\
**Mr. Kozlov**: Of course, of course, it's all in hand already. Our Alia, always such a self-starter.

科兹洛夫咕哝着转过身。比起抱怨，他的语气更多地呈现出一种自豪。\
Muttering, Mr. Kozlov turns away. It sounds more like pride than complaint.

**科兹洛夫**：拉普拉斯的先生女士们眼光可高着呢！说到底，还是我们的阿涅娅够出色，做什么都仔细得很……\
**Mr. Kozlov**: Laplace sets a very high standard for its staff! Our Alia could only have been chosen if she were very special. Just see how she pays attention to each little detail.

有主意的小姑娘等待着科兹洛夫的身影彻底消失。\
The clever girl waits until Mr. Kozlov has disappeared.

她很少撒谎，所以偶尔为之的谎言也几乎不会被揭穿。\
She rarely lies, so, on the rare occasion she needs to, no one ever suspects.

名片还在她这儿，被收在衣服的内袋里。\
The card's still with her, tucked in the inside pocket of her coat.

她说不清自己是否有一瞬间想要前往更远的、更辽阔的土地。\
She isn't sure yet whether she really wants to chase after a faraway, wider world.

**库珀花环**：北方哨歌。理线学学者。\
**Kiperina**: Windsong. Ley Lines Scholar.

**库珀花环**：还是不明白这门学科要学习什么，工程类？数学？根本打听不到相关的消息……\
**Kiperina**: I still don't get it. What even is "The Study of Ley Lines"? Is it like Arcanist Engineering? Or Math? I've never seen or heard of anything like it.

**库珀花环**：等见到了她，去学习理线学，我是不是就要离开乌特恩亚亚？\
**Kiperina**: If I start to study these ley lines, does that mean I'll have to leave Utrennyaya forever?

**库珀花环**：……科兹洛夫先生已经不需要我参加演出了吗？\
**Kiperina**: That I won't be with Mr. and Mrs. Kozlov and the circus anymore?

她无法立刻得知答案，只能选择先回房间睡个好觉。\
She's still waiting on an answer from her mind, her heart, somewhere. So for now, she'll go back to her room and sleep in it.

**库珀花环**：乌特恩亚亚的顶棚……是娜塔莉亚女士装饰的，她说那是宇宙的样子。\
**Kiperina**: Our circus's big top was decorated by Mrs. Kozlov. She said that she wanted it to reflect the beauty of the stars and the weightlessness of outer space.

**库珀花环**：我离开乌特恩亚亚之后，还能再见到这么好看的景色吗？\
**Kiperina**: Such a beautiful view. Will I ever be able to see it again if I leave here?

**库珀花环**：去见大家期望我见的人。然后一切都会变得更好……是这样吗？\
**Kiperina**: I suppose I must meet these Laplace people, if that is what my family wants me to do. This way, we'll all be able to live a better life, right?

她慢慢闭上眼睛，想象着许多光点从眼前丝绒幕布般的黑暗中浮现。\
She lets her eyes close, picturing tiny specks of light emerging from the velvet darkness behind her lids.

**库珀花环**：一颗……两颗……大熊座，小熊座……\
**Kiperina**: One star ... two stars ... Ursa Major—the Great Bear, and the Little Bear ...

**库珀花环**：米尔内……真奇怪，马戏团应该没去过那里，但我却能想象出那里的星空。\
**Kiperina**: Mirny ... I don't think we've ever been there before, but I feel like I already know what the stars look like from there. How strange.

**库珀花环**：那些遥远的星星，也会迷失、也会流浪吗？\
**Kiperina**: I wonder if the stars ever wander away from the sky. Will they all disappear one day?

**库珀花环**：它们做的梦……又是怎样的呢……\
**Kiperina**: What are their dreams like?

女孩渐渐沉入梦乡。在梦中，她带着一颗闪烁的星星，踏进了那座名为米尔内的小镇。\
She drifts off to sleep. Soon, she finds herself walking through Mirny, holding a sparkling star in her hand.

更北边的小镇，能见到极光的小镇。至少那应该是个美丽的地方。\
Mirny is a place in the far north where you can see the aurora. She hopes it's as beautiful as it is in her dream.

Красивая?“美丽的？”\
Красивая?"Beautiful"?

**米尔内驻军Ⅰ**：在那边！跟紧点，那到底是什么玩意？\
**Mirny Soldier I**: Over there! Keep up! What the hell is that?!

**？？？**：……\
**???**: ...

**米尔内驻军Ⅱ**：该死，是熊？这么灵活的熊？\
**Mirny Soldier II**: Damn, is that a bear? But it's so fast!

**米尔内驻军Ⅲ**：它到底从哪儿进来的？难道附近还有能穿墙的魔精？！\
**Mirny Soldier III**: How did it get in here? I've never heard of any kind of critter around here that can pass through walls like that!

**？？？**：……\
**???**: ...

**米尔内驻军Ⅱ**：我跟上了！就在这里！快——\
**Mirny Soldier II**: I caught it! Over here! Help, quickly!

追在身后的脚步彻底远去。\
The sound of her pursuers fades into the distance.

必须摆脱周围的黑暗，前往有光亮的地方。\
She must escape the darkness around her and move toward the light.

有光的地方，就有活物，有其他声音。\
Where there is light, there is life, and other voices.

**电台节目**：“旅行者二号的拍摄平台已顺利修复，将依照原定计划继续前进，以对天王星进行探测……”\
**Radio**: "Voyager 2 has successfully repaired its imaging platform and will proceed according to its originally scheduled exploration of Uranus ..."

**电台节目**：“旅行者一号仍在向太阳系外飞行，根据预测，大约七万年后，它会掠过半人马座比邻星……”\
**Radio**: "Voyager 1 continues its journey to the edge of the solar system and beyond. According to our projections, it is expected to pass by Proxima Centauri in around 70,000 years ..."

**库珀花环**：呃……\
**Kiperina**: Mmm.

从毯子里探出的手摸索一阵，终于成功按下了收音机的开关。\
A hand slips out from under the blanket, fumbling around until it finally finds the radio's switch.

**库珀花环**：又做了那种奇怪的梦。明明已经来到米尔内一段时间了，梦里的场景却越来越清晰了……\
**Kiperina**: The same strange dream again. It's gotten more and more detailed since we arrived in Mirny.

**库珀花环**：别总想着它，得想点儿其他的。团长和北方哨歌女士约定了一周后再见面，在此之前，我还是要认真准备好演出。\
**Kiperina**: I need something to distract myself. Ms. Windsong and Mr. Kozlov made an appointment to meet next week. Until then, I should continue to prepare for our show.

**库珀花环**：今晚就是乌特恩亚亚在米尔内的第一场马戏表演，在这个新地方……\
**Kiperina**: Utrennyaya is making its debut in Mirny tonight. It's a new beginning.

她稍稍探出脑袋，向帐篷外看去。\
She peeks her head out just a little, peering past the tent flap.

马戏团的帐篷对面是一家小餐馆，远远传来的喧闹令她安心。米尔内的街巷总回荡着士兵巡逻时整齐的脚步，这在别处也很少见。\
Across from their circus tent stands a small restaurant, and the distant sounds of conversation put her at ease. The streets of Mirny echo with the steady rhythm of patrolling boots.

尽管还没有见到大家所说的极光，但这些独特的体验足以叫她的心脏怦怦直跳。\
She hasn't seen the aurora yet, but even so, the novelty of it all makes her heart race.

**库珀花环**：呼……待会儿我得打起精神，好好表现。\
**Kiperina**: *deep breath* I just need to cheer up and do my best.

**库珀花环**：第一场表演，必须给每个观众都留下好印象。\
**Kiperina**: I guess it's also my debut in Mirny. And first impressions are everything.

**库珀花环**：也许我赢得足够多的喝彩声，科兹洛夫先生和娜塔莉亚女士就会改变主意……\
**Kiperina**: Maybe Mr. and Mrs. Kozlov will change their minds if I can win over the audience.

她踏出帐篷，准备迎接自己在米尔内的首次演出。\
She steps out of the tent, ready for her first performance in Mirny.

**马戏团员**：接下来登场的是我们乌特恩亚亚马戏团最年轻的空中飞人、钢丝上的舞者——\
**Circus Barker**: Ladies and gentlemen, introducing our fabulous wire dancer, the youngest acrobat of the Utrennyaya Circus—

**马戏团员**：——库珀花环！\
**Circus Barker**: Kiperina!

**？？？**：……！\
**???**: ...!

就在这里。\
Right here.

朝着光亮的地方前进，她见到许多发出声音的生物。\
Heading toward the light, she sees many creatures making noise.

所有声音似乎都指向她的头顶，为了瞧得更清楚，她努力地穿过人群，高高仰起头。\
The sounds seem to rise above her head. To see more clearly, she pushes through the crowd and looks up.

欢呼与呐喊，掌声与心跳。它们如同行星环绕着高空的身影。\
Cheers and shouts, applause and heartbeats—they circle the figure above like planetary rings.

在身影周围绽开了许多光点，其中一小部分令她感到熟悉。那些粒子诞生于她故乡的星云。\
Points of light burst around the figure's silhouette. A few of them feel familiar. These particles were born from the nebula of her home.

她观察四周，在这片喧哗中露出微笑。地球是多么热闹而美丽的地方啊。\
She looks around, smiling in the middle of the noise. Earth is such a lively and beautiful place.

吸气，在钢丝上腾跃，回身，抬手致意，吐气。\
Breathe deep. Leap onto the wire. Twist, raise a hand in salute, and then exhale.

观众的欢呼为这套动作打出十分。\
The audience erupts into applause—a perfect score for her routine.

**库珀花环**：——像这样做到完美，真的就能留下来吗？\
**Kiperina**: Will they let me stay if I keep giving perfect performances like this?

压在心底的疑惑伸出了触角。\
The doubts buried in her chest begin to stir.

钢丝上的库珀花环恍然回望，突然发觉现在无论往前、往后，都是空无一人。\
On the wire, Kiperina looks back, only to realize there's no one ahead of her nor behind.

——我该前进，还是后退？\
Should I move forward or back?

她下意识攥紧手掌，向着欢呼声投去视线。\
Instinctively, she clenches her fist and follows the cheers with her eyes.

从高空望下去，几乎不可能认得清哪张脸。\
From these heights, it's hard to recognize anyone.

就算是再熟悉的朋友，都会融入这片遥远的洪流。\
There are no friendly faces, no family. She's alone on the wire.

如无意外，本该如此。\
And that's how it's supposed to be.

**？？？**：……！\
**???**: ...!

就像那个梦境一样。一颗闪烁的星星为她指引了方向。\
Just like her dream. A flickering star points the way forward.

——别停留在这儿。前进，这也是大家所期望的。\
Don't stand still too long. They all want you to move on. They all want to see how far you'll go.

她稳了稳心神，再次迈步。\
She steadies herself to take another step.

向前走。\
Move forward.

演出结束，观众们都已离场。中年人边收拾着舞台的布景和道具，边向女孩传达自己的骄傲。\
The show is over, the audience gone. Mr. Kozlov packs away the stage props, his voice booming with pride.

**科兹洛夫**：刚才我和娜塔莉亚在后台还担心呢，但最后的效果完全超出我们的预料！\
**Mr. Kozlov**: Natalya and I were a little worried for you back there, but it seems our worrying was for nothing. The show was even better than we hoped.

**科兹洛夫**：你做得太好了，阿涅娅！这是近段时间以来观众反响最好的一次，来米尔内真是个正确的选择！\
**Mr. Kozlov**: You did such a good job, Alia. The audience was thrilled! I knew we came to the right place.

**科兹洛夫**：今晚可得让娜塔莉亚做顿丰盛的好好犒劳一下你。也庆祝我们的阿涅娅马上能和拉普拉斯的先生女士们共事了！\
**Mr. Kozlov**: I'll ask Natalya to prepare us a proper banquet tonight, something to reward our darling Alia and celebrate your new job at Laplace.

**库珀花环**：这还是说不准的事呢……不过我会努力的。\
**Kiperina**: We still don't know about that yet, but I'll try my best.

**科兹洛夫**：我知道的，你只要下定决心，什么都能做到！好了，好了，我得和娜塔莉亚好好商量一下今晚的菜谱……\
**Mr. Kozlov**: I know you can do anything once you make up your mind to do it. And now, I must go discuss tonight's food with Natalya.

中年人拿着道具絮絮叨叨地走远了。库珀花环环顾四周，发觉这里只剩下了两个小小的身影。\
He walks off, still rambling, with the props in hand. Kiperina looks around. The massive tent now holds just two small figures.

一个是她，另一个是刚才的女孩。\
One is her, and the other is the girl from before.

**库珀花环**：……\
**Kiperina**: ...

女孩似乎还沉浸于演出中。她仰望着舞台，眼神和库珀花环在高空中捕捉到的一样明亮。\
The girl seems lost in the performance. She stares up at the stage, her eyes just as bright as the star that guided her to the other side of the rope.

**库珀花环**：或许她只是想多休息一下？或者，她在等人……\
**Kiperina**: Perhaps she's taking a break? Or waiting for someone.

乌特恩亚亚从不拒绝观众的停留，库珀花环也不擅长和陌生人打交道。\
She knows that Utrennyaya never turns away lingering audience members, but talking to new people has never been her strength.

但刚才的演出让她觉得，虽然还不明白之后会如何，但有时尝试向前一步也不错。\
Still, the show reminded her—sometimes it's worth taking that step forward, even if you don't know what comes next.

她不再犹豫，向着女孩走去。\
She doesn't hesitate this time.

**库珀花环**：……您好？\
**Kiperina**: ... Hello?

## CO-05 时间简谱 / A Score of Time

**电台节目**：“我们认为，旅行者一号也许将永远在银河系漫游……”\
**Radio**: "We believe Voyager 1 will continue to explore the galaxy on and on ..."

**电台节目**：“它将带着人类探索的证明前往星空深处，很可能会比地球上的生灵存在得更为长久……”\
**Radio**: "Traveling into the depths of the universe, carrying with it humanity's spirit of exploration, it is likely to persist longer than life on Earth ..."

收音机的播报总能吸引这位新朋友的注意力，她这几天都花上相当多的时间研究这个小方盒子。\
The radio catches her new friend's attention in an odd way. She's spent the past few days fascinated with the little musical box.

直到有其他声音盖过播报声。\
Until another voice cuts through the broadcast.

**库珀花环**：明天天气怎么样？如果是晴天，去散步的时候就能走得稍微远一些。\
**Kiperina**: What will the weather be like tomorrow? Maybe we can take a longer walk if it's sunny.

**库珀花环**：你还没有见过米尔内的钻石矿对不对？\
**Kiperina**: You haven't seen the diamond mine here in Mirny, have you?

女孩儿摇了摇头，把收音机放到旁边，等待库珀花环的下一句话。\
The girl shakes her head, sets the radio aside, and waits for Kiperina to speak.

为了更好地继续这场对话，库珀花环蹲下身。现在她们的视线平齐了。\
Kiperina kneels down. Now, they're eye to eye.

**库珀花环**：你回忆起什么了吗？我试着打听你的家，但大家都说对你没有印象。\
**Kiperina**: Is anything coming back to you? I asked some people around about you, but no one had any clue.

**库珀花环**：不过别担心，我们大多数人都是科兹洛夫团长收养的孩子。就算你继续在这里停留，他也不会介意的。他从不拒绝真正需要帮助的人。\
**Kiperina**: Don't worry. Most of us in the circus were adopted by Mr. Kozlov, so he won't mind if you stay with us. He always gives a hand to those in need.

**库珀花环**：而且，我明天会去和一位很厉害的女士碰面。她见识很广，也许她听说过你。\
**Kiperina**: And I'm going to meet an extraordinary lady tomorrow. She knows a lot. Maybe she will know who you are.

**？？？**：……\
**???**: ...

库珀花环惯于处理这样的茫然，她还记得那些无法回家的孩子刚来到马戏团时，是怎样在她和娜塔莉亚女士的安抚下露出笑容的。\
Kiperina is used to this kind of blank stare. She's seen it on the faces of children that were lost while they were at the circus—how Mrs. Kozlov had comforted them, and kept them entertained until the smiles returned to their faces.

她站起身子，往后退开一两步，向眼前的女孩儿伸出手。\
She stands up, steps back, and reaches her hand toward the girl.

**库珀花环**：对了——你瞧。\
**Kiperina**: Hey, look at this.

指尖绽开的小小光亮为房间增添了一缕暖色。\
A soft glow blooms at her fingertip, warming the tent with its light.

**库珀花环**：这是我的神秘术，虽然派不上什么用场，但是不是还挺漂亮的？\
**Kiperina**: It's my arcane skill. It's not very useful, I know, but don't you think it's pretty?

**库珀花环**：他们都说像星星一样。\
**Kiperina**: People say it looks like the stars.

**？？？**：……嗯。\
**???**: ... Mhm.

细微的亮光让女孩儿露出笑意，她看上去放松了许多。\
The tiny light served its purpose. She seems far more at ease now.

**库珀花环**：如果你喜欢，我还可以再给你表演这个。\
**Kiperina**: I could do it again if you like.

**库珀花环**：我们再试试——你能不能拼出自己的名字？\
**Kiperina**: Let's try something. Can you spell your name?

女孩儿打量着被推到眼前的积木块。她不知道如何写出这颗星球上的文字，于是无从分享自己的故乡与名姓。\
The girl eyes the colorful, crooked row of blocks placed in front of her. She doesn't know anything about the writing of this planet, so there's no way to share her name or where she's from.

这些生物需要一个称呼来达成交流。她明白了。\
But this creature wants a name to communicate with her. She understands that much.

积木块组成了一条歪歪扭扭、颜色缤纷的轨迹。\
The blocks form a messy, colorful path. A logic forms in her mind.

库珀花环尝试着将自己认识的词汇从这片彩色中打捞起来。\
Kiperina searches for something familiar among the colors.

**库珀花环**：……航行……者？\
**Kiperina**: Long journey ... traveler?

**库珀花环**：总觉得这是你刚从收音机里挑的词……\
**Kiperina**: *sigh* Sounds like you just picked these words up from the radio.

**？？？**：……\
**???**: ...

**库珀花环**：你也像它们一样走过很长的路，才来到米尔内吗？\
**Kiperina**: Did you go on a long journey to reach Mirny?

**库珀花环**：唔……我想想，科兹洛夫先生是怎么给我们起演出用的名称来着？\
**Kiperina**: Hmm. How was it that Mr. Kozlov decided on our stage names? Give me a second.

**库珀花环**：“漫长的旅程”和“旅行”，合并起来——\
**Kiperina**: "Long journey," we could call that a "voyage." That would make you, who traveled a long journey, a ...

**库珀花环**：——“远旅”。\
**Kiperina**: Voyager.

库珀花环伸出手，比划出她想象中旅行者号的飞行轨迹。\
Kiperina stretches out her hand and traces the imagined path of the Voyager probe.

女孩儿思索了片刻，然后也学着伸出手。\
The girl watches for a moment, then imitates the gesture.

**远旅**：……库珀花环。\
**Voyager**: Kiperina.

手指调转方向，她指了指自己。\
She twists her finger and points to herself.

**远旅**：远旅。\
**Voyager**: Voyager.

**库珀花环**：你有了一个“乌特恩亚亚”风格的名字，现在你也是马戏团的一员啦。\
**Kiperina**: Now that you have a stage name, you are now an official member of the Utrennyaya Circus.

**库珀花环**：……咦？\
**Kiperina**: Hmm?

远旅忽然转头望向帐篷门口，没过几秒，脚步声和亲切的呼唤声一同响起。\
Voyager spins herself toward the tent's entrance. A moment later, footsteps and a familiar, friendly voice arrive together.

**娜塔莉亚**：阿涅娅，你带过来的小姑娘呢？我见她总盯着动物笼子看，就从里头给她捉了只兔崽。\
**Natalya Kozlov**: Alia, where's that girl? The one who was staring at the animals before? I brought a bunny around for her.

**娜塔莉亚**：科兹洛夫让我来照顾她，你明天还得和拉普拉斯的先生女士们见面，是不是？\
**Natalya Kozlov**: I suppose I'll be looking after her now, because you're meeting those Laplace people tomorrow, right?

**娜塔莉亚**：你得好好休息。就听我的，去镇上吃一顿，早点儿睡。\
**Natalya Kozlov**: You need a rest, Alia. Now do as Mama Kozlov says: go have a nice meal at the restaurant in town and then straight to bed early.

**库珀花环**：娜塔莉亚女士！我不需要——\
**Kiperina**: Mrs. Kozlov, I don't need to ...

**娜塔莉亚**：好啦，今晚我可没煮你那份炖菜。快去吧，科兹洛夫都给餐馆付过钱了。\
**Natalya Kozlov**: Hush, just go. I didn't cook anything for you tonight. We've already paid the restaurant.

远旅在门和自己的朋友之间来回瞧了几次，最终还是选择了那只毛绒绒的兔子。\
Voyager's head twists, unsure of where to look between the door and her new friend, but in the end, she chooses the fuzzy rabbit.

帐篷里重归安静，只剩下满脸无奈的库珀花环。\
The tent falls quiet again, leaving Kiperina alone, looking helpless.

**库珀花环**：……\
**Kiperina**: ...

**库珀花环**：我早就不是需要被过度关心的小孩子了……\
**Kiperina**: I'm not just a little kid that you need to take care of.

**库珀花环**：好吧，去餐馆，然后回来多做一个小时训练。\
**Kiperina**: Fine. I'll go, and after that, I will train for another hour.

**库珀花环**：对……就这么办。\
**Kiperina**: Yes, that's for the best.

**冷周六**：就这么办，老板。\
**Hissabeth**: That's all. Thanks.

研究员合上菜单，把它推往柜台对面。\
She closes the menu and slides it across the counter.

**冷周六**：不好意思，我点完了。继续说说？你在米尔内捡到了一位小朋友，然后呢？\
**Hissabeth**: Sorry, it sometimes takes us a while to decide on an order. So, you were saying you found a strange girl here in Mirny, and then?

**冷周六**：你手上的仪器很别致，这是北方哨歌留下的？\
**Hissabeth**: Hold on! That special device you're holding. Did you get it from Windsong?

**库珀花环**：是的。来米尔内之前，我不小心在一场表演中摔下了钢丝，那时北方哨歌女士恰好在现场。\
**Kiperina**: Yes. Before I came to Mirny, I fell from the wire during a show, and Ms. Windsong happened to be there.

**库珀花环**：虽然记不清具体细节，但北方哨歌女士说，是我的神秘术保护了我不摔伤。\
**Kiperina**: I don't remember the details, but she said my arcane skill was able to protect me.

**库珀花环**：她帮助我收起了身体周围的光幕，还试着分析了神秘术的原理。虽然我最后仍然没听懂。\
**Kiperina**: She helped me draw out the aura from around my body and analyzed how it worked. Though I didn't understand that part at all.

**库珀花环**：但我记住了她用的方法，理线学。她借给我的测量仪也的确让我更容易控制自己的神秘术。\
**Kiperina**: But the name of her theory is still clear in my mind—The Study of Ley Lines. She gave me this device before she left. She said it would make it easier to control my arcane skill.

**库珀花环**：再加上，团长也希望我能答应邀请……所以我决定明天还是去和她见一面。\
**Kiperina**: Mr. Kozlov wants me to give it a try again, so I've decided to go see her tomorrow.

**冷周六**：挺好，她是个很不错的学者。虽然理线学基本上是纯理论内容，但实践研究也离不开理论支持。\
**Hissabeth**: Cool. She's a great researcher. The Study of Ley Lines is still highly theoretical, but as we say at Laplace, theory often lays the foundation for practice.

**冷周六**：你要是真打算加入拉普拉斯，我也能给你写推荐信。\
**Hissabeth**: If you do decide to join us, I'd be happy to write a reference letter for you.

**库珀花环**：您也是拉普拉斯的研究员？\
**Kiperina**: You're a Laplace researcher?

**冷周六**：我看起来不像？奇怪，那群家伙总说我打扮得很符合他们的刻板印象，怪胎科学家之类的。\
**Hissabeth**: You didn't already guess? Hmm. My colleagues often say I dress, you know, like a mad scientist.

**库珀花环**：不，我还以为你们不会来吃这种普通的路边餐馆……\
**Kiperina**: I guess it's that I never thought I would meet a scientist eating at a little restaurant like this.

**冷周六**：拜托啦，搞研究的也是活物，得吃饭睡觉——\
**Hissabeth**: Oh, please, I'm sure you're aware that scientists are living things too. We need to eat just like everyone else.

几条小蛇从冷周六的头发里探出身子，跟着她的笑声点了点头。\
A few little snakes poke out of Hissabeth's hair, nodding along with her laughter.

其中一条仰着头，让库珀花环抚摸它的脑袋，鳞片的触感光滑且冰冷。\
One tilts its head up, letting Kiperina stroke it. Its scales feel smooth and cold.

**冷周六**：你真的不怕他们。\
**Hissabeth**: Looks like you meant it when you said you're good with animals.

**库珀花环**：我和动物们相处的时间久着呢。马戏团里有一只我自己养大的小熊。\
**Kiperina**: I spend a lot of time with them in the circus. I even helped raise one of our bear cubs.

库珀花环走进店里不久，这位研究员就也进了门，径直坐在她旁边。\
Kiperina hadn't been in the restaurant long before Hissabeth walked in and sat right beside her.

一条小蛇率先好奇地打量起库珀花环，她也友善地和这条小蛇打了个招呼。\
One of the snakes takes the lead in inspecting Kiperina, who greets it kindly in return.

借着这份契机，她们很快找到了共同话题。\
That's all it takes for the two to find common ground.

**冷周六**：回到我最开始的疑问，你为什么要坚持做空中飞人？\
**Hissabeth**: You know you haven't answered my question yet. Why do you choose to be an acrobat?

**冷周六**：在高空靠一根这么细的线行走，你不会害怕？还是说你觉得干这行很酷？\
**Hissabeth**: Don't you find it scary to walk on a wire all the way up in the air? I suppose it is a really cool job, though.

**库珀花环**：嗯……我承认这是很酷。但我喜欢的其实是从空中往下望，那是平时无法体会的视角。\
**Kiperina**: Well, it is cool, I have to admit. But what I really like about being up on the wire is that, when you look down, you get to see a view that no one else gets to in their daily life.

**库珀花环**：所有人看起来都一样。就像我在宇宙里，和无数相似的星星一同漂浮。\
**Kiperina**: When I stand on the wire, the audience below look just like stars, and it feels like I'm floating in space with them.

**库珀花环**：那不是很棒吗？不用担心是否能派上用场，只是维持住自己的光就好。\
**Kiperina**: Isn't that great? In that moment, I stop worrying about my performance and forget all expectations. I can just be in the moment, shining like a star.

**冷周六**：噢……的确。真有意思，我之所以跑到这个荒凉的鬼地方，就因为也有类似的念头。\
**Hissabeth**: Oh, intriguing. You know, in a way, I came all the way out here because I had the same thought.

**冷周六**：我要和最聪明的大脑们在一块儿，那些闪耀的、人类和神秘学家的群星。\
**Hissabeth**: I wanna work with the smartest minds in the world, whether humans or arcanists. They're also like the stars in a lot of ways, each one bound to go down in history.

**冷周六**：我也想弄清楚头顶这个罩子外头有些什么玩意。\
**Hissabeth**: And I'm trying to find out what really exists beyond the limits of the sky.

**库珀花环**：你的兄弟姐妹也这么想？这些小蛇们……啊，它们睡着了。\
**Kiperina**: Do all your siblings share the same feeling? They're such neat little snakes. Oh, it looks like they have fallen asleep.

**冷周六**：我们从未改变想法。\
**Hissabeth**: We've always been on the same page when it comes to these things.

研究员转过头，库珀花环注意到她的瞳孔收成一条细线。\
Hissabeth turns her head. Kiperina notices her pupils narrowing to a slit.

**冷周六**：你的神秘术和我预想中差不多。\
**Hissabeth**: Your arcane skill is exactly as I expected.

**冷周六**：储存光，捕捉高能带电粒子，极光……原理类似于等离子防护罩……\
**Hissabeth**: It captures photons from the aurora and stores them as latent energy; then, when it's deployed, it appears to form a kind of prismatic plasma barrier.

**库珀花环**：什么？\
**Kiperina**: Wh-What?

**冷周六**：有空我会给你解释那些理论。太复杂了，一时半会讲不明白。\
**Hissabeth**: I'll explain next time. It's complicated. It could take hours to get it into your head.

**冷周六**：好了，我大概清楚了。这里有一个适合你的机会，你要不要试着够到它？\
**Hissabeth**: Still, it is most obvious to me that you are exactly the person we want for this opportunity. What do you say? Will you give it a try?

**库珀花环**：……？\
**Kiperina**: ...?

**冷周六**：一个真正前往宇宙中的机会。\
**Hissabeth**: An opportunity to reach the stars.

**库珀花环**：——！\
**Kiperina**: ...!

**库珀花环**：您——您是北方哨歌女士的那位同事？邀请我来米尔内的人？\
**Kiperina**: You mean you're the colleague Ms. Windsong mentioned? The one who invited me to Mirny?

**库珀花环**：我应该早点意识到……这是您设计的测验？可是，我刚才真的把您当做一位聊得来的……朋友……\
**Kiperina**: I should've known. Was this a test? I thought you were a friend I could talk to.

**冷周六**：那就太好了，你能觉得我算“朋友”，这可是我近几个月听过最好的夸奖。\
**Hissabeth**: A "friend"? Superbe, that's the best compliment I've received in months.

**冷周六**：谁会费尽心思设计这种测验？只是碰巧我俩都有不错的用餐品味而已。\
**Hissabeth**: Relax, this wasn't a test at all. We just happen to share the same taste in food.

**冷周六**：不过，为了这个奇迹般的巧合，你也该认真考虑一下邀请。\
**Hissabeth**: But I do hope you'll consider our offer seriously, in the spirit of the good time we had together.

**库珀花环**：去宇宙里？您想要让我试着做一位……宇航员……？\
**Kiperina**: Are you serious though? You really mean you want me to become an astronaut?

这份邀请听起来过于遥远，即使在最不切实际的梦境里，她也没有想过。\
The invitation seems too far-fetched. Even in her wildest dreams, she could never have imagined it.

**冷周六**：是的。\
**Hissabeth**: Exactly.

但冷周六的确认非常郑重。与此前闲聊时的态度截然不同。\
But Hissabeth's response carries a rare weight, different from her usual casual tone.

**冷周六**：你仍然可以明天再答复。\
**Hissabeth**: Don't rush to a decision. We can wait till tomorrow.

**冷周六**：算着时间，我正等的那批材料也该在明天送到。或许那位送货的职员还能顺路给你捎点小礼物。\
**Hissabeth**: In fact, the materials I've been expecting should arrive tomorrow as well. Maybe the delivery guy will bring you a small gift along the way.

**库珀花环**：不用这么麻烦的，我也没有给大家准备什么东西……\
**Kiperina**: You don't have to. Sorry, I didn't prepare any gifts.

**冷周六**：别紧张，你们的家乡都在这片土地上，应该能好好相处。而且他的名字和你一样有趣，怎么说来着……对了。\
**Hissabeth**: Don't be silly. It's just a friendly gesture. I believe you come from the same region, so I'll bet you two will get along quite famously. And he has an interesting nickname too. It was, umm, oh, right—

“命名日”。\
Name Day.

## CO-06 比旅程更险恶的 / What's Worse than the Journey

骨头船舶、精巧的彩蛋、生锈的零件与边角泛黄的稿纸。\
Ship models made of bone, delicate painted eggs, rusted parts, and yellowed scraps of draft paper.

众多陈旧物件被陈列在一块儿，出乎意料地达成了某种和谐。\
Old pieces hastily thrown together somehow form an unexpected harmony.

**命名日**：136号，来自……科雷马山地。\
**Name Day**: No. 136, from near the Kolyma Mountains.

**命名日**：讲述了“极地之星”的传说……某种突然发作的集体癔症。科拉半岛也有过类似记载。\
**Name Day**: Tells the tale of the Polar Star icebreaker. The crew suffered some kind of mass hysteria. The same thing happened later in the Kola Peninsula.

基金会职员为这份笔记贴好标签，写上编号，最后仔细地收进抽屉。\
He labels the notebook, writes down its number, and stores it away.

**命名日**：这次的目的地离北极圈很近，运气好的话也能看到极光吧？\
**Name Day**: Our destination is close to the Arctic Circle. With any luck, we should get a great view of the aurora.

1987 6月 基金会远东分部\
June 1987, Far East Branch of St. Pavlov Foundation

命名日，基金会调查员。目前供职于远东分部。\
Name Day, Investigator for St. Pavlov Foundation. Currently serving for Far East Branch.

加入计划的原因……这可是工作。\
Why did I join this project? Well, it is a job, and I like to do as I am told.

**命名日**：涅瓦河，斯维里河，然后到奥涅加湖……走水路还挺快的，兴许还来得及捎点小礼物。\
**Name Day**: Neva River, Lake Ladoga, Svir River, then Lake Onega ... It takes less time to travel by water. Maybe I can even buy a small gift along the way.

**命名日**：米尔内除了钻石矿还有别的特产吗？噢，说不定回程可以顺路去彼得罗扎沃茨克。\
**Name Day**: What sort of specialties does Mirny have other than diamonds? Oh, maybe I can stop by Petrozavodsk on my way back.

年轻人尝试着从地图上寻找出一条合适的线路。\
He examines the map, plotting out a workable route.

**命名日**：剩下的一点路得靠腿走了。普列谢茨克，那地方最多的就是雪地，除了雪什么也没有。\
**Name Day**: Looks like I'll have to walk the rest of the way after landing. Ah, Plesetsk, a place of boundless snow and not much else.

好在他很熟悉该如何穿越整片茫茫白色。\
Fortunately, endless white fields of snow are something with which he has a wealth of experience.

在极北之地追逐星星？把监测器送到星空中监测“暴雨”？听起来倒很不错。\
Trying to reach the stars in order to monitor the "Storm" from space, huh? Sounds like a good gig, even if it does mean being stationed at the northernmost frozen tip of the world.

或许只是他们众多研究里又一个徒劳的尝试。不过有人试试也挺好。\
Maybe it will go nowhere, but what would we be without a little pioneering spirit?

在传说中，流星可以象征厄运将至，也可以预示即将到来的幸运。\
In legends, a meteor may signal incoming disasters or foreshadow good fortune.

就像“永恒的灵魂”一样，这全都取决于看到它的人愿意相信哪种解释。\
Like the "eternal soul," it all depends on what the viewer chooses to believe.

Вечный?“永恒的？”\
Вечный?"Eternal"?

**小命名日**：穿过这片雪地，对面就是……列宁格勒……\
**Little Name Day**: Leningrad is just on the other side of this snowfield.

**小命名日**：希望这颗星星会带来好运。\
**Little Name Day**: I'll let that meteor guide my way.

最后他的确抵达了列宁格勒。\
In the end, he made it to Leningrad.

**命名日**：好吧，基金会的活儿总有这么多，很难说这是好运还是厄运……\
**Name Day**: The Foundation never gives me a break, which I guess makes me equal parts lucky and unlucky.

**？？？**：命名日先生？\
**???**: Mr. Name Day?

**命名日**：噢，我在——稍等！\
**Name Day**: Yep. Hold on!

门扉敞开后，教师的脚边不出意料地跟着一团雪白的毛绒。\
As the door opens, a bundle of energetic fluff appears, orbiting at his teacher's feet as expected.

**维拉**：我听说你们今天就要出发执行新任务，要往更北边走，对吗？\
**Vila**: I heard you were leaving for the north on a new mission. Is that true?

**命名日**：只是个送东西的活儿，分部人手还是不太够，我一个人去。\
**Name Day**: Just for an errand. The Far East Branch is short on staff right now, so I'm going all on my own.

**命名日**：北方哨歌女士应该正在那儿做实地考察。有没有什么需要捎带的东西？\
**Name Day**: Ms. Windsong should be on a field trip there. Is there anything you'd like me to give her?

**阿夫西维**：是比来亚什基更北的地方吗？维拉和我能去那儿吗？\
**Avgust**: Where is it? Is it north of Rayashki? Could I come visit there with Vila?

孩子的话语总是更为直接，熟悉的地名引发了一两秒沉默。\
Children speak more directly, but the mention of a familiar place brings a few seconds of silence.

**命名日**：这个……如果你好好完成课程，维拉女士也有足够的时间，你可以去任何安全的地方……\
**Name Day**: Well, so long as you finish all your classes and get good grades, I'm certain you'll be able to go anywhere with Ms. Vila, as long as it is safe.

**命名日**：但我没法保证未来的事儿。所以——阿夫西维同学，你有什么想要带去的东西，或者想要收到的礼物吗？\
**Name Day**: But things could change. I can't promise anything. Except maybe a little souvenir when I get back. Now, Avgust, do you have anything you want me to give Ms. Windsong?

**阿夫西维**：我有，维拉也有。我写了很多字，没有人讲睡前故事的时候，北方哨歌可以读它们。\
**Avgust**: Yes, and Vila does too. I've written lots and lots of things. Comrade Windsong can read them when no one is there to tell her a bedtime story.

**阿夫西维**：还有这个，来自长得最高、站得最直的一群向日葵哨兵！\
**Avgust**: And this, from my tallest and most spirited sunflower guards!

小男孩费力地摸索着外套口袋，找到了他珍贵的收藏。\
He fumbles through his coat pocket and pulls out his most prized possession.

**阿夫西维**：不用给它们浇太多水，要晒太阳。\
**Avgust**: You must not water them too much, and they should be placed somewhere under the sun.

一只手轻轻交出了信封，将它搭在种子旁边。\
Vila passes an envelope over, placing it next to the seeds.

**维拉**：我的确想拜托您为北方哨歌同志带一封信。\
**Vila**: I'd like this to be delivered to Ms. Windsong.

**维拉**：上次她在来信中提到，自己也尝试着当了回老师，发现教孩子们真是件不简单的事。\
**Vila**: She said in the last letter that she had started to teach again, and it was more difficult than she remembered.

**维拉**：我在信里写了些简单的教学经验，希望能帮上她。\
**Vila**: I wrote a little bit about my own experience teaching. Hope it helps.

**维拉**：如果您有什么好办法，也可以和她聊聊。尼娜、彼得森、帕索诺……都会时不时问起您，想知道您还会不会来和他们玩耍。\
**Vila**: And please talk to her if you have any ideas. You're so good with kids. Nina, Pyotr, and Pasono ask about you all the time, always wondering when you'll visit again.

**阿夫西维**：我没有问，我知道浣熊先生很忙。维拉也很忙，维拉每天都在涂涂画画，和白色衣服们说话……\
**Avgust**: I didn't ask. I know how busy you are, Mr. Raccoon, and so is Vila. Every day, she's either painting something or talking to the white clothes.

**命名日**：运气好的话，这趟任务结束我就能闲一阵子。我会来找你们玩，给你们变小玩意儿，怎么样？\
**Name Day**: With any luck, I'll be free for a while after this mission. I'll come back and do some magic for you kids. What do you say?

年轻人蹲下身，朝那朵摇晃的向日葵伸出手指，勾了勾它的叶片。\
He crouches and hooks his finger around the leaf of the wobbling sunflower.

**命名日**：说好了？\
**Name Day**: Deal?

**阿夫西维**：一位真正的好同志从来都不违反约定！\
**Avgust**: A good comrade must always keep his word!

毛绒绒的帽子上下摇晃了两次，看得出孩子正严肃、用力地点头。\
The fuzzy hat bobs up and down twice—an earnest and sincere nod.

话题重新回到两位成年人之间。\
The conversation shifts back to the two adults.

**命名日**：听上去您最近的工作还挺顺利？基金会的课本不算复杂，但我想备课也得花不少工夫……\
**Name Day**: Sounds like you've been doing well recently. The Foundation's textbook is an easy read, but I really hadn't expected just how effortlessly you'd be able to make your lesson plans.

**维拉**：总不会比外勤任务更麻烦。不过您应该记得现在的任务要求——安全为先。\
**Vila**: Lesson plans are nothing compared to field missions. Just keep this in mind during your errand: your safety is our first priority here.

**命名日**：当然。而且外头现在恰好是个还算熟悉的时代……\
**Name Day**: Of course, but the good news is I'm quite familiar with this era.

在这时代里，这座城市还没有改回“圣彼得堡”的旧名。\
Though in this era, the city hasn't yet reverted to its old name—Saint Petersburg.

但涉足类似的话题，就难免也会提及那座消失在雪中的小镇。\
Talk like this always seems to circle back to that little town swallowed in snow.

现在还不是合适的时机。\
But now's not the time for that.

**命名日**：……总之，信和种子我一定会带到北方哨歌女士手里。\
**Name Day**: Um, anyway, I'll make sure Ms. Windsong receives Avgust's seeds and your letter.

**维拉**：非常感谢。虽然有些啰嗦，但您独自执行任务，还是多加小心。\
**Vila**: Thanks a lot. I don't want to make our goodbyes here too long-winded. Just take care, especially since you're going to be all on your own.

**命名日**：其实准确来说，也不算真的只有我“一个人”……\
**Name Day**: Well, I won't exactly be "all on my own."

**含章鼎**：还有多远？我觉得我们马上就到了，我简直已经看到拉普拉斯建筑那种特别的金属房顶了！\
