**Han Zhang**: Hey, so, any idea how far off this place is? I think we must be pretty close. I can almost see that unmistakable Laplace metal roof!

**含章鼎**：我打算在米尔内简单做点生意，他们的金刚石能卖出好价钱。尤其是卖给东方分部那群家伙——\
**Han Zhang**: I've actually got some business lined up in Mirny. Those diamonds of theirs are certain to fetch a tidy profit back in the East Branch.

**命名日**：我真后悔答应让你出来透气。能不能打个商量？你，安安静静地扮演货物，我，把你送到地方，剩下的话你可以找那个需要你帮忙的家伙念叨。\
**Name Day**: I should've never let you out. Can we make a deal? You stay quiet, and I'll get you safely to our destination. Then, you can say whatever you've got to say to whoever made the mistake of inviting you here.

**命名日**：唉……你实在话太多了，他们不肯跑这趟肯定也有这原因！\
**Name Day**: *sigh* You know you really, really, really like to talk? I'm beginning to understand why no one else would take this job!

**含章鼎**：难道你见过不擅长说话的商人？而且路上要是没点声响多无聊。\
**Han Zhang**: Whoever heard of a merchant who doesn't like to talk? Ha. Admit it, you'd be bored to tears if I were not here.

**含章鼎**：——？！\
**Han Zhang**: ...?!

喋喋不休的小生物被罩进了外套底下，连带着盖住了它细碎的说话声。\
The chatty salamander is tucked under Name Day's coat, its muttering smothered along with it.

**命名日**：安静。\
**Name Day**: Quiet.

**含章鼎**：真稀奇，这地方也能碰到土匪打劫……\
**Han Zhang**: Bandits—in the Arctic Circle? That's new.

附近的雪堆恰好能充当掩体，将基金会职员的身影挡得严严实实。\
Nearby snowbanks serve perfectly as cover, shielding Name Day from view.

**投机者Ⅰ**：怎么没见着人？刚还瞅见那小子往这走。\
**Robber I**: Where is he? I saw someone coming this way.

**投机者Ⅱ**：再往前他进不去，那是个什么军事基地吧，总有带枪的守着。\
**Robber II**: We can't let him get any further. There's some kind of military base up ahead. And it's heavily guarded.

**投机者Ⅱ**：费了老大劲跟这段路，别啥也没捞到！我看那个神秘学道具还值点钱。\
**Robber II**: Think how far we've gone. We can't go home empty-handed. That arcane item they've got is probably worth a few Sharpodonties, don't you think?

**含章鼎**：**的[友善的东方粗口]，我是活的！我活得好好的——\
**Han Zhang**: &%#*! (curses from the east) "Item." Hey! I'm a living, breathing creature!

**命名日**：别和我说。对他们喊这句话，让他们听清楚。\
**Name Day**: You don't need to yell at me. Say it to them if you like!

太沉重的雪压断了树枝，他从地面找到正好合手的一段枝条。\
A branch heavy with snow snaps and is broken into a stick that fits his grip comfortably.

**含章鼎**：喂！你确定？！我要大声喊他们过来吗？！我得说什么？！\
**Han Zhang**: What? Are you sure? Never mind. What should I yell?

**命名日**：随便什么，能吸引他们的注意就行。\
**Name Day**: Anything. I just need you to draw their attention.

**命名日**：我不能让他们一直跟到普列谢茨克附近去。\
**Name Day**: I'm not letting them anywhere near Plesetsk.

**投机者Ⅰ**：往这走！这边有动静，快点！\
**Robber I**: This way! I hear something. Keep up!

雪堆上突兀地闪出一点深色，模样古怪的金属器皿吸引了所有视线。\
A dark shape juts out of the snow—the odd appearance of the strange metal vessel draws every eye.

**含章鼎**：呃——打劫！！留下买路财！！\
**Han Zhang**: Errrr. Ro-Ro-Robbery! Hands up, and give me all your cash!

刀锋适时地抵住了那只向金属器皿伸出的手。\
Name Day's blade lands right in time, stopping the hand reaching for the vessel.

**命名日**：*Čабля。\
**Name Day**: *Čабля.

基金会职员随手丢开了那段树枝，从地上抓起一把雪。\
Name Day tosses aside his stick and scoops up a handful of snow.

歪歪斜斜的脚印逃往远处，这些投机者仅剩的优点就是懂得放弃。\
The robbers' footprints trail away into the distance. If they had one redeeming trait, it was knowing when to cut their losses.

**含章鼎**：你手上不是本来就有刀吗！\
**Han Zhang**: What were you waiting for with that knife?

**命名日**：噢，那是收藏品，不是武器。\
**Name Day**: Oh, well, it's more of a collectible than a weapon.

**命名日**：现在你明白为什么需要找人亲自送货，而不是把你丢上哪趟车捎过来了？\
**Name Day**: But I guess you understand now why they sent me to escort you instead of hiding you in the back of some truck, huh?

**含章鼎**：也没见到有车往这种地方跑……刚刚你用了神秘术？为什么不直接变把枪？\
**Han Zhang**: I didn't see a single truck heading for Plesetsk on our whole journey here. By the way, was that knife thingy part of your arcane skill? Why don't you just make a gun instead?

**含章鼎**：那些铁块已经过时了，小子，科技发展了——现在是热兵器的时代！\
**Han Zhang**: Times have changed, friend. Blades are out of date. You should give yourself an upgrade and start blasting!

**命名日**：变不了，有这种水平，我现在就会在芝诺。\
**Name Day**: Nah. I'd probably be serving with Zeno if I was any good with guns.

**命名日**：听过芝诺那位传奇飞行员的新鲜事迹吗？“巴伦支海手术刀”。\
**Name Day**: Have you ever heard of that legendary pilot from Zeno, the Barents Witch?

**命名日**：很遗憾，这么酷的家伙不会来护送一只聒噪的蝾螈。而我最多变点手边的垃圾，来点废物利用。\
**Name Day**: If you were really important, then you would get a guard like that. All that being a noisy little salamander gets you is a guy that can turn trash into knives.

**含章鼎**：……这简直是我见识过最没用的神秘术。\
**Han Zhang**: Ah! That's nearly the most useless arcane skill I've ever heard of.

**含章鼎**：除了我自己的神秘术以外。好吧，我们扯平了。\
**Han Zhang**: I say "nearly" because it's still better than mine. So, I'm not in a position to criticize.

**命名日**：你的神秘术是什么？\
**Name Day**: What does your arcane skill do?

小蝾螈的轮廓晃了晃，骤然消散成一捧香灰，又迅速地凝聚回原貌。\
The salamander's silhouette flickers, crumbling into a puff of ash, then, in the blink of an eye, reforms itself.

**含章鼎**：……像这样？\
**Han Zhang**: That's it.

**命名日**：……很有特色。\
**Name Day**: It's certainly ... something.

接下来的路程终于迎得了暂时的安静。\
The rest of the journey is at last blessedly quiet.

目的地越来越近，建筑物的轮廓逐渐清晰，有人已经提前在雪地里等候。\
Their destination draws near. The outlines of buildings take shape, and someone is already waiting in the snow.

**命名日**：北方哨歌女士。\
**Name Day**: Ms. Windsong.

所谓的航天基地也并没有想象中那样高大。\
The so-called cosmodrome isn't nearly as grand as imagined.

在这样辽阔的土地上，任何生物和建筑都显得相当渺小。\
Surrounded by the vast expanse of white, people and buildings alike feel small.

**北方哨歌**：你们好，两位先生。\
**Windsong**: Hello, gentlemen.

**北方哨歌**：欢迎来到普列谢茨克。\
**Windsong**: Welcome to Plesetsk.

## CO-07 园圃与花园 / The Wilds and the Garden

**北方哨歌**：你们到得比预计时间更快，我想指针和冷周六会相当开心。\
**Windsong**: You arrived earlier than expected. Pointer and Hissabeth will be happy to know you got here safely.

**北方哨歌**：噢，指针就是那位介绍我去拉普拉斯的职员，你应该见过她……在来亚什基。\
她正在帮忙招待几位重要的访客，晚些我们再去找她。\
**Windsong**: Oh, FYI, Pointer was the researcher who introduced me to Laplace. You might have met her before in Rayashki. She's occupied with a few important visitors right now. We'll talk to her later.

**北方哨歌**：至于冷周六，我觉得亲自见个面会比我来做介绍更快。\
**Windsong**: As for Hissabeth, you can meet her in person and save me the trouble of an introduction.

她推开了眼前的房门。\
She pushes open the door.

与此同时，在大楼另一侧，指针也推开了办公室的门。\
Meanwhile, on the other side of the building, Pointer enters through another door.

**指针**：离约定时间还有一个多钟头，你们来得这么早？\
**Pointer**: Our appointment was set for an hour from now. You're a bit early, sir.

指针往旁边让开身子，示意身后的两个人先进门。她打量着那个沉默的小姑娘，没有从对方身上看出什么特别之处。\
Pointer steps aside, motioning for the people hurrying behind her to go in first. She studies the quiet girl, not finding anything particularly unusual.

**科兹洛夫**：马戏团今天不算忙——重要的事总是早做准备才好。您放心，我们也没等多久……\
**Mr. Kozlov**: There wasn't much work to do today. And Alia always has everything prepared ahead of anything important. I-It's nothing to worry about.

**指针**：坐吧，挑哪把椅子都行。北方哨歌和冷周六应该会准时过来。\
**Pointer**: Please take a seat. Windsong and Hissabeth will join us later.

**指针**：有什么问题都可以先和我聊聊。\
**Pointer**: If you have any questions, feel free to ask me.

**库珀花环**：麻烦您了。您可以称呼我库珀花环，我想向您询问一件事。\
**Kiperina**: Thank you, ma'am. Please call me Kiperina. I have something to ask you.

先开口的竟然是这个小姑娘，这让指针略微感到意外。她调整了自己的表情，带上少量柔和的笑意。\
Kiperina is the first to speak, surprising Pointer. She adjusts her expression, adding a hint of warmth to her smile.

**指针**：叫我指针就行。请说吧。\
**Pointer**: That's fine with me, Ms. Kiperina. My name is Pointer. So, what would you like to know?

**库珀花环**：如果我愿意参加训练，接受成为宇航员的邀请，我会得到相应的……无论是卢布还是别的任何东西吗？\
**Kiperina**: If I take the offer and complete all the required training, what will I get in return? Do you pay in ruble or something equivalent?

**库珀花环**：我还想确认，假如发生任何意外，是否可以确保这些东西能送到我的家人手上？\
**Kiperina**: And I'd also like to know if my family will receive my pay in case anything happens to me.

指针抬头重新端详着眼前的人。她读得出科兹洛夫脸上的担忧，但没有立刻为库珀花环的神色找到合适的分类。\
Pointer looks up and examines the girl once more. She can read the worry in Mr. Kozlov's face, but she still can't quite place the look on hers.

介于勇气和恐惧之间。这样的划分对指针而言太过精微。\
Somewhere between courage and fear. Too fine a line for Pointer to draw.

植物与机器平分了不多的空间，室内比开着暖气的走廊温度更高。\
Plants and machines crowd the limited space, struggling for a balance somewhere between jungle and office floor. It's warmer here than in the hallway outside.

年轻人往旁边瞧了一眼，北方哨歌没有要开口的意思。\
Name Day glances sideways, but Windsong has no intention of speaking.

**命名日**：……打扰了，有人在吗？\
**Name Day**: Hello? Is anyone there?

**命名日**：从基金会远东分部调用的材料已经安全送到。\
**Name Day**: The materials you sent from the Far East Branch have arrived safely.

**命名日**：请及时检查，清单上的所有东西都在这儿了。\
**Name Day**: Everything you asked for on your list is there. But you should check it over as soon as possible.

他在桌面上找到一块空隙，从口袋里捞出那个金属物件。\
He scrounges around for a clear spot on the desk and pulls a metal vessel from his pocket,

小蝾螈团在里头睡得正香，直到有人戳了戳它的脑袋，抖落一捧灰尘。\
revealing a little sleeping salamander roused from its slumber by a tap on the head that sends a puff of ash into the air.

**命名日**：醒醒，现在是工作时间。\
**Name Day**: Hey. Wake up. You're at work.

研究员从众多机器后闪出身影，首先和北方哨歌打了个招呼。\
Hissabeth emerges from behind the machinery and offers a brisk wave to Windsong.

**冷周六**：嗯？你今天这么早就从矿坑回来，是打算给远道而来的同事办个欢迎会？\
**Hissabeth**: Windsong? Back from the mine already? Are you going to throw a welcome party for our new colleagues?

**北方哨歌**：矿坑的调查可以先放一放，事情还是有重要与次要之分。\
**Windsong**: The mine can wait, but I can't. Those materials are top priority.

接着，研究员的目光转向眼前的年轻人。\
Now Hissabeth turns her attention to the young man in front of her.

**冷周六**：多谢，应该有人跟你提过，我是冷周六。\
**Hissabeth**: Thanks. You might have heard of me. My name's Hissabeth.

**冷周六**：我们的计划书你应该也读过？我就不多废话了。指针还在忙，待会儿你会见到她的。\
**Hissabeth**: You've read our proposal, haven't you? It'd save me a lot of trouble if you had. I'll catch you up with Pointer as soon as she's available.

基金会职员盯着那几条探头探脑的小蛇，发誓自己看见其中一条在吐信子。\
Name Day finds himself staring at the curious little snakes poking out, swearing he saw one flick its tongue.

他没法犹豫太久，还是选择了按社交礼节走完整套流程，握手，然后自我介绍。\
There's no time to hesitate. He decides to follow proper etiquette—handshake, then introduction.

**命名日**：命名日，远东分部调查员。\
**Name Day**: Name Day, Foundation Investigator for the Far East Branch.

**命名日**：我能不能先提个问题？\
**Name Day**: Mind if I ask you a question?

**冷周六**：请讲，我们提倡自由发言，这又不是审讯现场。\
**Hissabeth**: Go on. But this is an office, not an interrogation room.

她轻松地四处打量着，瞧见桌面多出的摆件，也轻轻敲了敲小蝾螈的脑袋。\
She looks around with an airy glance and, spotting the extra object on the desk, gives the little salamander a second gentle rap on the head.

**命名日**：——为什么要偷运卢恩矿石？\
**Name Day**: Why did you ask me to smuggle in this runium?

**冷周六**：哈？\
**Hissabeth**: What?

**命名日**：我没有别的意思，这么点数量……大概两三块？其实不算严重。\
**Name Day**: Don't get me wrong. I didn't report it. It's just ... it's odd. You didn't ask for much, just a few pieces.

**命名日**：虽然它现在不属于能随意取用的资源，但正常提交申请书也就是流程长一些……\
**Name Day**: It is a rare resource, I grant you. But I think you could've gotten this amount with no trouble by submitting an application. All you'd need to do is wait for a few weeks.

**命名日**：有必要为几块矿石冒风险吗？\
**Name Day**: Was it really worth the risk?

**冷周六**：当然有。因为我们没有多余的时间用来等待。\
**Hissabeth**: Yeah, because we don't have a few weeks to spare.

**北方哨歌**：“时间”现在就像这些从远方送来的向日葵种子一样宝贵。\
**Windsong**: Saving every bit of time we can is vital. It is as precious as this bag of sunflower seeds from a distant land. You don't find them often in these parts.

**北方哨歌**：接着。\
**Windsong**: Here.

理线学者扬起手，将小布袋抛向研究员。\
She lifts her hand and tosses Hissabeth a small cloth bag.

**北方哨歌**：我的那份已经拿走了，你也可以在办公室里种一些。\
**Windsong**: I've already taken my share. Why not plant some of these in the office?

**北方哨歌**：向日葵很容易养活，它们或许会追着白炽灯太阳移动脑袋呢。\
**Windsong**: It won't take too much effort. If you're lucky, you'll get to see them turn their heads towards the light bulbs.

研究员从袋子里取出她真正想要的东西。\
Hissabeth pulls out exactly what she was hoping for.

稀有的神秘学能源被随手抛起，又稳当地接住。\
Rare arcanum energy, tossed carelessly into the air but caught with practiced ease.

**冷周六**：要找到一个见过卢恩矿石，能顺理成章送它们过来，还会同意这件事的家伙，还挺不容易的。\
**Hissabeth**: Actually, Mr. Name Day, you're the perfect man for this job. You knew what you were smuggling, you had the perfect excuse to come here, and you were kind enough to help. It was quite the effort to track you down, you know.

**冷周六**：路上有没有碰见麻烦？\
**Hissabeth**: So, how did the trip go? Any trouble?

**命名日**：说不准他们是看中了矿石还是那只聒噪的“工艺品”。\
**Name Day**: You bet there was. Though I'm still not sure what those bandits were after, the runium or our noisy "arcane item."

**冷周六**：到处都缺资源，就得从市面上、从外边尽可能地收集，不管用不用得上……\
**Hissabeth**: There's a shortage of supplies everywhere nowadays. People take what they can, whether they need it or not.

**冷周六**：就算让那些人得手了，东西最后大概率还是会流回基金会或者拉普拉斯吧。\
**Hissabeth**: Even if they managed to take the cargo, it'd probably just end up in another branch of the Foundation or Laplace.

**冷周六**：你这趟外勤可是帮忙省了一大笔采购经费。\
**Hissabeth**: Anyway, you saved us a lot of time and resources.

**命名日**：有的东西花再多经费也买不到。还没听说哪儿发现了能替代来亚什基的矿场。\
**Name Day**: Just bear in mind, this runium is not something that you can replace even with Sharpodonties.

**冷周六**：我会省着用。替我谢谢维拉女士。\
**Hissabeth**: Thanks. We'll use it sparingly. Please send my gratitude to Ms. Vila.

**冷周六**：第二件事，轮到我提问了。\
**Hissabeth**: And one more thing.

**冷周六**：你打算留下帮忙吗？\
**Hissabeth**: What would you say if I asked you to stay?

**冷周六**：请你偷运矿石用的是北方哨歌的关系，现在是我的个人请求。\
**Hissabeth**: Don't worry. I won't play the Windsong card. It's only a personal request.

**冷周六**：如果有基金会的人参与，很多需要走流程的事儿都会方便些。\
**Hissabeth**: We could save a lot of time with our procedural work if we had a Foundation Investigator on the team.

**冷周六**：对你而言，这也是一个很好的机会——如果我们的小队最后取得成功，你的名字当然会被写在表彰名单上。\
**Hissabeth**: And it could be a great opportunity to earn a reputation. Imagine the prestige if the project ends up a success.

**命名日**：……\
**Name Day**: ...

基金会职员咽下了刚要说出的话。他不打算对自己来这里的理由多做解释。\
He swallows his words, not intending to explain his reason for being here.

冷周六给出的理由也不错，方便理解，也不会涉及太多私人信息。\
Hissabeth's version works just fine—easy to understand, and not too personal.

**命名日**：你们现在进度如何？\
**Name Day**: Are you making any progress?

**冷周六**：如你所见，真是穷得叮当响，最新进账就是这些矿石。\
**Hissabeth**: As much as we can, but we don't have a single Sharpodonty to our name, and this runium is the sum total of all the supplies we've received recently.

**冷周六**：研究基地余下的大部分资源会留给我们，可那本来就没多少。不过好消息是航天飞船不用自己从头造，燃料也是现成的，启动按钮谁都会按——我们缺人。\
**Hissabeth**: They told us we could use all the resources left in Plesetsk, but that amounts to jack all. Thankfully, we still have half a rocket, fuel, and a launch button. Still, to make up for the supply shortage, we need additional manpower.

**冷周六**：当然，还有一个能令你安心的好消息。我们已经找到了一名合适的宇航员。\
**Hissabeth**: Oh, but there's some good news: we don't have to worry about finding our astronaut. We already have a perfect candidate.

**指针**：我们非常需要一位宇航员。\
**Pointer**: We're in dire need of an astronaut.

**指针**：能够用于训练的时间并不多，绝大多数人选都不可能短期内适应失重环境，更无法承受高温和高压。\
**Pointer**: There isn't enough time for anyone to finish the full training course. No one would be able to acclimate to a zero-gravity environment in such a short time, not to mention the high pressure and heat.

**指针**：但库珀花环小姐的神秘术或许能帮助她做到这件事。\
**Pointer**: But you may be the exception, Ms. Kiperina. Your arcane skill may allow us to work a miracle.

**指针**：不仅仅是经济补贴，我们也能为你提供担保，为你争取一张拉普拉斯的正式员工证。\
**Pointer**: So, if you take the offer, we'll provide you with a salary and try to get you a permanent position here at Laplace.

**指针**：冷周六已经在着手准备这件事，她找了基金会人员来帮忙，好加快审批进度。\
**Pointer**: Hissabeth is already working on it. She has a contact in the Foundation who can help with the procedures.

**库珀花环**：我没有别的问题了。\
**Kiperina**: Alright then. I have no more questions.

指针注意到，即便听完了这些详尽的解释，女孩脸上的忧虑也没有丝毫减少。\
Pointer notes that, despite their thorough explanation, the girl seems no less worried.

**库珀花环**：但我还是要说明，我并不像你们想的那样厉害，我的神秘术仅仅能用于照明。所以……\
**Kiperina**: But, just to be clear, I don't think my arcane skill is as useful as you believe. It only makes a little firework show.

**科兹洛夫**：您知道，这个年纪的孩子都很容易害羞——您这样夸奖她，阿涅娅肯定不好意思。\
她是愿意尝试的，让她先参加训练，您就知道她很可靠！\
**Mr. Kozlov**: Heh, she's being modest. You know how children are when they receive a compliment, but I tell you she is more than willing to take your offer. Please give her an opportunity. You'll see how reliable she is!

**科兹洛夫**：对了，我们马戏团里还有个新来的小姑娘，她或许也能试试……\
**Mr. Kozlov**: By the way, another little arcanist girl joined our circus recently. Do you think she could stay with you too?

**指针**：并不是每个人的神秘术都合适。\
**Pointer**: That's not really how this works. Not everyone's arcane skill works in the same manner.

**科兹洛夫**：她也能和阿涅娅做个伴儿，您想想，她再怎么说也还是玩洋娃娃的年纪——\
**Mr. Kozlov**: But she would keep Alia company. Please, madam, Alia is still just a child who plays with dolls.

**库珀花环**：我很早就不这么做了，科兹洛夫先生！\
**Kiperina**: Mr. Kozlov, stop! I haven't played with dolls in ages!

**库珀花环**：……我已经是个大人了。\
**Kiperina**: I ... I'm already grown up!

**指针**：……\
**Pointer**: ...

看见进门以来就不动声色的女孩终于有了些外露的情绪，指针觉得自己终于触摸到了问题的核心。\
Seeing emotion break through the girl's steady silence at last, Pointer feels she's reached the root of the issue.

**指针**：我们可以考虑。您方便把提到的人选带来吗？\
**Pointer**: We'll take a look at what she can do. Would you be able to bring her here now?

**科兹洛夫**：当然方便！我现在就去。\
**Mr. Kozlov**: Of ... of course. I'll be right back.

他跑出办公室的速度相当快。库珀花环犹豫着在椅子上调整姿势，坐得更加端正。\
He bolts up and out of the office. In his wake, Kiperina hesitates, shifting in her seat, until at last sitting up straighter.

指针也收起了笑容。她觉得接下来的对话中并不需要这种社交技巧。\
Pointer's smile fades. There's no need for social niceties in what comes next.

**指针**：——现在，你可以说出你的真实想法了。\
**Pointer**: Alright, we're finally alone. Now, how about you tell me what you're actually thinking?

**冷周六**：最大的技术难题尚未解决，不过我有九成把握。\
**Hissabeth**: Our biggest issue remains unsolved, but I'm most certain we can resolve it.

**冷周六**：情况好坏参半——整体向好。\
**Hissabeth**: The entire project is a mixed bag right now, but I'd say more good than bad.

**冷周六**：假设这位睡着的朋友能按照预想提供帮助，情况就会继续往“好”倾斜。\
**Hissabeth**: If our little sleepyhead in that pod there can provide what we need, our situation should improve dramatically.

她摇晃那枚四足小鼎，让小蝾螈体会了一把失重的感觉。\
She tips the little vessel, giving the salamander a brief experience of zero gravity.

**含章鼎**：我……我梦到自己在月球……砍树……\
**Han Zhang**: I was dreaming of cutting a tree on the moon.

**含章鼎**：有什么一定要我参与的活儿吗？如果没事，请你们就把我当做普通摆件，我需要死一样的睡眠！\
**Han Zhang**: *yawn* You'd better have a good reason to wake me up. I'm not your lackey. We made a deal, that's all. And I'm freaking tired after that trip!

**冷周六**：按我们约好的，我需要你为我的材料研究帮点小忙。\
**Hissabeth**: Yeah, and about that deal? I need something from you, now.

**冷周六**：绝缘，耐高温，具有良好的神秘术耐受。你这间金属屋子的材质可真不错。\
**Hissabeth**: This little pod of yours. It's electrically insulated, heat-resistant, and highly durable against arcane energy. In short: the perfect aerospace material.

**冷周六**：我刮些粉末做成分分析。很快，就像你看了次牙医……\
**Hissabeth**: All I need is to sand off a bit of material from it. Don't worry. Just think of it as dental work.

**含章鼎**：等等！等等！我们应该一手交钱一手交货！\
**Han Zhang**: Wait, wait. You haven't paid for that yet.

**含章鼎**：你不会忘了条件吧？\
**Han Zhang**: A deal is a deal.

研究员确实需要一点时间回忆，好在她最后找到了答案。\
She needs a moment to think but eventually lands on a solution.

指甲盖大小的工牌被挂在了小蝾螈的尾巴上。\
She hooks a tiny badge the size of a fingernail onto the salamander's tail.

**冷周六**：你的员工证。先告诉你，这是实习证件，请好好表现。\
**Hissabeth**: Here's your ID card. Just to be clear, this is only for an internship. You'll need to actually work to earn yourself a permanent one.

**冷周六**：这可是用我的正式员工身份做担保才要来的。\
**Hissabeth**: And don't do anything stupid. I vouched for you, and now both our necks are on the line.

**含章鼎**：我看它很适合我！我早就说我瞅着该在拉普拉斯就职，东方分部的工程类竞争太强了……\
**Han Zhang**: Oh, it does look good on me. I knew I belong with Laplace. *sigh* The engineers at the Foundation's East Branch are way too competitive for my liking.

**含章鼎**：你还想知道什么吗？我这里也有一些试图用火药飞天的记载，或者炼丹……这个比较难。\
**Han Zhang**: So, what else you need? I've brought some records about gunpowder-fueled flight, and a few books on Eastern alchemy. Though, I'm not sure you'd be able to read any of them.

在小蝾螈喋喋不休时，研究员已经把它翻来覆去瞧了个遍，最后指向容器底部四四方方的文字。\
As the little salamander chatters on, she flips over its vessel and inspects it thoroughly before pointing to the square markings on the vessel's base.

理线学者和基金会职员都围了过来，人们总是难以抗拒自己的好奇心。\
The others gather close, unable to resist their curiosity.

**冷周六**：我想知道这行字的意思。\
**Hissabeth**: What does this mean?

**含章鼎**：这个？我现在住的鼎来自潘家园，说真的，工艺不错。\
**Han Zhang**: Oh, that? You know, I got this pod from the Panjiayuan Antique Market. It's not a genuine antique, but the craftsmanship is quite excellent.

**含章鼎**：这行字是“微波炉可用”。那时候微波炉是稀罕物件！\
**Han Zhang**: These characters here mean "microwave safe." Funny enough, microwave ovens were not that popular when I got it.

**含章鼎**：说到潘家园，这么大这么有意思的旧货市场很难得，买什么古董啦收藏品啦，就适合往里头钻。\
**Han Zhang**: Speaking of Panjiayuan, you can't find a flea market as big or as fun anywhere else. If you're ever looking for antiques and collectibles, it should be your first stop.

**含章鼎**：如果你们真心想看看，我也不是不能找机会带你们去……\
**Han Zhang**: Humph, if you want to go take a look, I might just be nice for once and take you ...

小蝾螈察觉到了理线学者和基金会职员闪闪发亮的视线。\
Little salamander notices their eager eyes.

终于有机会发挥商人的好口才，它打算进一步抓住这个时机——\
At last, a chance to show off its salesman charm—a moment it's determined to seize.

**冷周六**：不是什么“禁止触碰，否则爆炸”就行，我吃过那些莫名其妙的神秘学发明的亏。\
**Hissabeth**: No, thanks. Just making sure it doesn't mean "danger, explosive." I already learned that lesson from another escapade with an arcane invention.

她把不知道何时借走的匕首还给基金会职员，又将那个装满金属粉末的小瓶塞进办公桌抽屉。\
She returns the dagger she'd borrowed—who knows when—and slips the vial of metal powder into her desk drawer.

**冷周六**：好了，我弄到需要的粉末了，很快吧？你光顾着说话，应该压根没感觉。\
**Hissabeth**: Alright. I've collected enough. You were so busy talking you didn't feel a thing, did you?

**冷周六**：然后——这位远道而来的灰白格子，你呢？考虑好了吗？\
**Hissabeth**: Now, back to our visitor in the checkered pattern uniform, have you made a decision?

短暂的沉默之后，命名日问出口的却是另一个问题。\
After a brief pause, the question Name Day asks switches the conversation to an entirely different track.

**命名日**：在计划结束之后，你们打算拿那位小宇航员怎么办？\
**Name Day**: What are you going to do with the little astronaut when the project's over?

**冷周六**：只要她同意加入计划，我立刻就会给她提交入职拉普拉斯的申请。你愿意为此添份力就更好。\
**Hissabeth**: I'll submit her application to Laplace once she agrees to join us. It'd be great if you could help with her employment procedures.

**命名日**：我指的是，她什么时候才会知道“暴雨”会造成怎样的后果。\
**Name Day**: I mean, when are you going to tell her the real consequences of the "Storm"?

**冷周六**：在她拿到正式员工证的时候。\
**Hissabeth**: Same as always, as soon as she gets a permanent position with Laplace.

命名日看向北方哨歌，他以为北方哨歌会加入这场对话，至少做几句解释。但她只是点了点头。\
Name Day glances at Windsong, thinking she might chime in—offer an explanation, at least. But she only nods.

事实如此。那位素未谋面的小宇航员也迟早该知道，灰白穹顶和冰冷的金属建筑无法庇护所有人。\
That's just how it is. That little astronaut, whom they've never even met, will have to learn it too: That pale dome and those cold steel buildings can't protect everyone.

雨水会将熟悉的事物冲刷殆尽。一次，再一次。\
Soon, the rain will wash away all that's familiar to them. Again, and again.

**命名日**：……\
**Name Day**: ...

**命名日**：我留下。\
**Name Day**: Alright, then I'll stay.

**指针**：你想留在马戏团？\
**Pointer**: You mean you really want to stay with the circus?

库珀花环没有直接给出答案。\
Kiperina doesn't have a straight answer.

**库珀花环**：我……我可以来帮忙，但能不能拿到拉普拉斯的员工证，对我来说不重要。\
**Kiperina**: I ... I meant that I'm willing to do whatever you need, but I don't think I want to do this permanently.

**库珀花环**：如果大家都说我的神秘术能起作用，你们需要我加入，我就答应——我自己也不清楚，我能做到哪些事，在哪些地方派上用场。\
**Kiperina**: Since you say that you need my arcane skill for this project, I'm happy to help, though I don't really know if I can.

**指针**：我觉得你其实很清楚团长为什么要做这个选择。\
**Pointer**: I think you know why Mr. Kozlov brought you all this way.

**指针**：你们多久没吃上肉了？\
**Pointer**: When was the last time you had a proper meal?

**库珀花环**：我们有炖菜吃，团长也会想办法弄到罐头。\
**Kiperina**: Well, we usually have stews, and sometimes Mr. Kozlov will find us some canned food if we're lucky.

她的反驳声音很小，因此越发缺少说服力。\
Her rebuttal is soft and utterly unconvincing.

**指针**：你准备在马戏团待一辈子吗？\
**Pointer**: And you still want to spend the rest of your life in that circus?

**库珀花环**：……\
**Kiperina**: ...

敲门声撞破了这阵沉默。库珀花环趁这个时候仰起头。\
A knock breaks the silence. Kiperina uses the moment to lift her head.

当她再次坐好，刚刚在她眼睛里闪烁的光点已经被抹得很干净了。\
By the time she sits back down again, the light that had flickered in her eyes is gone.

**科兹洛夫**：我们的另一个小姑娘在这里，她不怎么喜欢说话，但性格很好。\
**Mr. Kozlov**: This is her, the girl I talked about. She doesn't speak much, but I feel that she has a good character.

**远旅**：……\
**Voyager**: ...

女孩儿好奇的目光扫过每个人，在指针那儿顿了顿。\
The girl casts a sweeping look across the room, pausing briefly on Pointer.

**科兹洛夫**：去吧，坐到阿涅娅旁边。\
**Mr. Kozlov**: Don't be shy. You can sit next to Alia.

**科兹洛夫**：你们刚才聊了些啥？阿涅娅没给您添麻烦吧，女士？\
**Mr. Kozlov**: What were you talking about? I hope our Alia didn't cause any trouble, madam.

他往房间里踏出两步，才发觉库珀花环的注意力在他手中提着的包裹上。那里边是他和娜塔莉亚收拾好的、认为两个女孩儿会需要的东西。\
He steps into the room, noticing immediately that Kiperina is fixated on the parcel in his hands. It's filled with things he and Natalya packed—things they thought the girls might need.

**库珀花环**：科兹洛夫先生……\
**Kiperina**: Mr. Kozlov ...

**库珀花环**：……我还会回到乌特恩亚亚吗？\
**Kiperina**: Will I ever have the chance to return to Utrennyaya?

## CO-08 当日子往前 / When We Move Forward

**库珀花环**：……我还会回到乌特恩亚亚吗？\
**Kiperina**: Will I ever have the chance to return to Utrennyaya?

冷周六带着其他人推门进入办公室时正遇到这一幕。她饶有兴趣地站在一旁，见证女孩得到她的回答。\
Hissabeth pushes the door open just in time to catch this scene. She lingers nearby, curious, watching the girl receive her answer.

**科兹洛夫**：那会是未来的事。\
**Mr. Kozlov**: We can talk about that in the future.

**科兹洛夫**：我们还会保持联系，你可以和远旅一起回来看望马戏团的大家。\
**Mr. Kozlov**: Of course, we will keep in touch. You and Voyager can pay us a visit whenever you like.

**科兹洛夫**：……她吃得不多，也是个聪明的孩子，不吵闹。她能留下，对吧？\
**Mr. Kozlov**: The girl's called Voyager, madam. She's clever, quiet, doesn't eat much. You-You will take her in too, won't you?

指针对此没有意见。她简单地进行了一些分析，认为同龄人的陪伴的确有助于缓解库珀花环的训练压力。\
Pointer doesn't object. She runs a brief analysis and concludes that the company of a peer could help ease the pressures of Kiperina's training.

仔细听完指针的说明后，科兹洛夫最后拍了拍花环的肩膀。\
After listening carefully, Mr. Kozlov pats Kiperina's shoulder.

**科兹洛夫**：努力让自己过上不用东奔西跑的日子，好吗，阿涅娅？\
**Mr. Kozlov**: I always hoped you would settle down and live a comfortable life. Promise me, you'll do your best, Alia.

**库珀花环**：……好的，团长。\
**Kiperina**: Yes, Mr. Kozlov.

**冷周六**：噢，你们终于商量完了。看起来不太需要我再做解释。\
**Hissabeth**: Oh, you've finally reached an agreement. Cool, looks like I won't have to do any more explaining.

**冷周六**：如果现在是告别时间，我觉得你得给这位看上去很不开心的小家伙留点什么纪念品。\
**Hissabeth**: If you're saying goodbye soon, maybe you ought to consider bringing her a parting gift. She looks like she could use one.

**命名日**：没错，到时候她能带着这份纪念品去找您。\
**Name Day**: Yeah, something to remind her of home.

懂得观察气氛的基金会职员飞快地接上这句话。\
Name Day picks up the thread without missing a beat.

北方哨歌也在此刻适时地迈出脚步，站到库珀花环身边。于是冷周六没再开口。\
Windsong steps forward just in time, joining Kiperina's side, and Hissabeth trails off.

**北方哨歌**：不需要什么贵重的礼物，但你至少得鼓励她几句，是不是？\
**Windsong**: Or maybe you can offer a few words of encouragement? What do you say?

科兹洛夫看到库珀花环用小指轻轻摩挲着手中的仪器，那是北方哨歌之前借给她的。这个小动作说明库珀花环感到紧张。\
Mr. Kozlov spies Kiperina rubbing the device in her hands with her pinky—the one Windsong had lent her earlier. He knows her well enough to understand the meaning: nervous.

他不清楚仪器的具体价值，但马戏团里肯定无法轻易找到这样的东西。\
He has no idea about the device's exact value, but he's certain it's not something you'd easily find in a circus.

**科兹洛夫**：哈哈，礼物嘛……得给我留点时间做准备。\
**Mr. Kozlov**: Right, right, a gift. I-I'll need some time to prepare it.

**科兹洛夫**：不如这样，我们做个约定——等你未来回马戏团看望大伙儿，再来取这份礼物。\
**Mr. Kozlov**: Let's make a deal, shall we? You'll get your gift next time you pay a visit to the Utrennyaya.

**科兹洛夫**：这么一来你肯定也会记得回家。我还怕你到时候嫌麻烦，不肯跑太远。\
**Mr. Kozlov**: That way, you'll keep us in mind and come home again one day. I was worried you might not want to travel such a long way for us.

**库珀花环**：不，即使乌特恩亚亚去了最远最远的北方，我也会来找你们。\
**Kiperina**: I will, Mr. Kozlov. I'll find my way back to Utrennyaya even if you've moved to the other end of the world.

她费力地拎起科兹洛夫带来的包裹，基金会职员赶紧接过它，把它放到了一旁的桌上。\
She struggles to lift the parcel Mr. Kozlov gave her. Name Day quickly steps in to assist her in placing it on the table.

时间过得真快。科兹洛夫的脑海里突然冒出这句感叹，但他说出的内容与此毫不相关。\
"Time flies." The thought pops into Mr. Kozlov's head, but what he says out loud has nothing to do with it.

**科兹洛夫**：好，好。阿涅娅是个好孩子——\
**Mr. Kozlov**: Hahaha, that's my girl.

**科兹洛夫**：记不记得那句话？“做好你能做的每件事，就能摆脱遗憾。”\
**Mr. Kozlov**: Remember what I said? Do the best that you can and have no regrets.

**科兹洛夫**：你能让我和娜塔莉亚放心，对吧？\
**Mr. Kozlov**: Natalya and I don't have to worry about you, do we?

**库珀花环**：嗯，我可以。\
**Kiperina**: No.

**库珀花环**：我一定会尽全力的，就像在乌特恩亚亚一样。\
**Kiperina**: I'll give my best performance here, like I always did with Utrennyaya.

像是为了说服自己，她连着点了两次头，用最严肃、最认真的语气做出许诺。\
Almost like she's trying to convince herself, she nods twice in a row and makes a solemn promise in her most serious tone.

未来是否只是个概念？这个问题被刻意地忽视，就像压在旧衣箱底部的秘密。\
A question rises up in her, just below the surface. How can she be sure? She chooses not to ask.

1987 6月 普列谢茨克发射基地\
June 1987, Plesetsk Cosmodrome

**指针**：感觉如何？许多人在开始训练的头几个月都会有较为明显的不适感。\
**Pointer**: How do you feel? Intense nausea is common for the first few months of zero-g training.

**库珀花环**：呼……我想基本上——没问题——\
**Kiperina**: *pant* I think I'm fine.

**库珀花环**：感谢您的关心。\
**Kiperina**: You're very kind to ask, ma'am.

第一次训练结束后，库珀花环吐了出来。\
Her first training session was rough and more than a little messy, causing her to throw up.

指针将她扶到医务室，等喘匀了气，她磕绊着说出自己的要求，和现在所说的一样。\
Pointer helped her to the infirmary. Once she could breathe again, she stammered out a request—just like the one she made today.

**库珀花环**：我们应该增加训练日程。\
**Kiperina**: I'm ready for more.

**指针**：我否决过很多次了。冷周六刚刚才看过你最新的体检数据和神秘术测试报告，你不能再给自己增加任何训练，而是要学会休息。\
**Pointer**: You're at this again? Hissabeth already checked your vitals and arcane skill test reports. Her conclusion was clear: You need to rest and recover before we begin again.

**指针**：如果你把自己逼到了极限，因此病倒，我们的计划也同样无法完成。\
**Pointer**: If you push yourself too hard and become too sick to perform the mission, that won't help us either.

**库珀花环**：我还可以更努力！只要反复练习，我就能做得更好——\
**Kiperina**: But I can do more. All I need is a bit more training. I need to perform flawlessly.

**指针**：你不需要做得更好，你只要保证“能够做到”。\
**Pointer**: We don't need "flawless," not at the cost of your health. We need "satisfies all requirements." Nothing more.

指针调整着语气，尽力在脑海里寻找着可以称得上鼓励或安慰的句子。\
She adjusts her tone, searching her mind for something that might qualify as comfort or encouragement.

**指针**：你已经超出了我原本的期待。\
**Pointer**: You're already doing better than we anticipated.

她担心这句话太过干瘪，但库珀花环认真地摇了摇头。\
She fears the words come out too flat, but Kiperina shakes her head sincerely.

**库珀花环**：谢谢您。但我还没有背熟操作流程，也还无法熟练运用神秘术。\
**Kiperina**: Thank you. But I still haven't memorized the flight procedures, and I'm still struggling with my arcane skill.

**库珀花环**：我会向北方哨歌女士申请增加理线学课程。我想，这应该不属于过度训练的范围了吧？\
**Kiperina**: Maybe I can ask Ms. Windsong to give me another ley lines lesson. That's not "pushing myself," is it?

**指针**：……\
**Pointer**: ...

**指针**：那么你必须保证每天的八小时睡眠。\
**Pointer**: That's acceptable, but you will ensure you get a minimum of eight hours of sleep every day.

指针妥协了。在这样的年纪，她也有过拧着一股劲，想要拼命做好某件事的时候。\
Pointer gives in. She too had once been hell-bent on proving herself.

**指针**：还需要保证一日三餐的正常饮食。\
**Pointer**: And promise me you'll eat well and never skip meals.

**库珀花环**：当然。我记得冷周六女士说今晚有一场聚餐，所以我打算在回来后再做半小时练习……\
**Kiperina**: Yes, ma'am. Ms. Hissabeth said there would be a team-building dinner tonight. I'll attend it and train for another half an hour after we come back.

**指针**：不，我不是这个意思。\
**Pointer**: No. That's not what I meant.

照顾过于懂事的孩子也是一件常常令人不知所措的活计。\
There are few tasks more difficult than instructing a child who is too mature for her own good.

**指针**：别考虑这些了，快去吧，去换身衣服。我和你一块儿出门。\
**Pointer**: *sigh* Anyway, go change. We'll go together.

米尔内的几家餐馆中，这是生意最好的一家。冷周六在其中做了不少贡献。\
Of all the restaurants in Mirny, this one does the best business, thanks in no small part to Hissabeth.

她的确把吃饭看做生命中的重要之事，也真诚地希望让朋友们都尝到这份乐趣。\
With all those mouths to feed, food has always been a vital part of her lifestyle, one that she is only too eager to share with her team.

而且这儿有一张足够大的餐桌，小组里的每个人都能在桌旁找到自己的位置。\
Plus, the tables here are big enough for everyone in their group to have a seat.

**冷周六**：你刚认识我那天是不是就坐这儿？\
**Hissabeth**: We sat here when we first met, non?

**库珀花环**：好像是。现在这张桌子甚至有点儿挤……\
**Kiperina**: I think so. This table seems a bit too small now.

**北方哨歌**：至少帮忙的人够多，成功的几率也会大很多。\
**Windsong**: Well, there's strength in numbers.

**冷周六**：但最关键的还是小宇航员。神秘术练习得怎么样了？\
**Hissabeth**: Yet everything now depends on our brave astronaut. How's your arcane skill training?

**库珀花环**：大概还不错。北方哨歌女士是一位很好的老师。\
**Kiperina**: Not bad, I guess. Ms. Windsong is a wise teacher.

**北方哨歌**：哈哈，看来我的那位教师朋友也教会了我很多。你会有机会认识她的。\
**Windsong**: Haha, I'm glad I've learned something from my experience with Vila. I hope you'll get to know her one day.

**冷周六**：等你从宇宙顺利返回，就有大把时间可以用来认识一群有趣的家伙。\
**Hissabeth**: You'll have plenty of time to make friends once you return from your mission.

**库珀花环**：好呀。到时候，我可能得先去见一见马戏团的大家，科兹洛夫先生还等着我去取礼物呢。\
**Kiperina**: Looking forward to it. But first I have to go back to the circus. I think Mr. Kozlov will have my gift prepared by then. I'm sure he will.

**库珀花环**：……虽然他这周都没有过来看望我和远旅。\
**Kiperina**: Though, he didn't come to see me and Voyager this week.

**命名日**：一边忙着演出，另一边忙着训练，也很难找到共同的空闲。\
**Name Day**: He has a whole circus to run, and you're busy with training. It's hard to find a good time when you're both free.

**命名日**：也许那位先生怕你看到他，想起马戏团的生活，想着要快些回去，干脆就不往发射基地跑。\
**Name Day**: Perhaps he didn't want to make you homesick, but I'm sure he misses you a lot.

**命名日**：但米尔内离得很近，你可以抽空来镇上，回马戏团，花两三个钟头休息会儿也没什么……\
**Name Day**: Mirny isn't far from here. You should go back and visit sometime. No one will blame you if you take a break for a few hours.

**指针**：我可以开车送你。\
**Pointer**: I am able to drive you to town, if you need.

**指针**：只要你提前两天左右提交你的日程安排，我很可能也能够腾出空来。\
**Pointer**: Just submit your schedule two days in advance. I will set some time aside for a short trip.

**库珀花环**：谢谢。我想，我还是要在一切都顺利结束之后回去。\
**Kiperina**: Thank you. But I think it'll have to wait until the project's over.

**库珀花环**：那应该就是科兹洛夫先生说的“未来”。而且我得给他留出准备礼物的时间。\
**Kiperina**: Mr. Kozlov said I would always be able to visit him in the future. Besides, he needs time to prepare the gift.

并非所有人都对未来感兴趣，至少库珀花环的朋友更关心眼前的物件。\
Not everyone is interested in the still distant future. Kiperina's friend, at least, is more focused on what's right in front of her.

她轻轻敲击小鼎的边缘，为它清脆的声响露出微笑。\
She taps the edge of the small vessel, smiling at the crisp, metallic sound it makes.

**含章鼎**：拜托，请别这么做，回声会让我的脑袋发晕……\
**Han Zhang**: Err. Don't do that. The echo from that sound makes me dizzy.

**远旅**：……？\
**Voyager**: ...?

她缩回手，仔细观察了一阵，发现这只生物并没有任何攻击性行为。\
She pulls her hand back and watches until confirming the little creature is friendly.

于是她再次伸出手，试图摸索出与它和睦相处的办法。\
Then she reaches out again, trying to figure out how to get along with it.

**库珀花环**：……远旅？\
**Kiperina**: Voyager?

**库珀花环**：别走神，他们都要把菜吃光了——\
**Kiperina**: Don't get distracted. They've almost finished the food.

基金会职员默默地给桌上的食物换了个位置，推过两个还满着的碟子。\
Name Day swaps the food around the table, pushing two still-full plates to the middle.

冰冷的鳞片也在此刻贴上库珀花环的手腕。\
Cold scales press against Kiperina's wrist.

**小蛇Ⅰ**：你不渴吗？瞧这里，热牛奶和果汁，随你选。\
**Snake I**: Feel like a drink? Here, we've got some hot milk or warm apple cider. Pick one.

它拖着杯子艰难地前行到此，在桌面上留下一道长长的痕迹。\
Dragging a cup behind it, the snake leaves splotches of spilled drink all across the table.

**库珀花环**：我要这个，谢谢你。\
**Kiperina**: Milk will be fine. Thank you.

库珀花环为自己和远旅选好了热牛奶，学着其他人那样抬起胳膊。\
Kiperina passes another cup to Voyager. She mimics the others by lifting the cup, first in both hands and then just one.

**冷周六**：干杯，朋友们。庆祝我们成功地拉起了一支小队——先别管成不成吧。\
**Hissabeth**: Let's have a toast, friends. To our new team, though no one knows for sure whether our project will succeed or is doomed to fail catastrophically.

**冷周六**：为我们共同的目标！\
**Hissabeth**: Together, we're working towards the future, cheers!

一个友好的信号，一种象征团结的誓言。\
A friendly signal. A quiet promise of unity.

故事或关系转变的标志。从陌生人，变为并不完全陌生的人，直到——\
A turning point in any story or relationship, from a stranger to a colleague, and eventually—

Друг/Товарищ.“朋友/同志”\
Друг/Товарищ."Friend/Comrade."

**众人**：干杯！\
**All**: Cheers!

**冷周六**：我们的成功概率还是很大的。虽然没完全恢复到最佳技术水平，但拉普拉斯仍然拥有足够先进的科技，以及最好的科学家。\
**Hissabeth**: Having said that, the odds are in our favor. Even though Laplace is no longer in its prime, it still has the best technology and the finest scientists.

**北方哨歌**：噢？你是说“我们”吗？这个小组里当然是“最好的”那群人——我一直认为做研究最重要的就是坚持。\
**Windsong**: The finest scientists? You mean us? I couldn't agree more. I've always believed that perseverance is the most basic fundamental quality that any researcher should possess.

**指针**：返回未来是我唯一觉得该坚持的事。\
**Pointer**: Perseverance ... There's only one thing that I think we should persevere with: our efforts to return to the future.

**命名日**：原来拉普拉斯的所有人都这么喜欢“怀旧”。\
**Name Day**: Didn't know you Laplace researchers missed the good old days so much.

**指针**：不管你怎么摆弄文字……你得承认，那就是个足够好的时候。\
**Pointer**: Laugh if you want, but you can't deny that our era was better than this one.

库珀花环努力捕捉着这些词汇。室内很暖和，长桌边的谈话也很轻松，她压在心底的疑问也终于有了浮出来喘口气的时机。\
Kiperina keens her ears in, trying to catch each word. The room is warm, and the conversation at their table easy and relaxed. The question she's been keeping down finally bubbles out of her mouth.

**库珀花环**：……未来是什么样的？\
**Kiperina**: What was the future like?

**库珀花环**：我读过给临时员工的说明，知道要取到的数据也许能帮助大家找回一些消失的东西，也知道你们见过的“未来”可能并不是最后被找回来的那个。\
**Kiperina**: I've read through the manual for temporary employees. The data we're going to collect may help people get back the things that they lost, right? From the futures that you've been to.

**库珀花环**：但我还是想知道，在你们的那个九九年，列宁格勒变成了什么样子？那时候有没有马戏演出？\
**Kiperina**: What's Leningrad like in 1999? Were there any circus shows in your era?

**库珀花环**：所有事都变得更好了吗？糖果和其他物资都不再限量供应了吗？\
**Kiperina**: Does that mean everything was better than it is now? I have trouble imagining it. Were there sweets for everyone and stores that never ran out of food?

**北方哨歌**：……\
**Windsong**: ...

**北方哨歌**：是的。所有事，除了理线学。它还是这么边缘，因为它甚至无法吸引学习者的关心，让她对这门学科的未来没有一点儿展望……\
**Windsong**: Things were much better then, well, except for the study of ley lines. It was still struggling as a scientific pursuit, especially when it came to attracting new students. Though, even now its only student seems to lack much interest in it.

**库珀花环**：不，不是这样！抱歉，我光想着生活里的事……\
**Kiperina**: Th-That's not true! Sorry, I'm just having difficulty focusing on it with all the other demands on my time.

**命名日**：我想北方哨歌女士只是抛给了问题太多的学生一个小玩笑。\
**Name Day**: It's okay. Ms. Windsong was only making a joke at the expense of her very overworked student.

**命名日**：未来的一切都很好，在路边随便哪家店都能买到糖和你想要的几乎任何东西。\
**Name Day**: It's true things were nicer in the future. I do miss the sweets, and that the shops were never empty.

餐桌上的交谈听起来如此令人愉快，所有见证者都向她许诺这是值得的。\
Every witness seems to offer her the same promise: it's worth it.

日子应该往前，而不是反复地驻留于过去。\
Life should move forward, not stay stuck in the past.

**库珀花环**：太好了，我们一定会成功的，为所有人！\
**Kiperina**: Amazing! I'm sure we'll make it back one day!

这次她主动举起了杯子。

为最美好的前途。\
This time, she raises her cup first.

## CO-09 致陌生人 / To Former Strangers

1987 普列谢茨克发射基地暴雨前3个月\
1987, Plesetsk Cosmodrome3 months before the "Storm"

三，二，一。咔。\
Three, two, one, cut.

录制结束，一切依旧顺利。\
And just so we're clear, everything went well as usual.

简单来说，我手上这张卡带承载的东西惊人的沉重。\
The video in this disk, to put it simply, is too much for anyone to handle.

猜猜里边是些什么？没关系，选个你能想到最离谱的答案。\
Guess what it's used for. Go on. Give me the most ridiculous answer you can think of.

用上现代化思维……是的，一切都在发展，有许多内容都能以数据形态保存。\
A little tip: think like a modern person. The development of technology allows us to save a lot of things as digital data nowadays.

来份录像作为电子遗书，这可比过去手写的玩意方便多了。\
Yes, it's a last record. A video is much more convenient than sitting down with a pen.

她将数据卡放到桌面，伙伴们的目光适时地追了过来。\
She places the data card on the table. It immediately draws in all eyes.

**冷周六**：录像数据没问题。指针，你的那部分需要现在补上吗？还是之后再说？\
**Hissabeth**: Data secured. Pointer, do you want me to add your part to the video now? Or maybe later?

**指针**：我就不用了。后续的内容都是你那边的活儿，材料相关的东西我帮不上忙。\
**Pointer**: Preferably never. This whole "last record" thing is your passion. Besides, I know nothing about material sciences.

**冷周六**：但你花了那么多时间帮忙转写术式，当然也得出现在这份记录里！\
**Hissabeth**: But you spent so much time transcoding the incantation. You simply must show up in my video. Please, I insist.

**冷周六**：我们是一个小组，谁都不该缺席，对吧？\
**Hissabeth**: We're a team. We shouldn't miss anyone's perspective, non?

**指针**：……嗯。\
**Pointer**: Yes.

长时间工作相当消耗精神，她平静的回应里流露出一些疲倦。\
Even for her, long hours can wear things down. There's a trace of fatigue in her otherwise calm reply, a lag in her response.

**冷周六**：如果大伙儿都没意见，我们就进入复盘时间。虽然我个人更愿意称呼它为公开检讨。\
**Hissabeth**: Superbe, then let's take a look at our work so far and learn from our mistakes, well, my mistakes.

我和指针之前在普列谢茨克发射基地研究关于传送术式的内容。\
Pointer and I had been working on the teleport disk at the Plesetsk Cosmodrome.

更具体些来说，阶段性目标是用传送术式向太空站和航天飞船运送物资，最终目的是实现稳定的、安全的、生命体可用的宇宙空间内超长距离远程传送。\
More specifically, our interim mission was to determine how to transport supplies to space stations and spacecraft using teleport incantations. The ultimate goal being to achieve stable, safe, and long-distance teleportation to outer space viable for living organisms.

项目稳步推进，直到一个坏消息来临——\
The project had been going smoothly until we received some bad news.

由于规划变动，普列谢茨克发射基地的大多数研究项目都要被迫中止。\
Due to a policy change at Laplace, most projects in Plesetsk were being suspended.

所幸接下来好消息追上了坏消息。如果接下发射监测器，拿回“暴雨”前宇宙数据的任务——\
Fortunately, the bad news was followed by a small amount of good. Madam Lucy said if we could send a monitor to space to collect data when the "Storm" arrived ...

我们的研究就还能继续！甚至有机会为解决“暴雨”的问题出份力！\
We'd be allowed to continue with our project! It was a vital opportunity to make our contribution to deciphering the "Storm"!

我们只有几个小麻烦要解决。人手，能源，以及个人决心。\
There were only three major issues to solve: manpower, energy supply, and determination.

显然，人手问题和能源问题已经得到了解决。感谢各位的协助。\
As you can see, the first two issues have been solved by our new members. Thank you all for your help.

尤其要感谢我们的小宇航员。\
Especially our brave little astronaut.

计划很简单。她进入宇宙，到达指定坐标，投放并校准监测器位置，呼叫返航。\
The plan is now simple. She'll fly into space, reach the required altitude, launch the monitor, and zero in on the correct coordinates, and then, she'll contact ground control to come home.

她的神秘术将保护她撑过可能会有的窒息或高温。\
Her arcane skill will protect her from any possible danger caused by pressure or heat in the vacuum of space.

最后一步，她激活传送软盘，在地面等待的我们也同样激活软盘。\
Then finally, she will activate the teleport disk, and we will activate our receiver on the ground.

砰——所有人顺利地回到极圈内的普列谢茨克基地，安全，成功！\
Ta-da! Everyone will arrive in Laplace's Arctic Branch safe and sound to acclaim and accolades from all around the scientific world!

当然，以上是理想情况。截止目前，我们还有一箩筐的问题没有解决。\
Well, that's a simple framework of the plan. But we still have tons of minor problems to tackle first.

而其中最大的问题，就是传送软盘无法远距离精准定位。为此我们反复进行了多次测试。\
Our top priority is improving the long-distance positioning accuracy of the teleport disk. We've already begun testing our latest prototypes.

……但大家都知道，最后这次测试结果不妙。\
Though the last test didn't end well.

目前我还在寻找具体的失败原因。但理论上，这不过是一场在实验中难以避免的小小事故而已……\
We're still searching for the cause of that particular catastrophic error. But we won't let it stop us. This was no more than an inevitable roadblock, a small accident on the way to technological progress.

**指针**：冷周六。既然要吸取失败的教训，就不能逃避问题。\
**Pointer**: Hissabeth, if we are going to have any chance of learning from our mistakes, we can't run away from our problems.

好吧好吧，那是一周前的测试……\
Alright, alright. That last test was a week ago.

**冷周六**：还是老规矩，虽然我们能给软盘做些改良，但免不了需要一个具有足够智慧的生物来执行测试。\
**Hissabeth**: Same as the last time. Though we've made some improvements, we still need an intelligent creature to run the test.

**冷周六**：这一次也还是我来。\
**Hissabeth**: And I guess it'll be me again.

**命名日**：你确定吗？我觉得考虑到危险性和对任务的价值，实际上让我……\
**Name Day**: Are you sure? Considering the danger and your value to the project, I think you ought to let me ...

**冷周六**：我做的东西如果自己都不敢用，怎么还好意思拿给别人尝试？\
**Hissabeth**: How can I ask anyone to try my invention if I wouldn't use it myself?

**冷周六**：怎么，你在等什么？对了，记得一会儿退到安全区域的时候启动办公室隔离门。\
**Hissabeth**: Now, what are you waiting for? Get to the safe zone. Oh, and remember to secure the blast door.

**命名日**：昨天库珀花环小姐来喂生态缸里的鱼，询问过这件事。\
**Name Day**: Ms. Kiperina asked about the test yesterday as she was feeding the fish.

**命名日**：她说已经能基本控制自己的神秘术了，有她帮你做防护，你会更安全。\
**Name Day**: She said she's been able to control her power more now. You'd be much safer with her help.

**命名日**：同一个队伍里的人应该共同承担风险，不是吗？\
**Name Day**: We're a team, right? We sink or swim together.

时针就在这时候走向了整点，小小的身影也及时地从门口探出头。\
As the clock strikes the hour, a small figure peeks in through the door.

**库珀花环**：我刚结束训练——应该还来得及吧，冷周六女士。\
**Kiperina**: My training just finished. I hope I'm not late, Ms. Hissabeth.

**冷周六**：虽然最后的确引发了实验事故，但大伙儿没受什么伤，北方哨歌的神秘术教学很有效，库珀花环也是个好学生。\
**Hissabeth**: Well, we did have a pretty bad accident, but thanks to Kiperina's arcane skill, no one was too badly hurt. Windsong is one cool teacher, and that girl's a phenomenal student.

**冷周六**：定位范围波动太大，这个问题的确有些棘手。在医疗室里躺了几天，我们也吸取了教训……\
**Hissabeth**: The margin of error remained high, a significant problem for sure. But we'd learned our lesson after spending all that time recovering in the ward.

**冷周六**：万一遇上最糟糕的突发情况，还是应该留下什么东西好让其他人处理……呃……遗留问题。\
**Hissabeth**: That is, that we should prepare for the worst, so that those who survive will know what to do with, umm, our legacy.

**冷周六**：这就是电子遗书的重要所在。\
**Hissabeth**: Our last record matters, my friend.

**小蛇Ⅰ**：二号，我觉得指针说的“吸取教训”可能并不是指这件事。\
**Snake I**: Two, I don't think that's what Pointer meant when she told us to "learn from our mistakes."

在冷周六捏住小蛇的嘴巴之前，它就机敏地藏回了头发里。\
Before Hissabeth can pinch its mouth shut, the little snake ducks back into her hair.

**指针**：……\
**Pointer**: ...

**指针**：我必须再次强调，实验安全比一切都重要。\
**Pointer**: Again, I emphasize that safety must come first in the lab. It is my first and most important protocol.

**指针**：我和北方哨歌只是回去取资料，你们就被打包送去急救。\
**Pointer**: Windsong and I left for all of ten minutes, and by the time we got back, each and every one of you ended up on death's door!

**指针**：还有那份延迟撤离的申请书……太荒谬了。\
**Pointer**: And now I find out you've even petitioned for a postponed evacuation. This is getting ridiculous!

**冷周六**：你清楚我们的时间多紧，“暴雨”应急预案不是已经启动了吗？\
**Hissabeth**: You know how tight the schedule is now that the "Storm" Emergency Plan has been activated, don't you?

**冷周六**：但往好处想，我们至少能大致知道还有多少时间，能优化方案，改进软盘。剩下三个月……\
**Hissabeth**: The silver lining is that now we know that we have exactly three months. We can still optimize the procedure and improve the disk and ...

**指针**：够了，西尔维！\
**Pointer**: Enough, Sylvie!

指针用从未有过的严肃语气打断了冷周六的话。\
Pointer cuts her off. Her tone is serious.

**命名日**：如果对计划的进展有疑问，我想大家可以坐下来讨论……\
**Name Day**: Oh, c'mon, friends. Can we just calm down and discuss our schedule over dinner?

**命名日**：或者您有一些好的建议，正急着要告诉大伙儿……\
**Name Day**: I believe Ms. Pointer was only trying to suggest a better plan.

**指针**：我建议现在中止计划。\
**Pointer**: I am. I suggest we stop all work on this project immediately.

这并不在年轻人的意料之内。他一时间找不到合适的措辞来缓和气氛。\
The young man is caught off balance, unable to find the words to ease the tension in the room.

**冷周六**：为什么？我们远远没到要放弃的时候。\
**Hissabeth**: What? Why? The situation really isn't that dire.

**库珀花环**：是的，这……这太突然了，指针女士。那次实验事故真的不算严重……\
**Kiperina**: Ms. Hissabeth is right. We shouldn't be discouraged over one accident, Ms. Pointer. The damage wasn't too severe.

**指针**：还有三个月。而我们最新的进展就是一次事故。\
**Pointer**: Only three months left, yet our latest "achievement" was a total catastrophe.

**指针**：我明白你们认为还能继续尝试，认为成功的概率很大——但那些都只是“预测”。\
**Pointer**: I know what you're all thinking. That the odds are still good, and it's more or less safe to continue. But all that is a weighted gamble.

**指针**：没有任何东西比眼前的生命更重要。\
**Pointer**: Nothing matters more than your lives.

她万分清楚这一点。因为她曾经是最敢于冒险的那部分人。\
She knows this all too well. This is not her first time making bold gambles.

**研究员Ⅰ**：指针，你觉得我们成功的概率有多大？\
**Researcher I**: Pointer, what do you think the odds are really?

**指针**：理论上是七成，在我看来几乎是百分之百。\
**Pointer**: Without diving into the calculations, it's around a 70% chance in theory. But my logic is screaming something else in my ear.

**研究员Ⅱ**：你没必要这么做，指针……\
**Researcher II**: You ... you don't have to take that risk, Pointer.

**指针**：我有分寸，我比任何人都清楚该怎么做。本来就不存在绝对成功的尝试。\
**Pointer**: I know what I'm doing. Nothing's guaranteed in the world of science.

**指针**：我——\
**Pointer**: I ...

她闭了闭眼睛，阻止更多画面继续涌入脑海。\
She closes her eyes, interrupting the playthrough of her memories.

**指针**：我绝对不会同意你们冒这么大的风险。\
**Pointer**: The risk is too high. I can't allow it.

**冷周六**：可是本来就不存在绝对成功的尝试。没有人去试，就永远不会知道结果。\
**Hissabeth**: But it's like we always say: there is nothing guaranteed in the world of science. You never know before you take that fateful step.

说得多么坚定，又多么理所当然的一句话，与当时的指针如出一辙。\
Such a firm, matter-of-fact statement. It sounds exactly like something the old Pointer might have said.

**指针**：但谁来保证计划百分百成功，谁来面对失败的后果？不是进医务室躺几个月、几年，而是——\
**Pointer**: My analysis points to a dangerous level of uncertainty in this project. The price of failure, even optimistically, could be much worse than a few days in recovery. There could be more permanent injuries. You could even ...

“暴雨”。\
The "Storm."

指针环视着所有人，他们都尚未领受过失败的教训，也不该承受那些。\
Pointer scans the room. None of them have known failure—not yet—and they shouldn't have to.

**指针**：那些消失的城市和人，我们都见过太多了。\
**Pointer**: You've seen how things, places, people just disappear in the "Storm."

**指针**：别再继续了。你们还不明白吗？\
**Pointer**: You need to stop this insanity before that happens to us. Don't you understand?

**冷周六**：我的确不知道……究竟有什么问题？\
**Hissabeth**: I really don't. Why should we stop?

她思考片刻，仿佛突然抓住了灵光，对指针点了点头。\
She thinks for a moment, then a spark of inspiration flashes across her face.

**冷周六**：你说得对，牺牲不应该是常态，活着的人才能保证这些研究的存续。\
**Hissabeth**: No, you're right. We shouldn't pretend as if it's normal to risk our lives for this. At the end of the day, if we die, our research dies with us.

**冷周六**：在危险的情况下，你会活下来。我希望你来保管这个故事。\
**Hissabeth**: But if something were to happen to the team, you would be the one to survive. That's why I want you to keep our records, to take down everything in case the worst happens.

**冷周六**：给你。\
**Hissabeth**: Here.

指针低头看着那张数据卡。\
Pointer looks down at the data card.

机械只能忠实地记录与复现数据，无法读出更多的含义，更无法理解人类所谓冲动的选择。\
Machines are only capable of faithfully recording and replaying data. They can't interpret meaning. They certainly cannot understand the reckless choices of human beings.

后来者能草草浏览每位成员的经历，知道他们如何相遇、做出选择、合作，以及分别。\
Those who come after might skim through the logs and learn how the team met, chose, collaborated, and parted ways.

但镜头之外的内容呢？实验室的温度、餐馆招牌菜的滋味，以及她当下的犹豫。没有任何东西能承载这些细节，除了记忆。\
But what about everything outside the frame? The temperature of the lab, the taste of a restaurant's signature dish, the hesitation she feels right now. No device can preserve those details—only memory can.

需要前进的人，也需要留下的人。\
Some need to move forward. Others need to stay behind.

她没有伸出手。再抬起头时，她已经做好了决定。\
She doesn't look up and never reaches for the disk. She's made up her mind.

**指针**：我不会收下数据卡，更不会去提交延迟撤离申请书——我不会帮你们送命。\
**Pointer**: I won't take it, and I won't submit this petition for you. I can't stand by and let you kill yourselves.

**指针**：我要退出计划。\
**Pointer**: I'm done. I quit.

## CO-10 冻雨天 / A Freezing Rain

1987 普列谢茨克分部暴雨前两个月\
1987, Plesetsk2 months before the "Storm"

指针。拉普拉斯科算中心普列谢茨克分部研究员。\
The name is Pointer. Researcher in the LSCC Plesetsk Branch.

加入计划的原因，和退出的原因一样。\
The reason I joined? The same reason I quit.

没有什么比眼前的生命重要。我一直是为了人们能活得更好而做研究。\
Nothing matters more than people's lives. All the research I've done has been for one purpose: to make people's lives better.

**北方哨歌**：你在这儿，指针！最近怎么样？\
**Windsong**: Pointer, there you are! How's everything going?

理线学学者似乎并不介意她的中途离场。每当在分部大楼碰见指针，她都会聊上几句，顺带提及一些航天小组的近况。\
Windsong doesn't mind her quitting. Whenever she runs into Pointer at the branch office, she always stops for a few words, often with updates on the aerospace team.

**北方哨歌**：我听说你正忙着帮相关人员撤离。情况如何？我看米尔内大部分的店铺都关门了。\
**Windsong**: I heard you're busy with the evacuation. Seems many stores in Mirny have already closed up.

**指针**：老样子。等之前的工作交接完了，我就会到米尔内镇上正式开始协助，应该也就是帮忙打包、协调人员、解释情况之类的。\
**Pointer**: As soon as I finish the handover here, I'm heading back into town to help with packing, coordinating, and explaining the situation to the locals. Same old, same old.

**北方哨歌**：我昨天问起冷周六研究情况，她也说是“老样子”。但我看他们进度还不错。\
**Windsong**: "Same old, same old." You know, Hissabeth said that exact thing when I asked about the team's progress yesterday. They seem to be doing alright.

**指针**：是吗。\
**Pointer**: Good.

北方哨歌从大衣里取出一个小袋子，把话题轻巧地拨向了其他方向。\
Windsong takes a small bag out from her coat, nudging the conversation in a lighter direction.

**北方哨歌**：噢，我刚想起来——这里还有点多出来的种子。这次多给你些。\
**Windsong**: Oh, by the way, I've got some seeds left. Do you wanna take them off my hands?

**指针**：……我看起来对园艺感兴趣？\
**Pointer**: Do I look like a gardener to you?

**北方哨歌**：米尔内的驻军和一些民众说，之前有拉普拉斯的研究员给他们送过向日葵种子。\
**Windsong**: Well, it's just that I heard from a few people here in Mirny that a Laplace researcher was giving out sunflower seeds.

**北方哨歌**：我只知道这个人不是我自己，但具体是哪位，也没有什么证据。\
**Windsong**: And it wasn't me, so I've been wondering just who it could have been.

**北方哨歌**：你不需要吗？我看他们很喜欢这份礼物。\
**Windsong**: Don't you want some? Seriously, everyone loves them.

**指针**：……\
**Pointer**: ...

在离开普列谢茨克发射基地的那天，她将花种分发给了沿途碰到的人。\
On the day Pointer left the Plesetsk Cosmodrome, she handed out these seeds to everyone she passed.

当时她是怎么想的？或许是急切地想抛开任何联系，避免自己中途折返。\
What was she thinking? Maybe she just wanted to break all ties, to stop herself from turning back.

她收起了这份礼物，打算在合适的时机再次送出。\
She keeps this bag, saving it for the right moment.

**指针**：多谢。\
**Pointer**: Thanks.

**指针**：说起来，那份延迟撤离申请书，最后是谁提交给路德维希的？\
**Pointer**: So, who ended up signing the application?

**北方哨歌**：冷周六打算在取监测器的时候顺带提交，正好展示她的研究成果。她说这样路德维希同意的概率会大很多。\
**Windsong**: Hissabeth will, when she goes to collect the monitor and report our research to Ludwig. She says it's more likely to get approval that way.

**指针**：他们是彻底不打算中止计划了吗？\
**Pointer**: They don't know when to stop, do they?

**北方哨歌**：我想他们不会放弃的。\
**Windsong**: They don't know the meaning.

**冷周六**：还是放弃吧。\
**Hissabeth**: Stop.

**冷周六**：那些鱼稍稍受了点刺激就不吃东西，你怎么喂也没用。\
**Hissabeth**: If the fish get startled, then they won't eat anything.

**库珀花环**：我明白了，冷周六女士。\
**Kiperina**: I see, Ms. Hissabeth.

但她依然在将鱼食仔细地撒上水面，希望这些脆弱的小生物能多少保留些求生意志。\
She sprinkles the fish food carefully over the water's surface, hoping these fragile little creatures might cling to some instinct to survive.

**命名日**：我刚清点完了剩余的材料，卢恩矿石的损耗比预想中好一些。\
剩下的文件要放到哪里？反面还能当计算稿纸用。\
**Name Day**: I finished a full inventory check. There's more runium left than we thought. Now, where should I put these useless old files? I was thinking we could use them for draft paper.

**冷周六**：如果你能帮我把这些文件变成一把刀，我会很感激你。\
**Hissabeth**: Maybe you can turn them into a knife or something.

**冷周六**：虽然派不上大用场，至少它们还能拿来切切水果。\
**Hissabeth**: A knife would be more useful at this point. You know, to cut fruit or whatever.

**命名日**：这个不行。你桌上废弃的名片可以。\
**Name Day**: Actually, that card there on the table would work better for that.

**冷周六**：有什么特别的？\
**Hissabeth**: Why is that?

**命名日**：材质。金属名片不算常见，它们做武器会比用于自我介绍更好。\
**Name Day**: It's all about the material. Metal makes a better edge than paper. Never quite understood why you made them like that.

**冷周六**：那是我之前研制的新型材料。北方哨歌和指针的名片也都是我做的，受热就会变锋利，在手里捏一会儿能当拆信刀用……\
**Hissabeth**: Oh. I was testing out the new alloy. I used it to make Windsong's and Pointer's cards. It gets harder and sharper when heated. Give it a rub with your hands, and you can use it as a letter opener.

话音在这里停住了。他们尽量不提及指针的离开，试图让一切按照寻常的模样继续。\
Their words trail off. They've been trying not to bring up Pointer's departure, to pretend like everything is still just as it was.

**冷周六**：这个术式不够稳定……要想预设目的地，必须锚定一片区域，或是一个明确的定位点。\
**Hissabeth**: The ritual still isn't stable enough. We need a specific location or area to set as a destination in advance.

**冷周六**：得先确定它能识别的范围。\
**Hissabeth**: But first, we need a way to pinpoint a recognizable area.

**冷周六**：公式是……\
**Hissabeth**: The formula should be ...

**命名日**：北方哨歌女士发了条消息提醒我们记得取监测器。\
**Name Day**: Ms. Windsong sent me a message. She said: "Don't forget to collect the monitor."

**冷周六**：噢，她给大伙儿都发了？替我谢谢她。\
**Hissabeth**: Oh, she sent it to you too? Tell her I said thanks.

**冷周六**：不对……不是这个数。\
**Hissabeth**: No, that number doesn't look right.

**含章鼎**：我尽可能打听过了，你说的神秘学矿物有好几种都相当稀缺，现在没法弄到手。\
**Han Zhang**: I tried my best, but those arcane minerals you were asking for are scarce as all hell! I haven't been able to find a single supplier.

**冷周六**：也行，能弄到更好，没有就算了。\
**Hissabeth**: Then, we'll carry on without them.

**冷周六**：是这个。\
**Hissabeth**: That's it.

**冷周六**：不，完全不对劲。\
**Hissabeth**: Nope. Wrong again.

**冷周六**：计算数据本来是指针拿手的活儿，如果她来算会快很多……\
**Hissabeth**: Pointer was the master of numbers. With that brain of her, she'd have had this over and done by now.

房间角落的声音引着她回过头，远旅正用几块矿石碎屑搭起摇摇晃晃的尖塔。\
A sound from the corner of the room draws her attention. Voyager is stacking pieces of mineral shards into a wobbly tower.

在灯光照耀下，塔尖闪闪发亮，格外引人注目。\
In the lamplight, the peak sparkles, strangely mesmerizing.

**冷周六**：当心别划伤自己了，那些东西看起来没用，但实际威力大得很。\
**Hissabeth**: Careful, don't hurt yourself. They're more powerful than they seem.

看见远旅半知半解地点点头，冷周六回过头来，打算重新想办法对付手里的数据。\
Voyager nods with a vague but accepting gesture, and Hissabeth turns back, ready to refocus on the data.

但微妙的平静一旦被打破，就很难再恢复原状。\
But the fragile silence is broken, and other words spill out.

**库珀花环**：冷周六女士。\
**Kiperina**: Ms. Hissabeth.

照顾完那些鱼，小宇航员走到了冷周六的旁边。她难得主动靠得这么近。\
The little would-be astronaut walks over and stands beside Hissabeth. It's rare for her to approach so closely.

**库珀花环**：我想询问您一个问题……时机也许不太合适。但是它对我非常重要。\
**Kiperina**: I have a question for you. Sorry if it's not a good time, but it's important to me.

**库珀花环**：我希望您能给我确定的、真实的答复。\
**Kiperina**: And it's something I hope you'll answer honestly.

金鱼缸成为了这个突兀话题的无辜受害者。基金会职员慌张地捞起地板上的鱼，为它在旁边找了个新的住处。\
Startled by the coming topic, Name Day broke the fish tank accidentally. He scrambles to scoop up the spilling fish from the floor.

**命名日**：抱歉——冷周六女士，您可以当我不在这儿。我并不知道你们有过什么谈话。\
**Name Day**: Sorry, ladies. Please ignore me. I'm not here, and I didn't hear a thing.

**命名日**：库珀花环小姐很聪明，她猜出任何事都不奇怪，对吗？\
**Name Day**: But if I pay, Ms. Kiperina is a smart young lady. It's hardly surprising that she'd be quick to figure things out, don't you agree?

**冷周六**：……\
**Hissabeth**: ...

冷周六俯视着她，这张仰起的脸很稚嫩，但神情也很坚决。\
Hissabeth looks down at her. The upturned face is young, but so very determined.

**冷周六**：你的问题是？\
**Hissabeth**: So, what's your question?

**库珀花环**：指针女士离开的时候提到过，“那些消失的城市和人，我们都见过太多了”。\
**Kiperina**: Ms. Pointer said something before she left about places and people disappearing into the "Storm."

**库珀花环**：我想，指针女士不是会轻易放弃的人。除非她知道，我们失败的后果远超能够承受的范围。\
**Kiperina**: It's hard to believe that she would ever give up on our mission, unless she knew the price of failing was truly horrible.

**库珀花环**：“暴雨”不只是一场自然灾害，是不是？\
**Kiperina**: Then the "Storm" can't just be some normal kind of natural disaster.

**库珀花环**：“暴雨”是不是会让我们现在生活的地方也消失……？\
**Kiperina**: This "Storm" will destroy everything, won't it?

她抛出了自己压在心底许久的疑惑，冷周六看见她的眼睛像漂亮的玻璃弹珠那样蓄满了光。\
She doesn't even know how long that question has sat in the pit of her chest. In her glass-marble eyes, Hissabeth sees a brightness welling up.

她不知该如何回答，但沉默本身也是一种答案。于是女孩明白了。\
She doesn't know how to respond. But silence can be an answer, too, and the girl understands.

**库珀花环**：我们认识的人也会吗？小熊、鸟儿、这些鱼也都会，对吗？\
**Kiperina**: All the people we know? All the bears, birds, these fish, everything?

**库珀花环**：在我们找回那个失去的“未来”之前，也要面对很多次……很多次的……消失。\
**Kiperina**: The lost future that you talk about, was it the first to disappear? Or are there more that have been lost? Will the same thing happen to our time?

**库珀花环**：它……没有你们描述得那么好。\
**Kiperina**: Things are much worse than you let on.

**库珀花环**：有多少东西改变了？\
**Kiperina**: What else has changed in the future?

女孩眼中的那些光始终没有真正地淌下来。库珀花环很早就明白眼泪的作用相当有限。\
The light in her eyes never fades—not completely. Kiperina has long understood that tears won't change anything.

**冷周六**：太多东西都不如人们想象的长久。\
**Hissabeth**: Many, many things changed. Some things won't last nearly as long as people think they will.

**冷周六**：对你们来说或许是天翻地覆的改变，但生活还在继续。有好事，也有坏事。\
**Hissabeth**: For you, the world might seem to have turned upside down, but life will go on.

麻烦总是接踵而至，指针离开，北方哨歌还有自己的地质勘察任务，而这里正在说话的人都在向她寻求回答。\
Pointer is gone. Windsong has her own geological surveys. Now everyone that's left seems to be looking to Hissabeth for answers.

冷周六尝试斟酌措辞，但她本就没有太多被关照的经验，并不理解要如何安慰他人。\
She tries to choose her words deliberately, but she has hardly ever been comforted, so she doesn't know how to comfort others.

**冷周六**：所以——你决定好要正式加入拉普拉斯了吗？\
**Hissabeth**: So, now that you know what's at stake, are you ready to officially join Laplace?

**冷周六**：只有正式员工才有知情权。在此之前我无法向你透露太多东西。\
**Hissabeth**: I'm afraid there is still a great deal I cannot tell you until then. Many of the answers you're seeking are classified, for employees only.

**命名日**：抱歉，冷周六女士。\
**Name Day**: Pardon me, Ms. Hissabeth.

**命名日**：考虑到库珀花环小姐要执行的任务，她有权知道“暴雨”意味着什么。\
**Name Day**: But given the danger of the mission we are expecting Kiperina to perform, I think she has the right to know what the "Storm" really is.

**库珀花环**：我明白，您不想违反拉普拉斯的规定。\
**Kiperina**: I understand that you don't want to go against Laplace's rules.

**库珀花环**：但我想您可以点头或摇头。\
**Kiperina**: But I'll bet there aren't any rules against me figuring it out and you simply nodding, am I right?

冷周六点头了。于是库珀花环继续说下去。\
Hissabeth nods. So Kiperina goes on.

**库珀花环**：我不会在未来见到科兹洛夫先生，也不会得到那份礼物。\
**Kiperina**: I won't get to see Mr. Kozlov or get that gift in the future.

**库珀花环**：加入拉普拉斯，意味着……我要和乌特恩亚亚的大家彻底告别。\
**Kiperina**: So, if I join Laplace, I won't see anyone from Utrennyaya ever again.

**冷周六**：……\
**Hissabeth**: ...

沉默片刻后，她再次点头。\
She hesitates but at last nods again.

**冷周六**：你可以做选择，像指针那样，我不会强迫你留下。\
**Hissabeth**: The choice is yours. I won't force you to do anything.

**冷周六**：在餐馆碰到你那天，我说可以给你写推荐信，和今天一样都是认真说的。\
**Hissabeth**: Remember the day we first met in the restaurant? I said I would write you a recommendation. I was serious. I still am.

**冷周六**：推荐信我其实已经写好了，以防万一，你后面那位灰白格子也会给你担保证明，北方哨歌也在推荐信上签了名。\
**Hissabeth**: In fact, it's already done. Windsong has signed on to it too, and our Foundation friend behind you is prepared to offer another guarantee just in case.

**冷周六**：你的朋友远旅也会得到推荐。但我们终究没法为所有人解决问题，也没法替任何人做决定。\
**Hissabeth**: We will make a recommendation for your friend Voyager as well, but that's all we can do. I'm afraid we can't protect everyone, nor can we make this decision for you.

**库珀花环**：……\
**Kiperina**: ...

**冷周六**：你要继续吗？\
**Hissabeth**: Do you want to keep going?

她也在问自己同样的问题。\
The question isn't just for Kiperina.

还要继续吗？如果拿回数据，如果数据有用，是不是总有一天所有人都不用再受“暴雨”的困扰？\
If they recover the data—if that data is any good—maybe someday no one will have to worry about the "Storm" ever again.

如果努力拿回的数据只是一堆无用的字符呢？\
But what if they put their lives in jeopardy and gain nothing from it?

**冷周六**：不做尝试就只能被迫接受，试一试至少还有机会改变。\
**Hissabeth**: If you don't, you'll be allowed to return and accept what's to come, but if you join us, there is a chance to change things.

这是她的答案。也只是她自己的答案。\
That is her answer—the only answer she needs to keep going.

**库珀花环**：我……\
**Kiperina**: I ...

## CO-11 偶然的诗 / Poems Come By Chance

沉默是有重量的。当它逐渐累积，终究会像细沙一样没过每个人的咽喉。\
Silence has weight. Like sand piling, layer on layer, on one's chest, eventually it can suffocate.

房间里响起的啜泣声极其微弱，只有两三声，很快就被压灭了。\
The sobs barely register—two or three, snuffed out before they can burst.

**库珀花环**：我会完成这个任务。\
**Kiperina**: I will complete my mission.

她咬字清晰，仿佛立下誓言般郑重。\
She speaks with clarity, as if making a solemn vow.

**库珀花环**：如果我拿到数据，顺利回来，我会考虑加入拉普拉斯。\
**Kiperina**: And if I successfully come back with the data, I'll consider joining Laplace.

**库珀花环**：现在我无法仔细思考该如何选择。所以，请原谅我无法立刻给您答复。\
**Kiperina**: But I can't make a decision now. I need more time to think.

**库珀花环**：但我会继续的，您可以放心。\
**Kiperina**: I will stay until my job is done. You don't have to worry about that.

**库珀花环**：因为这是科兹洛夫先生和大家都希望我做的事……现在也是我唯一能做的事。\
**Kiperina**: That is what Mr. and Mrs. Koslov and my friends in the circus would all want. It is the right thing to do.

**库珀花环**：……\
**Kiperina**: ...

**库珀花环**：我要去训练了，晚些见。\
**Kiperina**: If you'll excuse me, I should return to my training. I'll see you later.

早在尾音落地前，她就迈开了步子，将一整片难捱的沉默抛在身后。\
She's already on the move before the last word is spoken, leaving behind another layer of suffocating silence.

没等上多久，另一个人也尝试着从中脱身。\
It doesn't take long before someone else tries to wriggle out from it, too.

**命名日**：我们也先走了，仓库里还有些材料等着清点，说不定里头有能用的东西。\
**Name Day**: Us too. Need to double-check the warehouse inventory. Might find something useful.

**含章鼎**：昨天不是都收拾好了吗？那些——\
**Han Zhang**: Wait, haven't we done that already? Those—

**命名日**：好了。如果找到什么，我们会列张单子送来的。\
**Name Day**: Alright! We'll let you know if we find anything.

小宇航员和基金会职员先后离开了房间。角落里的少女疑惑地偏过头，努力地比划出几个手势。\
They leave the room one after another. In the corner, Voyager seems entirely unsure of what to do.

**冷周六**：跟他们去忙吧，我还有数据没处理完。\
**Hissabeth**: Join them if you want. I have some unfinished business.

**远旅**：……\
**Voyager**: ...

片刻过后，轻快的身影迈出了房门。\
Moments later, the last light-footed silhouette exits the room.

**远旅**：……\
**Voyager**: ...

熟悉的金色就停留在走廊远处，低下头靠着墙壁。\
The familiar gold glint rests at the far end of the hallway, her head lowered against the wall.

远旅试图跟上同伴的脚步，但很快又犹豫地刹住了步子。\
Voyager tries to approach but hesitates, stopping mid-step.

左右张望，确认过走廊上再没有其他身影，她将小提琴架上肩头。\
She looks around to make sure the hallway is empty, then lifts her violin onto her shoulder.

**远旅**：……\
**Voyager**: ...

**远旅**：……阿涅娅！\
**Voyager**: Alia!

琴音和呼唤绞成一股颤颤的丝弦，让小宇航员回过头来。\
The music strings and her voice twist together like a trembling thread, calling her friend to turn around.

**库珀花环**：是你在叫我吗？\
**Kiperina**: Was that you? Did you just say my name?

**库珀花环**：你学会了——\
**Kiperina**: You learned how to—

在看清那些闪烁的光点后，她骤然间收住了声音。\
As she sees those flickering sparks, her voice falters.

只是短暂的、眨眼间的工夫，眼前的少女又恢复了普通的模样。\
Then, in a heartbeat, Voyager resumes her usual appearance.

**远旅**：星星……很好。\
**Voyager**: Stars ... good.

**远旅**：阿涅娅、开心。\
**Voyager**: Alia, happy.

冷周六久违地独享了整间办公室，却并未如预料中那样顺利地推进工作。\
Hissabeth has the office to herself for once, but the progress she had hoped would come to her is still elusive.

在又一次计算失败后，她撂下了手里的笔，开始重新确定今日目标。\
After yet another failed calculation, she sets her pen down and reconsiders her goals.

**冷周六**：至少今天把所有数据算完。\
**Hissabeth**: These calculations need to be finished today.

**冷周六**：“转念即至”要求施术者默念目标地点，这可以大致理解成是为了校准定位。\
**Hissabeth**: The "Teleport" ritual requires the caster to recite the location. It could be understood as calibrating in a way.

**冷周六**：按照之前的思路想下去，如果从这个阶段入手……\
**Hissabeth**: Let's continue with that thought.

**冷周六**：预设好软盘的目的地，使用口令触发……之前无法稳定传送，或许是因为在过远的距离下，锚定目的地的术式达不到足够的精确度……\
**Hissabeth**: The destination must be preset, and the ritual cast through incantation ... But the further the distance, the harder it is to stay on target.

**冷周六**：如果能有一个独特的、绝对不会被识别错的神秘术反应源用于定位的话……\
**Hissabeth**: If only there were an arcane reaction strong enough and unique enough to calibrate to ...

周遭突兀地静默了一瞬。那台监测神秘术能量反应的仪器发出的警报可称惊天动地。\
It's only then that she notices the strangeness of the moment, which is abruptly broken by the arcane energy monitor as it lets out an ear-splitting alarm.

灼眼的亮光迅速覆盖了整块屏幕，紧接着——更快地熄灭。\
A blinding light flashes across the entire screen, then cuts out.

仪器的监测范围被她有意设置得很窄，最多覆盖到走廊。这个反应源只和她隔着一堵墙。\
The instrument's detection radius is small, barely beyond the nearby hallway.

**冷周六**：——！\
**Hissabeth**: !

因为步子太急，她险些在门口造成一次碰撞事故。\
She narrowly avoids a full-on collision in the doorway.

好在她很快就借着女孩儿的肩膀找回了平衡。\
Luckily, she catches herself using the girl's shoulder.

**库珀花环**：发生什么了？您还好吗，冷周六女士？\
**Kiperina**: What happened? Are you alright, Ms. Hissabeth?

**冷周六**：刚才是你在用神秘术？\
**Hissabeth**: Was that you? Did you cast that arcane skill just now?

**冷周六**：不，这超过了正常情况下绝大多数神秘学家的极限。还有谁和你在一起？\
**Hissabeth**: No, those energy levels were too high for you—beyond most arcanists. Who was with you just now?

**库珀花环**：……还有远旅小姐。\
**Kiperina**: Voyager.

**库珀花环**：她只是为了安慰我——如果她不小心干扰了什么实验，我帮她向您道歉。\
**Kiperina**: She was just trying to make me feel better. Did it interfere with your experiments? I apologize, Ms. Hissabeth. I promise it won't happen again.

**库珀花环**：如果您要找她，我也可以陪您一块儿去。她刚离开不久……\
**Kiperina**: She just left. If you want to find her, I'll go with you.

**冷周六**：你能确定她刚才在你面前用过神秘术，是吗？\
**Hissabeth**: Are you saying she was the one that cast that arcane skill?

**库珀花环**：是的，那是个很漂亮的神秘术。看起来就像……\
**Kiperina**: Yes. It was so pretty. It was like ...

**冷周六**：中子星。\
**Hissabeth**: A neutron star.

这个词显然不在库珀花环的知识范畴里，她疑惑地偏了偏脑袋。\
It's obvious that the concept is beyond Kiperina. She tilts her head expectantly.

**冷周六**：它们中的一些有强磁场，能起导航作用，就是所谓的宇宙灯塔。\
**Hissabeth**: It's a type of highly magnetized star that emits powerful beams that can be traced to show us its precise location. We call them the beacons of space.

**冷周六**：换成神秘术的能量反应也一样！一个足够明亮的反应源，能轻易地被定位！\
**Hissabeth**: Such a strong arcane reaction would be so bright that it'd be trivial to locate even from an extreme distance!

**库珀花环**：我不知道什么是中子星……但我大概明白了您的意思。就像太阳在许多星星里是最显眼的。\
**Kiperina**: I don't know much about space, but it sounds like the difference between finding a star in the sky and looking for the sun.

**库珀花环**：但是宇宙应该很大，或许和其他一些我们还没见过的星星比起来，太阳没有那么明亮……\
**Kiperina**: But then the universe is also very big. I imagine if you were looking from far enough away, even the sun would seem small.

**冷周六**：没错，没错……与整个宇宙比起来，就算是剧烈的神秘术反应也显得微乎其微。\
**Hissabeth**: Damn! I'm afraid you're right. When comparing all the stars in the observable universe, our sun is far from the largest or brightest. Only the closest. We can't assume proximity in our case.

**冷周六**：但是……反过来呢？\
**Hissabeth**: But then, there's still got to be a way, non?

抓住刹那间的灵光，冷周六沿着全新的思路推导。\
Capturing the fleeting aura, she propels a new train of thought forward.

**冷周六**：“暴雨”来临前，神秘术会得到增幅，波动更加剧烈——而不受“暴雨”影响的地方呢？\
**Hissabeth**: Before the "Storm" arrives, the levels of arcane energy in all affected areas will be greatly amplified. But, what about places that won't be affected?

**冷周六**：这个地点也会在监测仪上格外突出，因为它几乎毫无增幅反应。\
**Hissabeth**: Perhaps then, the trick will not be to look for the light in darkness, but for the darkness in the light, like finding a dim bulb in a string of Christmas lights.

冷周六扶住库珀花环的肩膀，郑重地许下承诺。\
Hissabeth places her hands on Kiperina's shoulders and makes a promise.

**冷周六**：我可以试着调整卢恩矿石的使用比例，严格限制软盘的定位范围在普列谢茨克分部附近！\
**Hissabeth**: If that's the case, I can adjust the portion of runium in order to focus the disk precisely on Plesetsk!

**冷周六**：如果这次实验成功——\
**Hissabeth**: If this works out—

**冷周六**：我可以保证，你一定能安全返航。\
**Hissabeth**: Then I guarantee you will arrive home safe and sound.

1987 普列谢茨克分部暴雨前两个月\
1987, Plesetsk2 months before the "Storm"

**指针**：好，我明白了。注意安全，回见。\
**Pointer**: Understood. Take care.

她按掉通讯，向朝自己走来的身影挥了挥手。\
She ends the call and waves at the silhouette walking her way.

**北方哨歌**：在忙什么？\
**Windsong**: What are you up to?

**指针**：和米尔内的驻军联系，他们巡逻时发现了异常的魔精活动。\
**Pointer**: I've been communicating with the garrison in Mirny. They've picked up some abnormal critter activity during their patrols.

**指针**：我稍后会赶过去帮忙，最后一批镇民也要开始撤离了。\
**Pointer**: Another batch of residents is set to evacuate too. I'll head over to help them shortly.

**指针**：你呢，你的地质勘察还顺利吗？打算留在分部躲雨，还是抓紧时间到总部报到？\
**Pointer**: What about you—your geological survey? Are you staying at the branch, or will you head back to HQ?

**北方哨歌**：没找到值得开发的矿藏，我决定再做点努力，应该会踩着最后时间回到这里。\
**Windsong**: Haven't found anything that's worth digging up yet, but I've decided to give it another try. Should be back here in time for the evacuation.

**北方哨歌**：那位小学徒说，等她顺利返回，就会决定是否加入拉普拉斯。我当然要等着好消息。\
**Windsong**: Though I'm hoping to stick around for my little apprentice. She said she'll only give us her decision on joining Laplace once she's back from her mission. I can't wait to hear the good news.

**北方哨歌**：你是彻底打算不再关注这件事了？\
**Windsong**: You still pretending not to care?

**指针**：无论我是否关注都不会影响结果，不过我希望他们能懂得及时放弃。\
**Pointer**: My concern, whether it exists or not, will have no tangible effect on their results. I just hope they don't kill themselves for nothing.

**北方哨歌**：冷周六打算后天进行最后一次传送实验，我会在分部的会议室等她。\
**Windsong**: Hissabeth is planning a final teleportation test the day after tomorrow. I'll be observing from the meeting room.

**北方哨歌**：就是楼上那间最常用的会议室，大概是下午。\
**Windsong**: You know the one we always use upstairs? Early in the afternoon.

**指针**：那时候我应该在米尔内。\
**Pointer**: I'll likely be in Mirny by then.

二人陷入了短暂的沉默。趁这个间隙，北方哨歌敏锐地抓住了下一个话题——人群中显眼的玻璃缸。\
A brief silence follows. In the pause, Windsong deftly shifts the topic to the conspicuous glass tank in the crowd.

**北方哨歌**：嘿，乌尔里希，又见面了。\
**Windsong**: Hey, Ulrich! We meet again.

**北方哨歌**：只是这么一小段时间没碰面，你竟然又憔悴了些！\
**Windsong**: You look even worse than when we last met.

**乌尔里希**：北方哨歌？还有……指针？\
**Ulrich**: Ah, Ms. Windsong? And Pointer?

**乌尔里希**：两位大忙人居然会同时出现在普列谢茨克分部的大厅里。\
**Ulrich**: What have we here, two of our busiest bees working together in the Plesetsk Branch?

指针实在无法理解磁流体“憔悴”的状态从何而来，她读不到对方的表情。于是她只能朝对方点头示意。\
Pointer has no idea why Ulrich looks "even worse." His expression, as ever, is nigh unreadable, so she simply nods to him.

**北方哨歌**：你的人道主义假期何时结束？还来得及去看点有趣的东西吗？\
**Windsong**: So, when is this "humanitarian vacation" of yours over? Any interest in sparing a little time to watch something fun?

**乌尔里希**：如果“有趣的东西”指德米特里他们的聚会，那就免了。\
**Ulrich**: If by "something fun" you mean Dmitry's party, then thanks, but no, thanks.

**北方哨歌**：不不。我应该向你提过的，是冷周六的传送软盘实验。\
**Windsong**: No, not that. I told you about it before—Hissabeth's teleport disk experiment.

**乌尔里希**：哦，这件事——我想起来了。你们要做的事在分部和总部都传开了。\
**Ulrich**: Ah, yes, that one. You know word of it is already spreading through HQ and all the other branches?

**北方哨歌**：怎么说？狠狠夸了一通？\
**Windsong**: And? What's the impression?

**乌尔里希**：我不确定，倒是给他们增添了不少饭后谈资。\
**Ulrich**: I wouldn't categorize it as "good," but it has certainly become a contentious topic.

**北方哨歌**：总还是有支持者，比如露西女士。听说她最近新邀请了一位来自东方的、研究弦理论的科学家去总部。\
**Windsong**: At least one of the bigwigs is supportive—Madam Lucy. It seems she intends to keep our experiment going either way. She even invited a prominent String-Theory Researcher to HQ.

**北方哨歌**：就像我之前说过的那样，有些事的价值不全在于立刻做出成果。\
**Windsong**: As I said, even if we don't get the results we hoped for, the work itself can be illuminating.

始终未发一言的研究员选择在此刻挥了挥手。\
The silent researcher at last offers a wave to attract the attention of the room.

**指针**：抱歉，我还有事，我得先离开了。\
**Pointer**: Excuse me. I have obligations to attend to.

**指针**：下次有机会再聊。\
**Pointer**: Let's talk again later.

她走得很快，磁流体和理线学者目送着迅速变成一枚小黑点的背影。\
She walks off, leaving Ulrich and Windsong to watch her as her figure passes into the hall and away.

几分钟后，理线学者突然发出一声惊呼。\
Several minutes pass, then Windsong gasps.

**北方哨歌**：该死！我没带工牌，现在指针走了——我要怎么搭电梯回实验室？\
**Windsong**: S**t! I forgot my badge, and Pointer's gone. How am I supposed to get back to the lab?

**北方哨歌**：乌尔里希，我得麻烦你多跑一趟。\
**Windsong**: Sorry, Ulrich, do you mind walking me back?

**北方哨歌**：正好你还没回答我，要不要去见证冷周六的实验……\
**Windsong**: By the way, you didn't answer whether you'll be at Hissabeth's experiment.

## CO-12 《协奏曲》 / Concerto

1987 普列谢茨克发射基地暴雨前两个月\
1987, Plesetsk Cosmodrome 2 months before the "Storm"

剧情场景-温室实验室

与平日相比，实验室里并没有太多不同。尽管伙伴们已经尽力将散落的小物件摆放齐整，但显然这种有序性难以得到维持。\
There's not much difference in the lab today. Even though the others had tried to tidy up the clutter, any attempts at organization are doomed to fail here.

冷周六将最后一叠文件推到桌面角落，退后几步打量着自己收拾出的成果。\
Hissabeth pushes the last stack of files to the corner of the table, then steps back to survey her work.

**冷周六**：我准备好了。你们也记得尽量保持安全距离。\
**Hissabeth**: I'm ready. Remember to stay within the safe zone.

**冷周六**：医疗队会在近期撤离，所以我们得尽量小心。\
**Hissabeth**: The medical team is helping with the evacuation, so we need to be extra careful this time.

**库珀花环**：您真的不需要我来做测试人员吗？我的神秘术已经足够熟练了，完全能保护自己。\
**Kiperina**: Miss, are you sure I shouldn't be the one doing this? I've mastered my arcane skill. I'll be able to protect myself.

**冷周六**：当然不能是你，宇航员身上不能有伤疤，它们会因为升空时的高压开裂。\
**Hissabeth**: No, no, no. Look at all the files here. They might give you a paper cut. It's an unacceptable risk for our astronaut. Even the slightest abrasion could explode under the pressure of lift-off.

**冷周六**：放心，这次成功率很高。多次数据核验和模拟都没什么毛病。\
**Hissabeth**: No need for concern. We've done the simulations and cross-checked the data thoroughly.

**冷周六**：以防万一，我今天早上起来还对着软盘读了好几篇露西女士的演讲稿，还有拉普拉斯神秘术科技化应用领域的前沿论文，试图让它做好足够的心理准备。\
**Hissabeth**: To aid in the disk's mental preparation, I even read it Madam Lucy's speech and some Laplace essays on the scientification of arcane skills.

**库珀花环**：可是——\
**Kiperina**: But—

**冷周六**：库珀花环。\
**Hissabeth**: Kiperina.

冷周六很少郑重其事地称呼谁。小宇航员不禁站直了身子。\
Hissabeth's tone is formal, far more serious than she is known for in any other situation. Kiperina's back straightens.

**冷周六**：带其他人撤退到隔离门外面。\
**Hissabeth**: Take the others behind the blast door.

**冷周六**：考虑到场地问题，我会用自己的神秘术给周围做隔热墙，尽力来点预防措施。\
**Hissabeth**: I'll use my arcane skill to protect the field as much as I can.

**冷周六**：毕竟需要实时沟通情况，隔得太远的话通讯信号会被电磁影响，所以你们还是得待在门外。我已经尽可能把风险降到最低啦。\
**Hissabeth**: In order to maintain communication, you'll need to stay behind that door, or else the signal will be disrupted. But with my arcane skill, the risk should be minimal.

**库珀花环**：如果出了什么事，你要怎么办？\
**Kiperina**: What if something goes wrong? What will you do?

**冷周六**：我会管好自己。你得开始熟悉一些流程，总会用得上的。\
**Hissabeth**: I will take care of myself. The only thing I ask is that you pay close attention to what I do.

**冷周六**：除非有谁主动退出，否则出了事就轮流顶上，直到没人能接手。说不定最后全得靠你一个呢？\
**Hissabeth**: Because in the worst-case scenario, if you find yourself out there alone, you'll need to be able to perform this intuitively.

**库珀花环**：我没有那么多经验……\
**Kiperina**: I don't know if I'm ready.

**冷周六**：现在下结论还早，别随便就说做不到啊。\
**Hissabeth**: Maybe, but it's still too early to give up, little astronaut.

她轻轻推了一把小宇航员的肩膀，让她往后退。\
She gives her a gentle push on the shoulder, nudging her back.

自动门开始合拢。\
The automatic door begins to close.

**库珀花环**：但……\
**Kiperina**: But ...

她没有来得及说完话，门扉便彻底关闭。\
She doesn't finish her sentence before the doors shut completely.

剧情场景-温室办公室

**冷周六**：哪来那么多严肃的告别，浪费时间。\
**Hissabeth**: Enough talking. We don't have time for any dramatic farewells.

**冷周六**：桌子上是……谁的工牌？指针走的时候肯定把她的东西全收拾好了。八成是北方哨歌的。\
**Hissabeth**: Wait, whose ID is this? Couldn't be Pointer's. She packs meticulously. Let me guess. Windsong?

她仔细确认了上面的文字。\
She reads the words on the ID, smiling smugly at her confirmation.

**冷周六**：还真是。也不知道她怎么进的分部大楼。\
**Hissabeth**: I knew it. How is she gonna get back into the lab?

启动软盘之前，她把这项意外收获挂在了脖子上。\
Before activating the disk, she hangs the unexpected find around her neck.

**冷周六**：给她来个惊喜。\
