**Hissabeth**: I'll just have to surprise her with it later.

空荡的会议室里，磁流体和理线学者分别占据了大门左右两侧的少部分空间。\
In the empty meeting room, Ulrich and Windsong take up space on opposite sides of the door.

会议桌边的位置并不舒适，谁都不想在闲暇时坐过去。\
No one feels like sitting at the uncomfortable conference table without a good reason.

**乌尔里希**：你对他们有多大把握？\
**Ulrich**: Where would you place their odds?

**乌尔里希**：或者说，按你的评估看，拿回的数据是否真能帮助我们找到“暴雨”的真相？\
**Ulrich**: Perhaps more importantly, is there any guarantee the data they collect will elucidate meaningful truths behind the "Storm"?

**北方哨歌**：这可谁也没法保证。虽然我们是“拉普拉斯科算中心”。\
**Windsong**: You know as well as I do. Laplace hasn't mastered the art of prediction. We don't offer guarantees.

**北方哨歌**：全知全能的拉普拉斯妖究竟把故事读到哪儿了？谁知道呢。\
**Windsong**: Besides, maybe our demon already knows how this all ends, but I'd rather not.

**北方哨歌**：我个人是不喜欢被剧透结局的那一派。\
**Windsong**: Personally, I hate spoilers.

**乌尔里希**：我也是。\
**Ulrich**: As do I.

磁流体耸了耸肩，正打算从最近关注的高新技术中挑选一个有趣的例子延续话题，熟悉的声音却不适时地响起。\
Ulrich shrugs, about to continue the conversation by mentioning a neat bit of tech he's recently looked into, when a strange but familiar voice cuts in.

**监测器**：有人在度假？真悠闲。真悠闲！\
**Monitor**: Slackers? Slackers!

**？？？**：找到他们了。感谢您的努力。\
**???**: Yes, I've found the room. Thank you.

磁流体的发声装置卡壳了片刻才成功喊出声音的归属者。\
Ulrich's voice modulator stutters for a moment before finally spitting out the name.

**乌尔里希**：……阿德勒研究员？\
**Ulrich**: Is that Adler?

**北方哨歌**：路德维希先生？\
**Windsong**: Mr. Ludwig?

理线学者的脸上一片愕然。磁流体的疑惑更明显，它明白地展示了大大的“！”。\
Windsong looks stunned. Ulrich, clearly confused, flashes a giant "!" mark.

停在机器头顶的渡鸦也歪了歪脑袋。\
The raven perched on the monitor's head tilts its own in curiosity.

**“路德维希”**：很高兴听到两位有这样的研究热情。同样感谢你们的努力。\
**"Ludwig"**: I'm glad to see you're so devoted to our research, and I thank you for your hard work.

**“路德维希”**：我来此等候冷周六研究员，并替露西女士转交“暴雨”监测器。\
**"Ludwig"**: I'm here to deliver the "Storm" Monitor on behalf of Madam Lucy.

**“路德维希”**：考虑到实际的物资使用情况，以及时间紧迫，由一个小组对原有的机器进行了必要改造。\
**"Ludwig"**: Given our lack of resources and time, we were forced to modify an existing device to perform as our monitor.

**“路德维希”**：它原本在科算中心承担日程汇报及工作提醒服务。\
**"Ludwig"**: It was originally a robotic assistant, something to set daily schedules and work reminders.

**“路德维希”**：阿德勒研究员的事我有所耳闻。\
**"Ludwig"**: You already noticed Adler's voice. It's synthetic, of course.

**“路德维希”**：出于同事间的人道主义关怀，他们收集了阿德勒曾经的发言数据，合成了语音包，把这台机器送到他的房间门口，试图让他和外界保证一定的社会化接触。\
**"Ludwig"**: His colleagues originally developed this machine for him as a "humanitarian gesture." It was trained to mimic his voice—an attempt to keep him social.

**“路德维希”**：结果是它被“退货”了。因此转往其他方向出力。\
**"Ludwig"**: It ultimately proved ineffective in that role, so now it will serve as our monitor.

**乌尔里希**：我明白。合理利用资源是正确的决定。但我觉得“人道主义关怀”可以有更明确的执行标准。\
**Ulrich**: I understand. Given the circumstances, recycling resources is wise. Though, I struggle to see how a robotic assistant could be a "humanitarian gesture."

**“路德维希”**：感谢理解。露西女士为你提交的休假理由也是“人道主义关怀”，看来你在普列谢茨克分部休养的期间，对这一词汇有了更多了解。\
**"Ludwig"**: Your appreciation is noted. And I supposed you might. In fact, this vacation Madam Lucy sent you on to Plesetsk is a kind of "humanitarian gesture" on her part. Perhaps she hopes you'll gain a deeper understanding of the term.

**乌尔里希**：……\
**Ulrich**: ...

渡鸦显然对这份沉默十分满意，它不再发表任何意见。\
The raven, pleased with the silence, offers no further input.

北方哨歌在监测器的屏幕上点了几下，为自己的新发现露出微笑。\
Windsong taps a few times on the monitor and smiles at her new discovery.

**北方哨歌**：让我瞧瞧这个监测器——可选的语音包还挺多。“钢铁的炼成方案”，我猜这采样自露西女士的会议发言。\
**Windsong**: Mind if I take a closer look? Wow, there are a lot of voice packs programmed into this thing. "How to Temper Steel"—Madam Lucy's voice, I'd bet.

**北方哨歌**：还有那位大明星玛丽莲小姐的。啊，这是斯普特尼克一号的播报语音。\
**Windsong**: And then, what else is here? Sweetheart, the superstar? Oh, and Sputnik-1 too.

**北方哨歌**：“毛绒且温暖的陪伴”？这又是……？\
**Windsong**: "Warm and Fluffy Company," who could that be?

**监测器**：’&#*（&！\
**Monitor**: '%#@&*$#!

**乌尔里希**：他们不该把时间都浪费在这种地方。送上太空的监测器怎么会需要魔精语音包。\
**Ulrich**: What a waste of time! Why would a monitor need a critter's voice in space?

**北方哨歌**：放轻松点，大家总得有办法缓解工作压力嘛。我觉得还挺有意思的。\
**Windsong**: Maybe they just put it in for fun. It could be useful to relieve a little stress.

**北方哨歌**：噢，看来时间刚好。冷周六也准备好了。\
**Windsong**: Oh, perfect timing. Hissabeth has entered the testing grounds.

**冷周六**：现场汇报。我启动了软盘，但它没有反应，猜测是某个部分读数有误。\
**Hissabeth**: Field report. I activated the disk, but it's not working. There must be an error in its incantation.

**冷周六**：噢，提示灯在闪烁，是红灯。这说明它的确有蓄积神秘学能量，并且很可能在按照我限定的范围进行定位校准。\
**Hissabeth**: Oh, the indicator is red, so then it must still be accumulating arcane energy. It may be calibrating its position within the range I set.

**冷周六**：但多出的能量似乎被用在了其他地方，这个术式的耗能是守恒的——所以它很可能会连带我附近的东西一起传送走。\
**Hissabeth**: But what about all this excess energy? I worry it might not just transport me but half the office.

**含章鼎**：……你还有什么想交代的吗？我愿意收养你办公室里能幸存下来的鱼。\
**Han Zhang**: Any last words? If you explode, I call dibs on your fish.

**冷周六**：耐心点，我觉得它在努力了。\
**Hissabeth**: Have some patience. It's doing something.

她甩了甩这枚软盘，但当她停下动作时，软盘依然在轻微地摇晃。\
She shakes the disk once or twice, but when she stops, it continues to tremble—

——剧烈地摇晃。\
—violently.

整间办公室似乎都跟着发起抖来，生态缸里的鱼不安地来回游动。\
The entire office begins to rattle along with it. The fish in the eco-tank dart anxiously.

**冷周六**：哈，很遗憾，我觉得可能不会有幸存的鱼。\
**Hissabeth**: Bad news: I don't think any of those fish are gonna survive.

**冷周六**：祝我一路顺风——！\
**Hissabeth**: Wish me a safe journey!

在会议室的地面开始起伏之前，监测器灵活地退到了走廊上的安全地带。\
Before the floor starts to ripple, the monitor scoots itself out into the hallway for safety.

北方哨歌也猛地贴紧了墙壁，试图稳住身体。抬头时，她发现磁流体的玻璃外壳在震动，内容物摇晃着散开成许多小颗粒。\
Windsong slams her back against the wall to steady herself. Looking up, she sees Ulrich's glass tank vibrating, its contents scattering into tiny particles.

**北方哨歌**：乌尔里希，我简直能听到你头脑风暴的声音——\
**Windsong**: I can hear you brainstorming, Ulrich. It's oddly literal.

**乌尔里希**：……！……，……！\
**Ulrich**: ...! ..., ...!

玻璃破碎声使北方哨歌多瞧了几眼旁边的同事，确认磁流体仍然好端端地待在外壳里。\
The sound of shattering glass immediately has Windsong turn to her colleague, confirming that Ulrich is still secure inside his case.

造成动静的是从半空中坠落的鱼缸，以及——\
The noise appears to have come instead from a fish tank falling and—

**冷周六**：嘿，各位小心！\
**Hissabeth**: Hey, watch out!

**北方哨歌**：我得说实话，冷周六，打个招呼用不上这么大的排场。\
**Windsong**: You know, Hissabeth, there's gentler ways to make an entrance.

**冷周六**：我——听——不——清——！\
**Hissabeth**: I—can't—hear—you!

无论是耳机里还是眼前的话语声都相当模糊，似乎随着空间的移动被撕扯得变形。\
The voices around her, whether in her headset or her ears, are garbled, twisted by the movement of space.

研究员在半空中调整好了姿态，稳当地落在会议桌上。\
Midair, Hissabeth adjusts her posture and lands squarely on the meeting table.

不提那条从石头鱼缸里飞出来的倒霉小鱼，这个见面招呼还算不错。\
Aside from the poor fish that were flung from their stone tank, it isn't the worst entrance.

躺在地板上的鱼有气无力地拍打着尾巴，远不如落在乌尔里希头顶时精神。\
The fish flopping on the floor begin to slow, except the one that has landed fortuitously in Ulrich's tank.

**冷周六**：可怜的鱼，它肯定没救了。就算我在中途把鱼缸变成石棉石，防止玻璃摔破，也没能防住它被甩出来。\
**Hissabeth**: Poor fish. I attempted to turn my aquarium into a fireproof ceramic to keep it safe, but it looks like it just made it easier to shatter.

**冷周六**：嗯……？\
**Hissabeth**: Wait ...

提到自己的神秘术，她慌忙低头查看手里向北方哨歌递出的东西。\
Mention of her arcane skill triggers a panic. She glances down at the object she'd been handing to Windsong.

它的重量显著增加。这应该是拉普拉斯首块拥有石棉石挂带的工牌。\
It's heavier than it should be. This must be Laplace's first ID badge with a ceramic strap.

**冷周六**：糟糕，没反应过来。\
**Hissabeth**: Uh-oh, I forgot about this.

**冷周六**：还好不是重要部分！\
**Hissabeth**: Luckily, it didn't affect the card itself.

她眨了眨眼，让神秘术的辉光完全褪去。\
She blinks, letting the shimmer of her arcane skill fade.

**北方哨歌**：这还挺罕见。我会带着它多走走，让大家瞧个稀奇。\
**Windsong**: That's a unique design. Thanks. It might make for a nice conversation piece.

忙着抢救头顶那只可怜生物的磁流体将小鱼放回鱼缸，直起身子。\
Ulrich is busy saving the poor fish swimming atop his head, dropping it back into the tank.

**乌尔里希**：——恭喜你，冷周六女士。\
**Ulrich**: Congratulations, Ms. Hissabeth.

**乌尔里希**：你的研究成果相当惊人，我必须向你致以真诚的掌声。\
**Ulrich**: Your results appear more than adequate. Indeed, you have exceeded my expectations.

**冷周六**：这么——这么严肃吗？我的确很高兴，不过——总之还是谢谢您。\
**Hissabeth**: Is that stuffy-office talk for a good job? Merci, all the same.

**北方哨歌**：我也得说声恭喜。以及，这是不是说明你能保证让我的小学徒平安回到地球了？\
**Windsong**: Congrats! So, does your success here mean my lovely apprentice has a chance to land back on Mother Earth safely?

**冷周六**：完全可以，虽然这基本上是为了计划临时改进的软盘，还不能推广应用……\
**Hissabeth**: More than a chance now. Though, I'm afraid the adjustments we've made to the process will be impossible to replicate at scale.

**“路德维希”**：但已经足够说服我了。\
**"Ludwig"**: Nonetheless, you've convinced me.

渡鸦乘着它的机械座椅靠近。\
The raven rolls toward them on its mechanical perch.

**“路德维希”**：我同意批准你的延迟撤离申请书。\
**"Ludwig"**: Your application for delayed evacuation is approved.

耳机里的欢呼先一步响起，冷周六还在回想刚刚听到的句子。\
The cheers in Hissabeth's headset reach her before she's finished processing the words.

**冷周六**：但我还……没有把它交给您？\
**Hissabeth**: But I haven't even submitted it yet?

**“路德维希”**：我的意思是，你现在就可以提交它。\
**"Ludwig"**: Well, you may submit it now.

**含章鼎**：所以这就是你带着一张支离破碎的申请书返回的原因？\
**Han Zhang**: So, that's why you're back here with that torn-up application form?

**含章鼎**：我佩服你们竟然能把它重新拼起来！\
**Han Zhang**: I gotta tell you, it's impressive you managed to piece it back together.

众多目光短暂地聚焦在这张薄薄的、由胶带粘合的、几乎难以辨认清原本字迹的纸张上。\
All eyes fall on the thin sheet of paper, held together with tape and barely legible.

**冷周六**：好吧，传送过程中还是不适合携带无防护的纸制品。\
**Hissabeth**: At least I learned something from it: Don't teleport paper products without a protective sheath.

**库珀花环**：没关系，我们离成功很近了。\
**Kiperina**: We seem so close to success.

**库珀花环**：接下来我只需要坚持训练，保持最佳状态，直到发射当天。我明白的。\
**Kiperina**: I will keep training. I need to stay at my best for our launch day.

站在库珀花环身侧的少女轻轻拍了拍库珀花环的肩膀，努力表达自己的意见。\
Voyager taps Kiperina on the shoulder, doing her best to express her opinion.

**库珀花环**：我明白你的意思。我会注意自己的身体状况的。谢谢你，远旅。\
**Kiperina**: I know. I won't push myself too hard. Thanks, Voyager.

**命名日**：也没剩多少时间，你可以适当地多歇一歇。\
**Name Day**: We don't have much time left. Remember to rest too, while you still can.

**命名日**：我建议你为了庆祝这次成功，给自己放个短暂的假期，一天也行。\
**Name Day**: You should take a day off. Consider it a celebration of our successful experiment.

**库珀花环**：我相信冷周六女士会有接下来的安排……还有很多事得忙。\
**Kiperina**: Actually, I believe Ms. Hissabeth already has plans for me. We still have a lot of work to do.

库珀花环向沉思着的研究员投去询问的眼神。\
Kiperina holds her stare on the pondering researcher, expectantly seeking her input.

**冷周六**：安排……我是安排了一些重要事项。\
**Hissabeth**: Plans? Yes, that we do.

**冷周六**：教会你监测器的使用流程，进行发射前的安全检查，确认传送软盘的最终锁定坐标……\
**Hissabeth**: I need to train you to use the monitor. You will have to confirm the final coordinates on the disk and be able to perform the final safety checks before launching.

**冷周六**：噢，对。我这次去取监测器还学到了一个新鲜词，我们也的确有执行它的必要。\
**Hissabeth**: Oh, I think it may be necessary to implement a particular procedure that Ludwig mentioned.

**冷周六**：“人道主义休假”。\
**Hissabeth**: A "humanitarian vacation."

## CO-13 永恒春天的地方 / Where Ever Spring Stays

1987 米尔内镇上暴雨前29小时\
1987, Mirny29 hours before the "Storm"

普列谢茨克镇，米尔内镇，无论叫什么名字，发射基地周围的镇子面貌都十分相近。\
Plesetsk, Mirny—whatever the name, the towns surrounding the Cosmodrome look more or less the same.

它们是为附近的研究基地而建的，也会因研究的中止陷入沉寂。一粒雪在茫茫雪地里并不起眼，它的融化不会有太大的声息。\
They were built to support the nearby research facilities and fall silent along with them. A single snowflake goes unnoticed in the vast white, melting into hot breath.

**指针**：我来吧，这应该是最后几箱物资了。\
**Pointer**: Allow me. These should be the last boxes.

**士兵**：不用，女士。您就告诉我们要搬走哪些就好，大家本来就各有分工嘛。\
**Soldier**: Leave them, miss. Just tell us which ones should be moved, and we'll take care of them. We all got our own jobs to do.

小伙子抢在指针前头弯下腰，动作飞快地把板条箱挨个儿摞进车厢。\
The young soldier bends down ahead of Pointer, loading the boxes into the truck one by one with practiced speed.

指针核对着手里的清单，示意他数量无误。倒数第二批物资的装车宣告结束。\
Pointer checks the list in her hands and gives a nod—correct quantity. The second-to-last batch of supplies is now loaded.

**指针**：你们这些驻军是跟着明天的最后一批人一起走，还是要多留几天？\
**Pointer**: Will you leave with the others tomorrow, or are you staying on until the final evacuation?

**士兵**：上头安排我们明天撤离，回到芝诺在附近的基地。\
**Soldier**: Our orders are to evacuate to Zeno's nearest base tomorrow.

**士兵**：您呢？我前些时候负责的就是普列谢茨克发射场的人员运输工作，那里应该已经全部撤空了。\
**Soldier**: How about you? We were responsible for escorting the last staff members from the Plesetsk Cosmodrome. That place should be empty now, shouldn't it?

**士兵**：您应该比我更清楚，这种大规模的、突发性的撤离行动不常见。\
**Soldier**: An evacuation like this has to be for something big. I'm sure you know better than I do.

**士兵**：早点去安全的地方吧，女士。\
**Soldier**: If you can, miss, find somewhere safe, ASAP.

**指针**：我打算今晚离开米尔内。所有人安全撤离了，我就走。\
**Pointer**: I'm leaving Mirny tonight, just as soon as I help finish with the evacuation.

**指针**：我记得还有几支驻扎在这里的队伍，但没见到那几个熟面孔，他们还好吗？\
**Pointer**: There are fewer troops around now. Have there been any further orders?

**士兵**：有些去清除路上的魔精了，您知道附近最近很有些不安分的魔精。\
**Soldier**: Some were sent to clear the roads. There's been more critters blocking the way lately.

**士兵**：另一些似乎被调去参与更紧急的支援任务，只有我这种新兵留在这儿……\
**Soldier**: I guess the others were assigned to an urgent support mission. So it's just the rookies like me left.

**指针**：撤离行动太危险，的确不该让新人留下。\
**Pointer**: Evacuations can be dangerous. A job like this shouldn't be left to new recruits.

**士兵**：瞧您说的，我倒是嫌这里太安稳——但我得服从命令。\
**Soldier**: You think so? Honestly, I was hoping for a little challenge. But we're soldiers, we follow orders.

他打开车门，伴随着发动机的轰鸣，轮胎下扬起一蓬细密的雪粉。\
The engine roars to life, sending up a small flurry of snow from its undercarriage.

**士兵**：用不用我捎上您？\
**Soldier**: Do you need a lift?

**指针**：不了，我去看看撤离人员情况如何。\
**Pointer**: Thanks, but I'm going back to check on the evacuation. Be safe.

车辆沿着路面碾出的泥泞道路驶远，指针选择了与它相反的方向。她往镇子更深处走去。\
The truck disappears down the slush-covered road carved through the snow. Pointer heads in the opposite direction, further into the town.

**含章鼎**：这就是你选的“人道主义休假”地点？一个矿坑？\
**Han Zhang**: So, this is our "humanitarian vacation" here? An open mining pit?

**冷周六**：当然。\
**Hissabeth**: You've got it.

**冷周六**：足够近，方便出行，没有不选这里的理由。就是来得好像有点早。\
**Hissabeth**: It's nearby and easy to reach. I can't see a reason why we shouldn't come check it out. The only problem is I got the timing a little off.

**冷周六**：等一会儿吧。现在不是极光最明显的时候。\
**Hissabeth**: But just you wait, it won't be long now before the aurora shows up.

她朝矿坑远远地掷去一颗小石子。它飞快地滚进夜色，半点踪影都没留下。\
She tosses a pebble toward the pit. It vanishes into the dark.

**冷周六**：给拉普拉斯和基金会都招揽了新成员，捣鼓出了有点用处的传送软盘，再顺利拿到数据……\
**Hissabeth**: We've recruited a great team from Laplace and the Foundation and worked out the kinks of our teleport disk. If we can just manage to collect some useful data ...

**冷周六**：仔细想想，大伙儿还真是前途光明。\
**Hissabeth**: Our future could be brighter than any aurora.

**命名日**：友情提醒，赌博有风险。\
**Name Day**: I hate to be negative at a time like this, but this is still a big gamble.

**冷周六**：也算赌对了，你不是为了好前途留下的吗？这些总能够你拿个调任通知了。\
**Hissabeth**: But we won big today. Didn't you join us to bring about a better future? Just think, our achievements on this project could pave the way to a promotion or at least a transfer.

**命名日**：别套我的话——这个节骨眼上大家进入坦白环节可不吉利，就像作品里常见的坏结局预警。\
**Name Day**: Don't try to butter me up with promotion talk. Anyway, it's bad luck to talk like that right before a mission. Worse than bad luck—it's cliche.

**命名日**：一群原本不相关的人莫名其妙聚在一起，干一件不被支持的大事，在中途忽然分享自己的过去。\
**Name Day**: Strangers coming together to do great deeds, risking mortal peril for the good of humanity. Now, just before the climax, we'll start talking about our motivations and backstories.

**命名日**：紧接着他们的故事就会急转直下，编剧随机抽取一位倒霉鬼干掉。剩下的人只能回忆永不复返的“最好的日子”。\
**Name Day**: All to give the story a twist: when someone bites it in the last act, and then the whole gang is haunted by their last moments of peace together.

**含章鼎**：这个我懂！有种理论能解释事物的潜在联系，叫什么——对，量子纠缠。\
**Han Zhang**: Oh, there's a theory about that! What is it called again? Right, quantum entanglement.

**含章鼎**：在我老家那边的《易经》里头也有记载，我觉得道理差不多，就是说我们在这里做的事情，总会和远处的另一些事物相关……\
**Han Zhang**: Where I'm from, there's a book called Yijing that has a similar idea, that the things we do are mirrored in faraway places.

转过数个相似的路口，指针终于到达了目的地。\
After turning several near-identical corners, Pointer reaches her destination.

一小撮人聚集在街边，当望见她的瞬间，那些冻得发红的脸庞纷纷露出笑容。\
A small group of people has gathered by the roadside. The moment they spot her, their wind-chapped faces break into smiles.

**指针**：情况怎么样？我过来核对撤离名单。\
**Pointer**: How are things proceeding? I'm here to perform a final check on the evacuation.

**镇民**：辛苦您！我们好着呢，随时可以上车。\
**Resident**: It's going well. We're all ready to leave.

**镇民**：就是可惜了这些花，本来大伙儿想找找办法，看能不能移到别的地方，但周围——您也知道，都是雪地，都冻得结实……\
**Resident**: It's just these flowers. We thought about planting them somewhere, just so we don't need to carry them, but with the soil frozen over ...

**指针**：……花？\
**Pointer**: Flowers?

**镇民**：是啊，您之前给我们的那些种子，原本只是这孩子种着玩，没想到却开出了花。\
**Resident**: Yes, you know, from the seeds you gave us. My daughter planted them just for fun, but they really thrived!

穿着厚衣裳的小姑娘把纸箱费力地抱起来，向指针炫耀她心爱的宝贝。几株向日葵在里面骄傲地昂着头。\
A little girl bundled in thick winter clothes hoists up her box of treasures to Pointer—several tall potted sunflowers.

**孩子**：妈咪说这非常——非常不容易。\
**Child**: Mommy said it's really really difficult.

**孩子**：这是一个奇迹！是我，还有大姐姐你一起做到的！\
**Child**: It's a miracle! Miss, but you and I did it together!

**指针**：是的……你说得对。但是你要带上它们一起走吗？会很重，一路上也会很累……\
**Pointer**: Yes, I suppose it indeed appears miraculous. But how are you going to take them with you? I think it will be a bit too heavy to carry on the road.

**镇民**：其余的我们分了出去，留下这几朵，开得最好，就心想还是多费点工夫带上算了。\
**Resident**: We've given away the rest to some of our neighbors. But these are the ones that bloomed the best. It hurts to think we'd just leave them here to die.

**镇民**：这么冷的天，要讨口饭吃本来就难得很，说要撤离，也不知道能到哪儿去，以后又会怎样。\
**Resident**: It's so cold now, and it's getting hard to find food. We know we have to evacuate soon, but no one has told us where we're going, or what's next.

**镇民**：但您看，您给我们的这些种子，孩子们照料着，竟然真开花了——还开得这么好。\
**Resident**: Despite all the hardship, these seeds you gave us somehow managed to bloom under my daughter's care. Look, they're absolutely radiant!

**镇民**：花草都能努力过活，人又怎么能随便泄气呢？\
**Resident**: If even these little flowers are ready to fight to survive, how can we give up?

周围的镇民附和着，小姑娘越发得意地捧好了自己手里的箱子。\
The townspeople around her chime in, and the girl beams even brighter, holding the box tight in her arms.

**指针**：其实……\
**Pointer**: That's true.

她想劝大家把空间与精力分给其他更重要的行李。\
She wants to tell them to save their space and energy for more important supplies.

这是北方哨歌给她的种子，应当经过神秘术改良，它也许早就习惯了长在冻土上。\
The seeds were a gift from Windsong, likely altered through an arcane skill, perhaps already adapted to grow in permafrost.

但此时此刻，她觉得自己并无权力评判这些花朵之于人们是否有意义。\
But at this moment, it doesn't seem right to judge these flowers that hold meaning for others.

**指针**：谢谢。我没有在这里见过别的花……但它们的确很漂亮。\
**Pointer**: Thank you. I'm not aware of the local species of flowers here, but I'm certain all the same that these are the most beautiful flowers in Mirny.

**指针**：希望它们能和你们一起去其他地方看看。\
**Pointer**: I hope you can find a way to take them with you.

目送着向日葵的那抹金黄逐渐远去，指针重新踏上街道。\
Watching the golden hue of the sunflowers fade into the distance, Pointer steps back onto the street.

她打算检查自己之前停放的车辆，接着简单地巡逻——最后离开，不再回头。\
She will check on the vehicle she parked earlier, take one final patrol, and then leave, without looking back.

而米尔内的确是一个足够小的镇子，意料外的相遇在此时有发生。\
Yet Mirny is, in fact, just large enough for chance encounters to still occur.

**拉普拉斯职员Ⅰ**：嘿——指针？我没看错吧？\
**Laplace Staff Member I**: Hey, am I seeing things? Pointer?

拉普拉斯制服的冷光在雪地里格外不起眼，指针眯了眯眼睛，这才认出前面招手的人影。\
The glint of a Laplace uniform blends into the snow, and she squints until she recognizes the waving figure.

**指针**：你不是还在假期吗？应该不需要参加协助撤离小组才对，怎么也跑这么远？\
**Pointer**: Oh, hey! Weren't you on vacation? Why are you back here with the evacuation team?

**拉普拉斯职员Ⅰ**：我看你们人手也不够，反正闲着也是闲着。\
**Laplace Staff Member I**: Well, I had nothing else to do anyway, and we need all the help we can get.

**拉普拉斯职员Ⅰ**：对了，跟你说个事儿。我前两天才听说路德维希批准了一个小组的延迟撤离申请。\
**Laplace Staff Member I**: Did you hear? There's still a team at Plesetsk. Ludwig even approved a delayed evacuation for them.

**拉普拉斯职员Ⅰ**：真佩服他们，这个节骨眼上竟然有人不想走！\
**Laplace Staff Member I**: I guess they're planning to stay to the very last moment. Can you believe that?

**指针**：路德维希同意了？他们……他们还在发射基地？\
**Pointer**: Ludwig actually approved it? They are going to stay in the Cosmodrome?

这个消息与她预计中的发展截然不同，她惊讶地提高了音量。\
The news is nothing like she expected. Her voice rises in shock.

**拉普拉斯职员Ⅰ**：很不可思议，对吧？不得不说，有勇气的家伙比我想象中要多太多了。\
**Laplace Staff Member I**: Unbelievable, right? That takes a lot of guts. Who would have guessed we had people like that here at Laplace?

**拉普拉斯职员Ⅰ**：你有空可以去发射基地那边问一声，看那群人会不会在这两天改变主意。\
**Laplace Staff Member I**: If you've got time, maybe you should go check on them, see if you can talk some sense into them.

他想拍拍指针的肩膀，考虑到那些机械零件，半途上又缩回了手。\
He aims to pat her shoulder. But considering her mechanical components, he lowers his hand halfway.

**拉普拉斯职员Ⅰ**：行，我还得去挨个儿清点这条街的屋子，先走了！\
**Laplace Staff Member I**: Anyway, I have a street of houses to check one by one for stragglers, so I've got to get back to it.

**拉普拉斯职员Ⅰ**：天这么冷，记得注意检查零件，小心它们冻上——回头平安到了分部，我们再聊！\
**Laplace Staff Member I**: Oh. It's freezing cold out there. Don't forget to check the components. I'll catch up with you when we get back to the branch.

**指针**：……\
**Pointer**: ...

她原以为路德维希会否决这个荒谬的提案，这个牺牲概率远大于成功意义的任务。\
She once hoped that Ludwig would shut down this absurd plan—a mission with far greater odds of failure than achieving any meaningful goal.

但她也早该承认，这群执拗的人为了最终的目标，无论遇到怎样的挫折都不可能放弃。\
But she should've known better. Laplace is filled with the most stubborn people imaginable. They would never give up, no matter how many obstacles stand in their way.

“暴雨”将至，她还能做什么？\
The "Storm" is coming. What else is left for her to do?

指针看向发射基地的方向，只有一片刺目得令人皱眉的雪白。\
Pointer looks in the direction of the Cosmodrome, the buildings obscured by a swirling sheet of white.

**含章鼎**：万物都由原子构成，太行如砺，黄河如带，等是尘埃。\
**Han Zhang**: Everything is made of atoms. From afar, Mount Taihang is like a grindstone, the Yellow River is like a belt, and all these things are but dust.

**含章鼎**：顺着这个概念说，今天我们能聚在这里，完全是偶然……\
**Han Zhang**: In other words, maybe the reason why we're here is only a complete coincidence.

**冷周六**：停，停，把话题拉回来。我对太浪漫的说法过敏。\
**Hissabeth**: Hold it, hold it, let's just get back to the topic at hand. I think I'm allergic to poetry.

**库珀花环**：但他都开头了，可不可以让他继续讲完？我想了解这种说法。\
**Kiperina**: Aww, I want to hear the rest. Would you please let him finish?

**冷周六**：饶了我吧，我真的受不了。我宁愿进入坦白环节，当然，还是先献祭我的队友。请。\
**Hissabeth**: No way. I think I'd rather take a chance on that lethal backstory cliche. How about you start us off?

小蛇们配合地歪过头，众多视线都落到基金会职员身上。\
The little snakes tilt their heads in unison. Every eye lands inquisitively on Name Day.

他敢打赌这是自己最希望挨一记石化神秘术的时刻。\
He almost wishes for a petrification spell to hit himself.

**命名日**：呃，好吧，要问什么？\
**Name Day**: Um, sure. What do you want to know?

**命名日**：怎么误打误撞加入了这支松散又野心勃勃的队伍？\
**Name Day**: Are you curious about why I chose our loose yet ambitious team?

**冷周六**：“松散又野心勃勃”，这几个词挑得挺不错。\
**Hissabeth**: "Loose yet ambitious," that's a good description.

**冷周六**：你自己选的问题，说明你就等着解释这个呢。快点，我懒得听太复杂的说法。\
**Hissabeth**: You brought it up. Now spit it out, and make it simple.

**命名日**：其实也没什么特别的。而且你们提的计划看起来比较有实践价值。\
**Name Day**: Maybe I shouldn't have oversold it. I just think you have a good plan.

**命名日**：万一跟着这群人真能做成大事，一不小心拯救了世界呢——大伙儿都很难抗拒这种念头，对吧？\
**Name Day**: What if this works? What if we do this and it changes the world? And I could be a part of that? It's a tempting thought. Don't you think?

**命名日**：如果可以，我可不想反反复复地看“暴雨”再把哪片熟悉的土地抹掉。\
**Name Day**: I just don't want to see another place I hold dear lost to the "Storm."

**冷周六**：噢。为了家乡？\
**Hissabeth**: So, you mean it was for your hometown?

**命名日**：要这么说也行。\
**Name Day**: Yeah, I guess you could say that.

**库珀花环**：这个时代也有你的家乡吗？\
**Kiperina**: Isn't your homeland still here in this era?

更多时候，库珀花环会选择倾听和等待。她鲜有主动插入对话的时刻。\
More often than not, Kiperina chooses to listen and wait. She seldom inserts herself into conversations.

**库珀花环**：你能接受它们就这么……消失？\
**Kiperina**: Have you just accepted the fact that it will disappear ... again?

基金会职员摇摇头。\
He shakes his head.

**命名日**：这个时代有它自己的图景，和我没太大关系。即使名字相同，消失的东西就是永远消失了。\
**Name Day**: My home isn't in this era. Maybe the names are the same, same old familiar buildings, but nothing that matters to me. What's gone is gone.

**命名日**：不过没事，我有个便携型“故乡”，仅此一份。\
**Name Day**: Don't feel bad for me though. Now, I have my own "portable hometown."

他竖起手指，敲了敲耳边那枚摇摇晃晃的小装饰。\
He raises a finger and taps the little ornament dangling on his ear.

**冷周六**：原来这不是储备金之类的？我一直以为和海盗的金币耳坠差不多，走投无路可以摘下来换路费。\
**Hissabeth**: Hey, I always figured you kept that around in case you needed some quick cash, you know, like those pirates that had coin earrings.

**命名日**：哦，我哥把它打上去的时候说弄丢了就会杀掉我。\
**Name Day**: Oh, no. My brother said he would kill me if I gave this away.

**命名日**：鉴于它的象征意义是“家里最后一个活着的孩子”，假如真丢了，我的家人可能会气得从坟墓里爬出来，如果他们有坟墓。不过必要的时候我肯定会选路费。\
**Name Day**: It's meant to be for "the last living child," a family heirloom of sorts. If I lost it, I think my family would crawl out of their graves and haunt me, if they had graves. Still, if I was in dire need ...

“家人”。这个词唤起了短暂的沉默。\
"Family." The word stirs emotions in all those listening.

小宇航员低下头，试图遮掩自己的表情。\
Kiperina lowers her head, trying to hide her expression.

**远旅**：阿涅娅、家？\
**Voyager**: A-Alia, family?

女孩指了指脚下的地面，她尽可能地用学到的词汇回应，尽管含义可能略有偏差。\
She points to the ground, doing her best to respond with the words she's learned, even if the meaning is slightly off.

**库珀花环**：我的家和家人不在这里，他们在乌特恩亚亚，远旅。\
**Kiperina**: No, Voyager, this is not my family. They're in Utrennyaya.

**库珀花环**：这里的是“朋友”。\
**Kiperina**: These are my friends.

**远旅**：……朋友。\
**Voyager**: Friends.

她知道这个词，但此前一直认为这是专用于形容库珀花环的音节。\
She knows this word, but until now she only used it to describe Kiperina.

对库珀花环而言，这个词则是消解隔阂、卸下防备的标志。\
For Kiperina, it's a word that breaks down barriers and opens doors.

**库珀花环**：就算大家说没关系，说只要有活着的人记住这些就好，对我讲很多道理，我还是没办法想清楚。\
**Kiperina**: You told me that as long as there are living people to remember what has been, that what we're doing will be worthwhile. I've tried to accept that, but I still can't.

**库珀花环**：会消失的不是一片叶子、一杯水、一点微不足道的存在，是我长大的地方和我认识的人……\
**Kiperina**: What has been ... It's not just an old building or some candy in a store. It's the place I grew up and the people I love that will be taken away.

**库珀花环**：——这就是生命里的全部内容。这就是我的生活。\
**Kiperina**: It's everything in my life. It is my life.

**库珀花环**：我知道我应该接受现状，我只是想知道怎么才能——怎么说服自己？\
**Kiperina**: I know I must accept it, that I can do nothing but accept it, but how can I ever accept it?

更长久的沉默。\
Another long silence.

会站在这里的每个人都有一个坚持下去的理由，这理由足以支持他们追逐任何看似荒谬的目标。\
Everyone standing here has a reason to keep going—reasons strong enough to chase the absurd.

换句话说，这里并没有谁知道问题的答案。\
In other words, no one here knows the real answer.

## CO-14 追星星的人 / We Who Chase the Stars

绝大多数情况下，说服自己比说服他人更困难。\
The hardest person to convince is often yourself.

察觉到库珀花环的失落，年轻人还是谨慎地开口了。\
Sensing Kiperina's disappointment, Name Day finally speaks up.

**命名日**：关于这个……\
**Name Day**: About that ...

**冷周六**：我不知道。\
**Hissabeth**: I don't know.

如此直截了当的回答让还在思考措辞的职员险些咬到舌头。\
The blunt reply causes him to bite his tongue and listen.

**冷周六**：我刚听到父母的死讯，就坐上了去拉普拉斯分部的大巴，什么都没来得及想。\
**Hissabeth**: When I heard about my parents' deaths, I was just stepping onto the bus to Laplace. I felt like I had no time to even think about it.

**冷周六**：我以为自己完全接受了事实，对没法改变的事情你能做什么呢？\
**Hissabeth**: I guess I mistook that for acceptance. After all, there's nothing I could do to change it.

**冷周六**：过了两三个月，我写研究日志的时候不小心摔坏了笔。\
**Hissabeth**: Then about three months later, I broke my pen while writing a research log.

**冷周六**：不夸张地说，我哭了整整四十个小时。天哪，感谢当时的舍友没把我拖出门锁在外头。\
**Hissabeth**: I cried for 40 hours. FORTY HOURS. And I'm not exaggerating. I'm grateful my roommate didn't have me committed.

**库珀花环**：那是他们留给你的……？\
**Kiperina**: Was it your parents' pen?

“冷周六会哭”这件事也让她颇感震惊，但她会及时掐断自己不够礼貌的念头。\
The very idea of Hissabeth crying seems almost impossible to imagine. She cuts off the thought before it turns impolite.

**冷周六**：拉普拉斯配发的。如果你需要，每个月都能免费换新，没人会管。\
**Hissabeth**: Nah. Just an ordinary Laplace office pen. They give them out by the box load.

**冷周六**：但以前我在家摔坏了什么东西，会被批评不够小心——接着他们再和我一块儿选新的。\
**Hissabeth**: But back home when I broke something, my parents would tease me for being careless, and then we would find a new one together.

**冷周六**：你根本没法真的说服自己，你只能不去想它，或者找很多理由。\
**Hissabeth**: You can't really accept a thing like this. The only thing you can do is put your pain aside and find something to do with yourself.

**冷周六**：像缠胶带球那样一点点裹起来，当你忙着考虑胶带要怎么卷，其实也就分心了。慢慢地就会看上去好点。\
**Hissabeth**: Even if it's just making a ball of tape. Just wrap a ball, round and round, over and over, until you've forgotten what it even looked like inside.

**库珀花环**：我会试试这个方法。\
**Kiperina**: Maybe that is something I can try.

小宇航员郑重地点头。\
The little astronaut nods solemnly.

**冷周六**：这是过来人的经验之谈。小孩子总爱想这个，弄掉了作业本就会觉得人生到此为止。\
**Hissabeth**: Cool, you should. I'm speaking from my experience. You know, when you're young, everything bad seems like the end of the world. Forgetting your homework might as well be the apocalypse.

的确如此。职员把用于缓和气氛的话都咽了回去。\
She's right. Name Day swallows the words he had meant to use to lighten the mood.

在出发前他听过类似的问题。他也问过自己类似的问题。\
He's heard enough of them before. He's even asked himself the same.

剧情场景-分部储藏间

**阿夫西维**：你要回家看看吗？\
**Avgust**: Are you going home, Mr. Raccoon?

**命名日**：不，只是去出任务。\
**Name Day**: No, I'm heading out for a mission.

**阿夫西维**：维拉说，外边是一个你们都很熟悉的时候。但你们都不打算回去。\
**Avgust**: Vila said it's a time that you're familiar with, but that you didn't ever plan on going back.

**阿夫西维**：我知道维拉住到来亚什基之前也有一个家。你来基金会之前肯定也有。\
**Avgust**: I know Vila had another home before she moved to Rayashki. You must have one too!

**阿夫西维**：那是什么样的地方？也下雪吗？\
**Avgust**: What was it like? Does it snow there?

**命名日**：会下雪。雪把白桦枝干压低，也会把野兔和其他动物的足迹盖住。\
**Name Day**: Yes. It snowed there, so much that it made the trees sag and covered up your footprints as soon as you walked past.

**命名日**：沃尔霍夫河结冰的时候，我和妹妹就砸开冰面钓鱼。\
**Name Day**: When the Volkhov froze over, my sister and I would go and fish from holes we cut in the ice.

**阿夫西维**：帕索诺从冰上掉下去过，他有好几个星期没来上学。\
**Avgust**: Comrade Pasono once fell in the ice doing that. We didn't see him at school for weeks.

**命名日**：确实很危险。\
**Name Day**: Playing on the ice can be dangerous, little Avgust.

传说里溺水的少女会变成鲁萨尔卡。他向维拉验证过，这只是个传说。\
Legend has it that girls who drown become Rusalki. He asked Vila once, and she confirmed it was only a myth.

大部分故事都是如此。在流传的过程里被过度加工。\
Most stories are like that, heavily embellished in the retelling.

为了和仍在思考的小男孩对话，或者为了控制浮起的回忆，他蹲下身，脑袋差不多和那朵向日葵平齐。\
To hold the boy's drifting thoughts or rein in his own memories, he squats down until his head is level with the sunflower.

**命名日**：不过它已经不存在了。虽然还能在地图上找到，但那不一样。\
**Name Day**: But it's all gone now. No matter the era, even if I went back to that little dot on the map, it would never be the same.

**阿夫西维**：我知道。就像来亚什基。\
**Avgust**: Like Rayashki.

**命名日**：……就像来亚什基。\
**Name Day**: Just like Rayashki.

它也只是被“暴雨”剥离了故事的一小块土地。记得的人寥寥无几。\
Another patch of land whose story was lost to the "Storm." Remembered only by the few lucky enough to have lived there.

他试图把话题往回拽，以免对话滑往全然无法应付的方向。\
He tries to pull the topic back before it veers somewhere neither of them can handle.

**命名日**：好好活着，很多事情就会突然在某天得到解决。\
**Name Day**: That is why we must stay alive, then things will work out some day.

**？？？**：列尼亚，活着比什么都重要。\
**???**: Lyonya, stay alive. That's the most important thing.

**？？？**：穿过雪地往我告诉你的方向走，别回头。\
**???**: Keep going. Follow the route I told you. Never look back.

**基金会登记员**：能独立出外勤任务，差不多就能正式入职了，恭喜你。\
**Foundation Registrar**: Being certified as capable for an independent field mission means you're an official Foundation member. Congrats in advance.

**基金会登记员**：大部分人都会在申请书上填个代称，也有少数人用真名，这个随你喜欢。但要改起来比较麻烦，你得好好想。\
**Foundation Registrar**: Most people here use an alias, though it's all up to you. Just make sure you pick a good one. It's not easy to change once it's confirmed.

**列昂尼德**：好的，谢谢您的提醒。\
**Leonid**: I see. Thank you for telling me.

离开家乡的日期与另一个即将被庆祝的日子很接近。\
The day he left home came close to another date soon to be celebrated.

就这个。\
That's it.

他递出了填好的申请书。\
He hands over his application form.

**基金会登记员**：我看看……好，没问题。\
**Foundation Registrar**: Let me check. Alright, no problem.

**基金会登记员**：“暴雨”可给大伙儿添了不少麻烦……眼下正缺人手，之后得加油干活儿啊。\
**Foundation Registrar**: The "Storm" has made everyone's life harder here. The Foundation is always in need of more manpower, and in need of honest men like you even more so.

**基金会登记员**：圣洛夫基金会远东分部欢迎您的加入，命名日先生。\
**Foundation Registrar**: Welcome to the St. Pavlov Foundation Far East Branch, Mr. Name Day.

名字意味着存在。\
A name means existence.

地图上找不到的城市，与地图上同名却截然不同的城市，哪种更不可接受？\
What is hard to accept? Knowing that your city can't be found on any map, or that city still shares its name but has changed entirely.

他尝试过，自己的神秘术并不能对生命体生效，记忆中稍纵即逝的辉光大概只是错觉。\
He's tried before, but his arcane skill doesn't work on living beings. That fleeting glow he remembers is probably just an illusion.

**阿夫西维**：你在想什么？你想家了吗？\
**Avgust**: You're thinking about something. Missing your home again, yes?

**阿夫西维**：没关系。维拉说只要认真上课，学好了知识，在哪里都可以重建我们的家。\
**Avgust**: It's okay. Vila said as long as we pay attention in class and keep learning, we will be able to rebuild Rayashki in the future.

**阿夫西维**：只要每位同志都不忘记！当然，我记得很牢！\
**Avgust**: We will rebuild it as long as each and every comrade keeps that goal in their mind, and I will never forget.

向日葵歪过脑袋。孩子学着自己看过的那样，拍了拍朋友的肩膀，送出一点鼓励。\
The sunflower tilts its head. The boy mimics it, then he pats his friend's shoulder, offering a little encouragement.

**阿夫西维**：加油，浣熊同志。\
**Avgust**: You can do it, Comrade Raccoon.

**命名日**：非常感谢，阿夫西维同志。\
**Name Day**: Thank you very, very much, Comrade Avgust.

在基金会职员被思考绊住的时候，极光已经铺满了天幕。\
Name Day is still lost in thought as the aurora begins to spill across the sky.

它遵循既定的规律，恒常且绚烂，不必依靠某个词语而存在。\
It follows its own patterns, constant and resplendent, existing without the need for names.

自然中并没有围绕人类打造的事物。\
Nothing in nature is made for humanity.

**冷周六**：把最好的位置让给你，来，阿涅娅。\
**Hissabeth**: Come here, Alia. You can have the best seat.

**库珀花环**：其实我已经习惯被叫做库珀花环了。\
**Kiperina**: Oh, I think for now, I'd prefer to be called Kiperina.

她小声咕哝了一句，但还是走到了预留出的位置。\
She mutters something more under her breath but still finds herself sitting in the offered spot.

**冷周六**：抓紧机会，这可是难得的极光爆发。\
**Hissabeth**: Hurry up. You don't get an aurora like this every night.

**冷周六**：——你的神秘术得依靠里面的高能带电粒子。\
**Hissabeth**: You need those charged particles up there for your arcane skill.

**库珀花环**：原来我们不只是出来散心……\
**Kiperina**: I thought we were here for a vacation.

**冷周六**：散心，顺便给你多添一份保障。\
**Hissabeth**: It can be more than one thing. You do need this though.

她找了块合适的石头坐下，顺手帮库珀花环和远旅拍了拍旁边石块上的灰尘。\
She finds a suitable rock to sit on and brushes the dust off the stones beside her for Kiperina and Voyager.

**冷周六**：别太紧张了，在宇宙里散步可比走在钢丝上简单。\
**Hissabeth**: Stay calm. Walking in space is definitely going to be easier than walking a tightrope.

**冷周六**：宇宙中没有绝对的方向之分，下落同时也能是上升。这取决于你使用的参照体系。\
**Hissabeth**: There's no absolute direction up there. Up or down depends on the reference you choose.

**冷周六**：简而言之，只要你愿意这么想，往哪走都一样。\
**Hissabeth**: In short, there's no "falling down."

小宇航员认真地点了点头。\
Kiperina nods seriously.

**库珀花环**：明天，后天……后天我就要去亲眼看一看头顶这些星星了。\
**Kiperina**: Tomorrow, no, the day after tomorrow, I'll be up there drifting above the Earth with the stars.

**库珀花环**：不知道它们摸上去有没有温度。\
**Kiperina**: I wonder if they'll feel warm to the touch.

出于紧张，又或者是因为夜风太冷，她稍微有些发颤。\
Whether from nerves or the night wind, she shivers.

冷周六伸出手，连带着远旅一块儿揽过来，三个人挤成一团。\
Hissabeth opens her arms wide to pull both girls into a huddle.

**库珀花环**：以前天气很冷的时候，我会抱着米莎，就是那只我照料的小熊，跟她一起休息。她身上特别暖和。\
**Kiperina**: The night is so cold. Back with the Utrennyaya, on nights like this, I would sneak into the pens and sleep beside Masha—the bear cub I took care of. She was so warm to cuddle.

**库珀花环**：和现在的感觉很像。抱歉，我并不是想说你们像小动物……\
**Kiperina**: And now I'm here, huddled with all of you. Oh, sorry, I'm not suggesting you remind me of bears.

**库珀花环**：只是这样很安心。\
**Kiperina**: It just feels safe.

**命名日**：我明白，那些格外难捱的冬天，得靠兄弟姐妹们捉几条附近的流浪狗，挤在一块儿取暖。\
**Name Day**: There were times, during the coldest winter nights, that my siblings and I would cuddle up with the stray dogs to keep ourselves warm.

**含章鼎**：我没多少过冬的经验，你们不能直接选择冬眠吗？\
**Han Zhang**: Hold on. You people don't just hibernate through the winter? You're missing out.

从这支小队凑齐以来，他们第一次这样轻松地聊天，谈论与任务无关的内容，提起遥远的过去和生活至今的经历。\
This is the first time their little team has sat together without the mission on their minds, chatting instead about past lives and faraway memories.

不知不觉，一点儿困倦悄然涌上库珀花环的脑袋。\
Before she realizes it, sleepiness sneaks up on Kiperina.

她站起身，试图摆脱这阵突然袭来的疲惫。冷周六也跟着她站了起来。\
She stands to shake off her sudden drowsiness, and Hissabeth rises with her.

**冷周六**：准备回去吧，别让我们的小宇航员累坏了。\
**Hissabeth**: Alright, we should head back. We don't want our little astronaut to be too tired.

**含章鼎**：但你还没说过你为什么要坚持到现在呢，别回避话题！\
**Han Zhang**: Hey, you think I don't see what you're doing? You haven't told us your story yet.

**含章鼎**：我一直都很好奇这个问题，你看起来不像会喜欢数星星的那种人。\
**Han Zhang**: It's been on my mind since I first got here: why would you do all this? You don't strike me as the hopeless dreamer type.

**冷周六**：是吗？好吧，新的刻板印象又多了一种。\
**Hissabeth**: I don't? Well, I should make more of an effort to match the stereotype.

研究员偏了偏头，恰好把打着瞌睡的小蛇托回肩膀上。\
She tilts her head just enough to catch the dozing little snake and nudge it back onto her shoulder.

**冷周六**：为了了解我们自己从何而来，将如何结束。\
**Hissabeth**: It's not so dreamy though. I just wanna know the answers. Where do we come from and how things will end?

**冷周六**：这个理由还不够充分吗？对我而言已经足够。\
**Hissabeth**: What? Not convincing enough?

**冷周六**：或者你想听个更加正式的说法？\
**Hissabeth**: Perhaps you want something more in-depth?

**冷周六**：之前我和指针快被手上的活儿逼疯，就会抽空过来散个心，她通常这么说——\
**Hissabeth**: Way back when, before all this, Pointer and I were being driven mad by work, we would walk out here and there was something she would say to me.

她稍稍眯起眼，饶有兴致地观察着那片绵延的光幕。\
She narrows her eyes, watching the shifting curtains of light with interest.

来自太阳的高能带电粒子，在地球磁场的作用下呈现出肉眼可见的炫目色彩。\
High-energy solar particles, shaped by Earth's magnetic field, dance across the sky in colors visible to the naked eye.

几乎可以听见它们微弱而含混的爆裂声。\
If you listen closely, you might even hear their faint crackling.

**冷周六**：有了语言之后，人就能够描绘宇宙何以至此，又何以终结。\
**Hissabeth**: Language is a tool that permits us to describe how the universe was created and how it will end.

**冷周六**：知晓死亡与短暂，人就开始追求存在的永恒，并思考自身。\
**Hissabeth**: Through it, we reflect on our existence. In order to understand eternity, we must first understand death and impermanence.

轻轻晃了晃脑袋后，她重新找回了平时略微散漫的语气。\
After a small shake of her head, she regains her usual casual tone.

**冷周六**：这可是我学指针说话学得最像的句子——每个见过的同事都这么夸我。\
**Hissabeth**: What do you think? Good impression of her, non? Everyone says it's my best.

天幕上高悬的极光回望着地面的人群。绚丽的光线落下，模糊了雪地与天空的交界，也令每个人的表情都变得朦胧不清。\
The aurora hanging high above the sky shines down at the people below. Brilliant beams fall, blurring the edge between snow and sky and softening every expression into something unreadable.

冷周六的声音像是从远处传来。\
Hissabeth's voice feels like it's coming from far away.

**冷周六**：明天很可能是“暴雨”前的最后一天空闲时间了。对了。你们有没有想过这个问题——\
**Hissabeth**: Tomorrow might be our last free day before the "Storm." I guess it's fitting then to ask the age-old question:

**冷周六**：如果明天是生命中最后一天，该去做点什么？\
**Hissabeth**: If tomorrow was the last day of your life, what would you do?

## CO-15 告别时刻 / Time to Say Goodbye

1987 普列谢茨克发射基地暴雨前17小时\
1987, Plesetsk Cosmodrome 17 hours before the "Storm"

剧情场景-拉普拉斯走廊

小宇航员站在厚重的防护门前，在识别器上按下指纹。\
The little soon-to-be astronaut stands before the heavy blast door and presses her finger against the scanner.

和之前几个月一样，她准时穿过逐渐空荡的走廊，在自己脚步声的陪伴下前往各个训练室。\
Just like several months before, she walks the quiet corridor on the way to her training.

**库珀花环**：只要做好能做的每件事……\
**Kiperina**: Do everything we can, and do my best.

**库珀花环**：就不会为遗憾所困扰。\
**Kiperina**: Leave no regrets.

**库珀花环**：希望今天我也能顺利完成训练任务。\
**Kiperina**: That's why I have to finish my training.

在长久地为一个目标努力之后，越是接近结局，就越是紧张。这是无可避免的正常的情绪反应。\
The closer she gets to the end, the more the nerves take hold.

因此，她尝试着从平稳而熟悉的日常生活中寻找一些慰藉。\
So, she looks for comfort in steady, familiar routines.

一，二，三。\
One, two, three.

她在心里完成了计数，防护门也准时向两侧滑开。\
She finishes her count silently. Right on cue, the blast doors slide open.

失重感令她安心。与模拟操作、神秘术培训和离心力训练相比，这是她最喜欢的项目。\
The weightlessness calms her. Compared to the other simulated operations, arcane skill practice, and centrifuge spins, this is her favorite routine.

走在钢丝上的感觉与此类似，但她眼下不必担心坠落。\
It's like walking a tightrope, but without the fear of falling.

没有了重力限制，似乎可触摸的高度也变得无限，世界像一张柔软的绒毯向周围铺展。\
With gravity out of the picture, the sky itself feels reachable, the world stretching out like a velvet blanket around her.

如果这是我生命中的最后一天。\
If this is the last day of my life,

怎样证明我曾在世界上拥有过生命呢？依靠名字，经历，记忆？\
how can I prove that I was here in this world? With my name, my memories?

我记得，他们这样称呼我。\
I remember what they called me:

阿丽娜·梅德韦杰娃。小熊一样的女孩儿。\
Alina Medvedeva. The girl like a bear.

我们得给你起个在马戏团表演用的名字。\
You must have a proper stage name for your performance.

**科兹洛夫**：“库珀花环”。\
**Mr. Kozlov**: "Kiperina."

**科兹洛夫**：这个名字怎么样？是娜塔莉亚和我一起想的，她最近很迷宇宙探索讲座。\
**Mr. Kozlov**: What do you think? Natalya and I decided on it together. She's a clever one, always reading the latest astrological lectures.

**科兹洛夫**：据说和天上某个由冰构成的小行星带有关，它长得就像甜甜圈或者蛋糕托，应该也像花环……\
**Mr. Kozlov**: It's from a place in the stars. Kuiper, she calls it, some asteroid belt made of ice.

**科兹洛夫**：花环，来自宇宙的礼物！\
**Mr. Kozlov**: This is because, to us, you are a gift from the stars!

她被稳当地抱着，高高举起。对孩子而言这就像飞行。\
He lifts her high, steady and secure. To a child, it feels like flying.

贴近灯泡与帆布构筑的天空。\
So close to a starry sky built from light bulbs and canvas.

科兹洛夫先生……娜塔莉亚女士……\
Mr. Kozlov ... Mrs. Kozlov ...

**娜塔莉亚**：真的连夜就走？我们的时间哪有这么值钱……我们去求一求那位拉普拉斯的女士，就晚一两天撤离，找机会和阿涅娅见一面，也不要紧吧？\
**Natalya Kozlov**: We're leaving tonight? Why all the rush? Let's wait one day later, or maybe two. Why don't we ask that Laplace lady to see Alia again?

**科兹洛夫**：也不好给别人添麻烦。而且这么多人都要走，把整座镇子都撤空了，肯定是因为什么大事。\
**Mr. Kozlov**: I am sure she is too busy. But look, everyone's leaving town! Something must be happening.

他随手指了指远处，街道尽头是安稳而寂静的夜色。\
He gestures to a place out in the distance, the dimly lit Cosmodrome barely visible against the night sky.

**科兹洛夫**：还好我们把阿涅娅提前送到了安全的地方。没听镇上的人说吗？就算世界末日到了，拉普拉斯的大楼也倒不了——\
**Mr. Kozlov**: She'll be safe there. Didn't you hear them say that? Laplace's building will be the last to fall, even if the whole world comes to an end.

**科兹洛夫**：我们努力活久点，你以后多留意来看演出的观众，说不定哪天就看到阿涅娅坐在台下，端端正正的，给你拼命鼓掌。\
**Mr. Kozlov**: What we must do then is keep ourselves safe. That way, some day in the future, we will have the chance to see her again, sitting in the audience, clapping for us, until her hands are red.

**娜塔莉亚**：你说得好听，真就一点也不挂念她？\
**Natalya Kozlov**: My big bear wants to pretend he doesn't have a heart. I know you miss her as much as I do.

**科兹洛夫**：我不是在做规划吗！我们回去把木头牌子修一修，为她多加一个圆圈儿在角落里，就像宇航员的头盔，怎么样？\
**Mr. Kozlov**: Of course, but I must stay in control of myself. Maybe we can put something on the signboard—a circle, like her space helmet.

**科兹洛夫**：乌特恩亚亚的招牌可是从我爷爷那辈就没改过！还是头回破例！\
**Mr. Kozlov**: You know that signboard hasn't been changed since my grandfather was the ringmaster. What a change it will be!

娜塔莉亚正皱着眉对付行李上的绳结，听到这句话，忍不住重新直起身子。\
Natalya frowns as she struggles with the knots on their luggage, but straightens up when she hears the comment.

**娜塔莉亚**：光一个圈儿有什么好看的，就不能照着画册描几颗星星、几艘飞船上去？回了莫斯科，我头一件事就干这个。你记得留个地址，往后好给她寄东西。\
**Natalya Kozlov**: Yes, yes, and we will add some stars and spaceships. I'll paint them on once we're set up in Moscow. Oh, and don't forget to take down their address so we can send things to her.

**科兹洛夫**：留了，留了！阿涅娅走了，你倒是开始琢磨这些零碎事情。以前也不见你们关心小事儿……\
**Mr. Kozlov**: You think I didn't do that the minute we came here? Natalya, you're showing so much concern. What happened to my carefree circus wife?

**娜塔莉亚**：能怎么办呢？事总得有人做。\
**Natalya Kozlov**: It's just that there is nothing else I can do.

她拍了拍手边的包裹，那里面有几只仔细收好的玩偶，和一套清洗干净的演出服。\
She pats the package beside her—a few neatly wrapped dolls and a set of freshly cleaned costumes.

**娜塔莉亚**：大伙儿都不在身边，谁还看顾她，关照她……\
**Natalya Kozlov**: We've always been there for her. Now she's alone and far from us, who will care for her now?

**科兹洛夫**：但我们可没法永远陪着她。\
**Mr. Kozlov**: *sigh* It is how it must be. We cannot be there for her forever.

**科兹洛夫**：这份活计可干不长久。\
**Mr. Kozlov**: You can't do this your whole life.

**科兹洛夫**：来看空中飞人表演的观众，想看到飞行的轻快，也期待看见失手坠落。\
**Mr. Kozlov**: Audiences come to watch an acrobat fly, but they also come to see if they will fall.

**科兹洛夫**：重要的是，走在一根钢丝上，这样的情景在日常生活中基本不存在。\
**Mr. Kozlov**: Most people would never dare to walk on a tightrope.

**科兹洛夫**：马戏团就是贩卖梦想和刺激的营生。\
**Mr. Kozlov**: They pay to see people do the thrilling things that they would never do themselves.

**科兹洛夫**：一辈子吃这口饭可不行。遇到好机会，我还是希望你们能用更安全的法子过活。\
**Mr. Kozlov**: But it is a dangerous business. I often wish that you will one day find a safer way to live than this.

走在地面就是安全的生活吗？\
Is walking on the ground really any safer?

一辈子的时间又是多长呢？\
How long will my life be?

八岁，十岁，十五岁，要往后数到多少才算数？\
Eight years, ten years, 15 years? What's next? When will it end?

**冷周六**：“时间”是不会被数尽的，它只是个概念，有许多种解释方法。\
**Hissabeth**: Time never ends. It's a concept, and there are many explanations for it.

**冷周六**：如果整个宇宙都由粒子构成，那么我们的思维就能够被推算，任何事情的发展也都是如此。\
**Hissabeth**: One suggests that since the whole world is made of particles, including our brains, then our minds too can be calculated, so that everything that's happening or about to happen can be predicted.

**冷周六**：宇宙爆炸的瞬间，一切就被摆放在其中，过去、现在、未来，像一锅奶油饺子汤。\
**Hissabeth**: Past, present, future. All that ever was, and is, and ever will be, was destined from the moment the universe began. Each moment like a knot on a string that's already been tied.

**冷周六**：我们只能沿着线性的时间往前走，就像走在钢丝绳上。\
**Hissabeth**: Our lives just moving along a fixed track from birth to death.

**冷周六**：但如果从“经历即存在”的角度而言，没有发生在当下的事情就都缺少真实感受，近乎不存在。\
**Hissabeth**: Then there is another, the theory that none of this is really happening at all, that all perception is illusion. Only the present exists, and only for as long as we're experiencing it.

**冷周六**：这是两种观点，我更支持前者。\
**Hissabeth**: If you asked me to choose, I prefer the first one.

**库珀花环**：我不太喜欢奶油饺子汤。我还是喜欢正在发生的事。\
**Kiperina**: It's not like a tightrope then. When I walk on the rope, I don't see past and future. I only feel what is happening right now.

**库珀花环**：比如这些光让我的手掌发烫，但很暖和。而石头摸起来是冰冷的。\
**Kiperina**: For example, these lights make my palms feel hot and warm. But the stones beneath me are cold.

**冷周六**：噢，听上去你是支持真实体验的那派。\
**Hissabeth**: Cool, sounds like you favor the second theory.

**冷周六**：不过无论支持哪种观点，都不得不面对一个事实。\
**Hissabeth**: But it doesn't matter which side you're on. There's one thing both have in common.

**冷周六**：——我们的存在其实相当短暂。\
**Hissabeth**: Our existence—whatever you make of it—is just a fleeting moment in time.

**库珀花环**：如果每个人都融入更大的存在，或许就能在时间的绳索上多拥有一些长度。\
**Kiperina**: But those countless moments string together into eternity.

**库珀花环**：我很渺小。乌特恩亚亚会更大一点儿。然后是城市，国家，星球，星系……\
**Kiperina**: I'm small to the universe, just a person, but I'm a part of Utrennyaya, which is bigger than myself. We belong to a people, a country, a planet, and a galaxy.

**库珀花环**：或许，变成一粒能被定位坐标的灰尘，在宇宙中有一个位置，就能和宇宙分享它的永恒。\
**Kiperina**: Maybe that's how we share in eternity, by existing as part of it. Each one of us, no matter how small, takes part in creating the universe.

研究员略感惊讶地睁大眼睛，但很快就恢复到往常愉快的笑容。\
The researcher widens her eyes in brief surprise but just as soon returns to her usual confident and breezy smile.

**冷周六**：对，就是这样。\
**Hissabeth**: You got it.

**冷周六**：宇宙的规律足以说明许多东西。明白它的运转，不需要谎言和奇迹也能活下去。\
**Hissabeth**: When we learn all the rules that govern our universe, we'll be able to predict all that is to come. We'll be able to survive without superstition and fear of the unknown.

活下去。既简单又困难的目标。\
Survive. That's easier said than done.

如果我明天没有成功……\
If we fail tomorrow ...

“暴雨”会把一切都冲刷掉，这些存在都会消失，宇宙里不再有我的坐标。\
The "Storm" will wash away all that we've done here, everything I've ever known.

所有记录都只留在那段录像里，他们可能会把它收藏进某个无人问津的铁皮柜子。\
The only trace of it will be that recording, stuffed away in some dusty cabinet in the Foundation.

——即使这样，我也希望他们提起我的时候，会指一指头顶的天空，然后这样说……\
Even so, I hope one day, when they mention me, they will look up at the sky and say:

“有一位勇敢的小宇航员到过那里。”\
"A brave young astronaut walked among the stars."

无关于科兹洛夫先生对“阿涅娅”的要求，也无关于朋友们对“库珀花环”的期待。\
It's not about Mr. Kozlov's wishes for Alia, nor about her friends' expectations for Kiperina.

这是阿丽娜·梅德韦杰娃自己的选择。\
And she, Alina Medvedeva, made the choice to go herself.

娜塔莉亚回到帐篷里取最后的几箱衣物，科兹洛夫则忙着用麻绳固定行李。\
Natalya returns to the tent to retrieve the last few boxes of clothes, while Mr. Kozlov is busy tightening the ropes on the luggage.

东西实在很多，他努力拽紧绳索，把库珀花环留下的玩偶安全地系在包裹里，随口嘀咕着刚才没讲完的话。\
There's a lot to pack. He tugs hard at the rope, tying the dolls Kiperina left behind safely onto a bundle, muttering the rest of what he didn't get to say earlier.

**科兹洛夫**：孩子们总会长大的，我们也总会死的。给阿涅娅找个更好的去处，也该放心了。\
**Mr. Kozlov**: Children grow up, adults grow old, and then we die, so what's the use in worrying? All that matters is our Alia will be safe.

**指针**：您还在这儿？我以为您会更早些走，越晚越容易遇见麻烦。\
**Pointer**: Mr. Kozlov? You should have already left. The longer you wait to leave, the more dangerous it will be.

科兹洛夫吃了一惊。他并不擅长和研究员们打交道，更没想到会在深夜的街道突然碰面。\
The man is startled. He's not good at dealing with researchers, and he never expected to run into one on the empty streets so late at night.

**科兹洛夫**：难道情况有变动……？这，我们已经收拾好了，立刻就能离开……您看……\
**Mr. Kozlov**: Is-Is there something wrong then? We are ready to go, as-as you can see. We're all packed up.

他局促地指了指身后垒起的箱子，语气近乎恳求。\
He motions to the stacked boxes behind him, his tone on the brink of pleading.

**指针**：没事的，一切照常，您向外面的士兵出示通行证就好。雪一时半会儿不会停，路上得多小心。\
**Pointer**: No. Nothing to be concerned with for now. But we need you to follow the evacuation notice for your safety. Keep your passes with you. You may need to show the soldiers on the road ahead. And please take care. The snowfall is getting heavier.

**科兹洛夫**：那就行，那就行。不过，我能不能再多问一句——\
**Mr. Kozlov**: Sure, sure. But if you don't mind my asking ...

**科兹洛夫**：阿涅娅还好吗？她的身体情况如何，训练表现怎么样？我倒不担心她不够认真，就是怕她努力得过了头……\
**Mr. Kozlov**: Is Alia alright? How is she? How's her training? Sorry, it's just ... I know that she's a good girl, but I'm afraid she'll push herself too much. She's always been so diligent.

**指针**：她一切都好。库珀花环是个很坚韧的孩子，我很佩服她能有这样的意志。\
**Pointer**: You have nothing to worry about. Kiperina is a very disciplined and intelligent young woman. We've been most impressed with her work.

**指针**：我个人认为她在拉普拉斯会有很不错的前途。\
**Pointer**: I believe that she could have a very promising future with Laplace.

中年人脸上的疲惫消退了许多，他找回了一点儿身为团长的得意神采。\
The fatigue on his face eases a bit, and some pride returns to him—the pride of a ringmaster.

**科兹洛夫**：我就知道这孩子能行！\
**Mr. Kozlov**: Promising! I knew it. My Alia is a promising candidate for Laplace!

**科兹洛夫**：刚在摩尔曼斯克捡到她那会儿，她还是个裹在被子里的娃娃。谁知道现在都这么有出息喽……\
**Mr. Kozlov**: *sigh* When we first found her in Murmansk, she was just an orphaned babe. And now, see how wonderful she has become.

**指针**：嗯，时间总是眨眼就过去了。\
**Pointer**: I believe I understand. Time really does fly, doesn't it?

**科兹洛夫**：多亏您肯跟我说说她的情况。我都不好意思去看她，怕打扰她，又怕见个面会舍不得。要是我没忍住哭出来，可就丢人丢大了。\
**Mr. Kozlov**: Thank you for telling me about her. I've wanted to pay her a visit, but I don't want to bother her, and I also don't think she wants to see an old man cry.

**科兹洛夫**：算了，都没事儿了，知道她过得好就行……您忙吧，我不打扰您了。\
不过这时候您怎么还往镇子里边去呢？\
**Mr. Kozlov**: But if you say she is doing well, this is enough for me. But I must ask, miss. Why are you still in town? Aren't you going to be busy with the launch soon?

指针顺着他的目光望向街道尽头，沉沉的夜色里，雪花打着旋儿落下。\
Pointer follows his eyes as he casts a look down the street. Bright fluorescent lights illuminate snow that swirls as it falls.

科兹洛夫肩上的雪无声地融化，指针肩头覆着一层薄薄的白色，像是凝结的时间。\
The snow falls on both of their shoulders. It melts on Mr. Kozlov, but it settles in layers on Pointer's metallic frame.

**指针**：我回来看看有没有落下的东西。\
**Pointer**: I'm here to see if we missed anything.

## CO-16 奶油饺子汤 / What's About Time

1987 米尔内镇上暴雨前14小时\
1987, Mirny14 hours before the "Storm"

灯光冲淡了少许寒意，也为空置的桌椅增添了一点儿生活气息。\
The lighting softens some of the chill, adding a touch of life to the empty tables and chairs.

中年人从柜台后伸出手，推过冒着热气的杯子和盛得满满当当的小瓷碟。\
The owner reaches out from behind the counter, pushing over a steaming cup and a small porcelain plate packed to the brim with gingerbread.

**餐馆老板**：您看这个时间，正好我快收拾好东西，明天就跟车队走了。\
**Restaurant Owner**: Sorry, miss, but we've already packed everything away. I'm leaving on the last truck tomorrow morning.

**餐馆老板**：要是昨天或者今天再早点，我还能请您吃一顿！现在真是找不出啥。\
**Restaurant Owner**: There was still some fresh food around yesterday, but today I've got nothing.

**餐馆老板**：喏，烧壶热水是没什么问题，还有点姜饼，看着填肚子吧。\
**Restaurant Owner**: All I can offer you is a mug of boiled water and some gingerbread.

**指针**：足够了。有吃的就好。\
**Pointer**: That will be enough. Thanks.

小镇的大多数人都已经离开。她这趟过来耽搁得有些晚，只剩这家餐馆还亮了盏灯。\
She got here a little late. This is the last place in town with a light on.

老板翻找半天，凑出一桶泡面和一些自制点心。\
The owner rummages around for a while and manages to find a bucket of instant noodles and some other homemade treats.

她咬了口姜饼，为它的好滋味发出赞叹。\
She bites into a gingerbread cookie, the soothing spice and sweetness lingering on her sensors.

**指针**：很不错。\
**Pointer**: Wow. This gingerbread tastes amazing.

**餐馆老板**：那当然，我家在新莫斯科夫斯克。我和您朋友说过，您不经常来，估计没听到。\
**Restaurant Owner**: You bet. I'm originally from Novomoskovsk. We're famous for it. I think I told your friend the story last time she was here.

**餐馆老板**：好几个朋友都比我走得还远些，去和冻土打交道。我呢，打以前就不擅长对付煤矿。幸好从家里的餐馆学点手艺，也能活下去！\
**Restaurant Owner**: I'm no good with hammers or rocks, but I know food, and the miners always work up a healthy appetite.

**餐馆老板**：但我做姜饼没拉伊莎好。她家是真有过间烘焙工坊。餐馆能开下去，主要也靠我的嘴皮子。\
**Restaurant Owner**: My friend, Raisa, makes much better gingerbread than I do. Sometimes I think the only reason people eat here is for the conversation, heh heh ...

**餐馆老板**：这边比较荒，天也冷，大伙呢也没啥好做的。我就陪大家多聊几句解个闷……\
**Restaurant Owner**: The winter chill keeps everyone huddled inside. So, what else can you do but talk the long nights away?

**指针**：有个人说说话确实很好。不过您怎么留到最后一批才走？\
**Pointer**: It is good to have someone to talk to. Still, I'm curious why you decided to stick around until the last minute.

**餐馆老板**：我也没要紧事。不知道撤离是为啥，但肯定让忙的人和年轻人先走，他们也安全些。\
**Restaurant Owner**: I'm in no rush. No one's bothered to explain why it is we have to evacuate, so I'll let all the young folks with something to live for get out first.

**餐馆老板**：对了，我想和您打听件事……\
**Restaurant Owner**: Could I ask you a question as well?

**指针**：您说吧。不过我也很久没关注外头的情况，不一定清楚。\
**Pointer**: Sure, but I can't guarantee I'll have an answer.

**餐馆老板**：要是您也不知道，我大概是再找不到人问了。拉伊莎在的那个小镇，我忘了名字，但我记得也是个有矿的地方。也有你们这样的大人物过去。\
**Restaurant Owner**: It's only that my friend lived in a town a lot like this, a mining town. They had their own big shots running things there too.

**餐馆老板**：她有两三年没来过信，我想问问看，是出事了，还是像米尔内一样撤空，换了地方？\
**Restaurant Owner**: In her last letter, she told me that those big shots were talking about evacuating them. Then, nothing. It's been years, and I haven't heard from her since.

多么熟悉的描述。\
The description seems eerily familiar.

赶在她说出某个地名之前，老板摇了摇头。\
Before she can say the name of the town, the owner shakes his head.

**餐馆老板**：算了，您要是知道，也不会费劲琢磨这么久。\
**Restaurant Owner**: Forget it, miss. It's a small town. I doubt you or anyone knows what really happened there.

**餐馆老板**：唉，其实我就想知道她是不是还活着……活着就总会碰到的。\
**Restaurant Owner**: *sigh* I often wonder where she is now, or if she's even alive, but I hope that I will see her again some day.

**指针**：……\
**Pointer**: ...

这样的问题注定得不到答案。她想起的那座镇子也已永远消失。\
It's the kind of question that can't be answered. The town she's thinking of no longer exists.

但她相信人需要信念的支撑。为此可以有善意的谎言。\
But she believes people need something to believe in.

**指针**：我确实不清楚。但没见过和这样的小镇有关的伤亡报道。\
**Pointer**: Sorry, I really don't know.

**指针**：很可能也是和米尔内类似的大规模撤离。她说不定也正担心你，安顿下来后或许还能联系上。\
**Pointer**: Perhaps they did evacuate, but relocation can be complicated. It can take years. Maybe you'll hear from her again when she settles down.

**餐馆老板**：好，好，至少我放心些。今晚能睡个好觉。\
**Restaurant Owner**: Yes, that's true. These things take time. Well, at least I can sleep at night.

老板转身继续去收拾他的行李，桌边只剩下她一个人。\
The owner turns back to his packing, leaving her alone.

她打量着这间餐馆。橱柜顶上的花瓶里插着一支稍稍垂头的花儿，色彩金黄。\
She takes a moment to examine the restaurant. In the vase atop the cabinet, a flower droops slightly, its color a bright golden yellow.

**指针**：这儿也有向日葵。\
**Pointer**: Sunflowers.

随意送出的、本以为无用的种子，现在竟在各个角落开出了花朵。\
The seeds given away so casually, like they meant nothing, are now blooming in corners everywhere.

橱柜里还有尚未收起的食材，密封袋和罐头各自占据了一小部分地盘。\
There are still some ingredients on the shelves that haven't been packed, sealed bags and cans each occupying a small space.

**指针**：真空冷冻……苹果。还有……\
**Pointer**: Freeze-dried apples, and ...

指针试图辨认那些包装袋上的字样，但并没取得什么成效。\
She attempts to scan their descriptions, but in the poor lighting, it's a lost cause.

**餐馆老板**：哦，那都还没来得及打包。米尔内这么远，路上又冷，很多食物还没送过来都冻坏了——尤其蔬菜水果之类的东西。所幸有这些配给，不至于路上饿坏。\
**Restaurant Owner**: Oh, I forgot to pack those. It's amazing, isn't it, when you think about it? Even here in the far north, we can get fresh fruit and vegetables.

**餐馆老板**：送货的人说，这些技术都还没普及开，是上过天的技术，只能在米尔内吃到。哈哈，我们也算是享受到高科技了。\
**Restaurant Owner**: I guess this technology was invented to make food for cosmonauts, but now people in Mirny get to enjoy it too! The benefits of science, heh heh.

**餐馆老板**：您如果需要，也可以拿一些走，我带不走太多的。\
**Restaurant Owner**: You can take some if you'd like. I have no room for them.

指针看着橱柜中的食物，一时有些失神。\
Pointer stares at the freeze-dried food on the shelf, momentarily dazed.

此前曾为之努力过的、被认为缺少价值的研究，竟然也在不知不觉中走入了人们的生活。\
The research she once worked hard on, once thought meaningless, had found its way into daily life.

**指针**：没事，我就不用了。您已经帮了我很多忙了。\
**Pointer**: Thank you. I'll be fine with just this. You've actually already helped me out a lot.

她撕开泡面的包装袋。\
She tears open the instant noodle packet.

**指针**：没有蔬菜包，哈……\
**Pointer**: No veggie packets, hah.

**指针**：人倒霉起来还真是走两步路都会摔一跤。几率这么小的事全让我碰见了。\
**Pointer**: Can my day get any worse?

**冷周六**：……所谓的“基础的”“有应用价值”的技术又不会凭空出现。\
**Hissabeth**: They act as if all of their essential and valuable consumer technology just popped up out of nowhere!

**冷周六**：航天工程没有用？随便说个简单的——他们吃泡面会没有蔬菜包！\
**Hissabeth**: To think that aerospace engineering has less to contribute than their other projects?! S**t! They wouldn't even have vegetable packets in their instant noodles without us!

近在身边的事物，坚实可靠、质地清晰。毫无疑问地彰显着存在。\
Things close by, solid and clear in texture. Undeniable proof of existence.

她一向看重真实可感的一切。\
She has always valued what can be felt and touched.

**指针**：搞什么，我从来不信什么占卜、预兆和命运。\
**Pointer**: Come on, pull yourself together, Pointer. We don't buy into karma.

**指针**：该死的巧合。\
**Pointer**: This is only another damn coincidence.

你愿意面对多大的风险？\
What price are you willing to pay for that answer?

**指针**：……\
**Pointer**: ...

这可能是她做过最不理智的决定。\
This might be the most irrational decision she's ever made.

下定决心后，研究员开始和眼前这桶泡面搏斗。\
Having made up her mind, she begins her battle with the bucket of noodles in front of her.

**指针**：一丁点儿菜都没有，真难吃。\
**Pointer**: Tastes awful, hmph.

1987 普列谢茨克发射基地暴雨前13小时\
1987, Plesetsk Cosmodrome 13 hours before the "Storm"

**冷周六**：最后确认。\
**Hissabeth**: Final check.

**冷周六**：飞船的情况？\
**Hissabeth**: Spaceship?

**含章鼎**：完全没问题，每个零件都合乎标准。燃料装载充足，隔热层用你的新材料完全处理过。\
**Han Zhang**: We've run a full diagnostic check. All components are operational. We're fully fueled, and we even installed that new insulation you invented.

**冷周六**：数据监测和通信措施？\
**Hissabeth**: Data monitoring and communication systems?

**命名日**：全部正常。备用方案也检查过了，可以做到三秒内响应。\
**Name Day**: Check. All systems are functional, including the backups.

**冷周六**：人员情况？\
**Hissabeth**: Astronaut status?

**库珀花环**：我检查了神秘术量值、各项数据指标、情绪状况，还有宇航服的状态，全部都很好。\
**Kiperina**: I'm all checked out too. My arcane skill energy level, physical and mental status, and the integrity of my spacesuit are all within your parameters.

**冷周六**：让我想想还有没有漏掉的内容……\
**Hissabeth**: Is there anything else we've missed? Anything at all?

她扫视过每个人，最终让目光停落在满脸好奇的女孩儿身上。\
She scans each person one by one until settling on the girl with curiosity burning in her eyes.

**冷周六**：特聘支援人员兼人道主义关怀员。我刚编的头衔。\
**Hissabeth**: Ah, what about our special humanitarian support staff? Maybe we should give her a check too.

**远旅**：*一段欢快的旋律*\
**Voyager**: *a cheerful tune*

**冷周六**：好，进入自由时间。三小时后准时在发射室门口集合。\
**Hissabeth**: Alright, dismissed. I'll see you at the launch bay doors in three hours.

**冷周六**：有事就用通讯器联络，干活去吧。最后关头才是最得仔细注意的时候。\
**Hissabeth**: Now everyone, cool off a bit. We need to decompress before the action starts. Stay in touch via your communicators. I need everyone frosty. We're in the last mile now.

**冷周六**：我手头也还有些需要检查的内容。\
没办法，人手不够，许多小事儿就得格外上心……\
**Hissabeth**: There are still some things left to be checked through. If only we had more help.

伙伴们陆续离开，冷周六的最后一次检查也宣告结束。\
As the others trickle out, Hissabeth's final inspection comes to an end.

她打开办公桌的抽屉，将那张躺在角落的卡片塞进口袋，关好了房门。\
She opens the drawer of her desk, stuffs the card lying in the corner into her pocket, and locks the door behind her.

积雪被反复踩成泥水，又再次被抹平为白色。指针挑着路走，尽量踩过还未消失的脚印和车辙。\
The snow is trampled into muddy slush again and again, then flattened back into white. Pointer steps carefully, trying to follow footprints and tire tracks that haven't yet been covered.

镇子里已经不再有其他人的声音。失去了最重要的装点，米尔内就只剩冰冷的砖瓦、带有刀痕的木头和沾有污渍的招牌。\
There are no more voices in the town. Stripped of its adornments, Mirny is now cold bricks, scarred wood, and stained signs.

军靴和车轮曾将它的白天与夜晚碾磨踏实，成为一块厚重的绒布。\
Boots and wheels once ground its days and nights into something solid.

马戏团的彩灯、餐馆菜肴的香气、研究员制服的银色和偶尔闪过的灰白格子都曾点缀过它，使它值得被记述。\
The circus lights, the scent of food from the restaurant, the silver of the researchers' uniforms, and the occasional flash of gray plaid—all once decorated it and made it worth remembering.

现在它只是一个镇子，地球上千千万万空荡城镇中的一个。\
Now it is a nameless ghost town, one of countless others.

**指针**：白天的米尔内也这么冷。\
**Pointer**: Mirny is so cold even in the daylight.

**指针**：看这样子，撤离工作还是挺顺利的……\
**Pointer**: At least the evacuation has gone smoothly.

话音刚落，她就注意到不远处店门口的身影。\
No sooner has she said this than she notices a figure near the entrance of a shop.

有哪只慌张闯进镇子的魔精遭了殃。处理它的士兵大概时间不够，就让它的身躯留在了雪地里。\
Some flustered critter had wandered into the town and met its end. The soldiers likely didn't have time to deal with it properly and left its body in the snow.

野狗们嗅着微弱血腥味跋涉而来，尽力享受这顿美餐。\
The wild dogs, drawn by the faint scent of blood, arrive to enjoy a feast.

**指针**：这也算安全隐患啊。\
**Pointer**: Well, that's a security risk.

她估计好了合适的突袭角度，迈开步子。\
She calculates the best angle for a clean attack and starts to move.

**指针**：跑远点，别回来了。我可没精力陪你们玩捕猎游戏。\
**Pointer**: Scamper off and don't come back. I don't have time for another round.

鞋底的血凝成冰渣，她踩过的路面留下一串不算清晰的暗红色脚印。\
The blood on her soles has been mixed with the snow, forming into icy red shards. Behind her, a trail of murky prints leads off across the snow.

就像系在树上指引道路的红布条，这抹红色蜿蜒向昨晚停车的角落。\
Like red ribbons tied to trees marking a trail, this crimson path winds toward where the vehicle had been parked last night.

**指针**：搞不清楚究竟还剩多少时间。\
**Pointer**: I don't really know how much time I have left at all.

**指针**：那个“暴雨”预测也只是靠神秘学能量波动来预估，说不定是其他原因导致的，最后压根没事。\
**Pointer**: These "Storm" predictions are based on fluctuations in arcane energy levels. There's even a chance that this won't be the "Storm" at all, just some kind of arcane phenomenon.

**指针**：先开车过去。路上可别碰见其他意外情况，我不需要什么跌宕起伏的英雄旅程。\
**Pointer**: No matter what the case may be, I can't afford an odyssey at a time like this.

**指针**：——我得尽快赶回发射基地。\
**Pointer**: I have to get to the Cosmodrome, ASAP.

研究员调试着房间里的仪器，小蛇们歪过脑袋，被屏幕上闪烁的提示吸引了绝大部分注意力。\
Hissabeth runs through delicate calibrations of all the equipment in the room. The snakes tilt their heads, thoroughly distracted by the many blinking prompts on the screen.

为了让自己集中精神，冷周六试着将脑内的喧哗变成切实的话语。\
To focus, she tries turning the noise in her head into spoken words.

**冷周六**：靠神秘术波动预估“暴雨”，这方法变量太多，根本不稳定。\
**Hissabeth**: Arcane energy fluctuations aren't a perfect method of predicting the "Storm."

**冷周六**：我真有点担心最后跟踪到的波动都来自那个小姑娘。\
**Hissabeth**: What if all these fluctuations are something else, something like that girl?

**冷周六**：远旅……还是交给基金会发愁吧，她拒绝更多研究，我也不好勉强。\
**Hissabeth**: Voyager, a mysterious girl with unbelievable power. I should let the Foundation handle this. I can't force her to join in an experiment against her will.

**冷周六**：发射室的操作系统也该优化，现在有太多冗余步骤，根本不合道理。\
**Hissabeth**: There are too many redundant steps in the launching system. We need to streamline them if we're going to make our deadline.

她用力按住指纹检测面板，勉强保证了自己的措辞听上去礼貌。\
She presses down firmly on the fingerprint scanner, keeping her tone civil through gritted teeth.

**小蛇Ⅴ**：我想这应该是出于安全考虑吧！\
**Snake V**: Aren't those steps important for safety?

**冷周六**：唉。除了指针，谁还背得下那么厚的操作指南？\
**Hissabeth**: Yeah, yeah, probably, but the process is too complicated. I think Pointer was the only one that ever managed to remember each step in order.

**小蛇Ⅴ**：没人帮你调试系统，你就想起她来啦——\
**Snake V**: Oh, so now you're thinking of her again?

**冷周六**：我只是想要个帮手罢了。她现在肯定在普列谢茨克分部忙自己的事。\
**Hissabeth**: Yeah, whatever. I could use another hand, is all. She's probably still in the branch building, busy with her own stuff.

**冷周六**：再说——\
**Hissabeth**: Besides—

**小蛇Ⅴ**：你听到了吗？\
**Snake V**: Hey, you hear that?

急促的脚步朝着发射室靠近。\
Hurried footsteps approach the launch bay.

**小蛇Ⅴ**：警戒！二号！你可不能让谁来搞破坏！\
**Snake V**: It's an intruder! Hurry, we've got to stop them!

小蛇的嘴巴被捏住，房间安静下来。她分辨着越发迫近的声音。\
The little snake's mouth is pinched shut, and the room falls silent. She listens closely to the increasingly urgent steps.

**冷周六**：没有额外负重，个子偏高，有轻微前倾身体的习惯……\
**Hissabeth**: Effortless steps from a tall figure, with a tendency to lean forward.

**冷周六**：没弄错的话应该是熟人。北方哨歌又落了东西在这儿？\
**Hissabeth**: Sounds familiar. Could it be Windsong? Did she leave something behind again?

冲进房间的身影的确很熟悉。意料之外，情理之中。\
The figure that bursts into the room is unmistakably familiar. Unexpected, yet somehow inevitable.

**冷周六**：——？\
**Hissabeth**: ...?

## CO-17 蛇靠星星证明 / The Measure of a Melusine

研究员还没来得及喘匀气，车辆没法直接开进发射场内圈，最后一小段路她是跑完的。\
Pointer is visibly winded. Her vehicle couldn't drive into the inner perimeter of the launch bay, so she had to run the last stretch.

但她必须抓紧时间，她回到这里就是为了说出自己的想法。\
But she has to make the most of her time. She came back to say what needed to be said.

冷周六比她更快地开口了。\
Hissabeth speaks first.

**冷周六**：你没事吧？怎么看起来像连着熬了好几个通宵似的？\
**Hissabeth**: Are you alright? You look like you haven't slept in days.

**冷周六**：说过多少次，疯狂科学家那一套没什么好处，科研也是体力活——\
**Hissabeth**: How many times have I told you that research requires a healthy body and mind? You need sleep.

**指针**：我……回来……\
**Pointer**: I'm ... here for ...

**冷周六**：最近我应该没做别的，就忙着手上这个要上天的大工程。\
**Hissabeth**: Just so you know, I've got no time to help with whatever you're working on, and we're finishing this project, no matter what you say.

**冷周六**：噢，车我用过，去矿坑附近跑了圈，没人查超载，没吃罚单，顶多油没加满。\
**Hissabeth**: Oh, let me guess. You're here for the car? Yes, I've used it a few times, took the team out to the mine, didn't break anything or get any tickets, but the tank's dry.

每个猜想都绕过了靶心，巧合得像知道正确答案后考出的零分。\
Her every theory misses the mark.

**指针**：和那些都没关系……！\
**Pointer**: It's not about any of that!

**冷周六**：早几天会更安全，你不该选今天。\
**Hissabeth**: Then you should have come earlier—days earlier, not today.

**冷周六**：“暴雨”很可能还有几个小时就会发生，你会来不及开车回分部大楼。\
**Hissabeth**: The "Storm" is due to come in a couple hours. You won't make it to the Northern Branch.

她干脆先沉默，直到调整好呼吸。\
Pointer falls silent for a moment instead, adjusting her breath.

**指针**：我来等着帮你们处理后事，顺便看看你们玩命拿到的数据究竟值不值得。\
**Pointer**: I'm here to settle your affairs. We need to secure your records in case you don't make it, and to see if the work you've done is actually worth your lives.

**指针**：如果你们出事，正好。我把传送软盘改良好，用自己的名义发表论文，给研究成果起名，把你们的名字写在最不起眼的角落。\
**Pointer**: Just so you know, if you don't survive, I'm going to finish our teleport disk and claim all the credit. Maybe I'll write a dissertation on it. I'll call it "Pointer's Teleport Disk," and you'll all just be a footnote, an "et al." in the citations.

**指针**：一定说到做到。\
**Pointer**: You know I'm not bluffing.

**冷周六**：能帮上忙就好。相信他们也不在意——别忘记用通灵板把论文结果告诉我。\
**Hissabeth**: Cool, whatever, Pointer. Just don't forget to tell me the results. Maybe send them to me via Ouija board.

**指针**：……你是在开玩笑吗？\
**Pointer**: Are you being serious?

**冷周六**：你不是认真的，指针？你学会了幽默？原谅我真的一点都没看出来。\
**Hissabeth**: Aren't you? Or are you trying to be funny now? I really can't tell.

她努力维持着的平静语气还是被摧毁了。\
The casual air she fought to maintain finally breaks.

**指针**：我发现没有蔬菜包的泡面太难吃，简直无法容忍！\
**Pointer**: I'm just sick of eating instant noodles without the veggie packets!

**指针**：你也让人无法容忍！\
**Pointer**: But more than that, I'm sick of you and your attitude!

**指针**：别在任何时候都轻描淡写地说所有事！\
**Pointer**: All you do is joke around!

**指针**：吃饭很重要，生死不也很重要吗！\
**Pointer**: If veggies matter that much to a stupid bowl of noodles, how could you think your lives matter any less to me?!

**指针**：说得轻松就能回避结果？少自以为是了！\
**Pointer**: You want to treat your lives like a cosmic joke? Like your deaths won't matter. Well, they will to the ones you leave behind.

在彻底放弃控制音量，也放弃思考后，她的确从冷周六脸上见到了不一样的表情。\
After giving up on controlling her volume and her thoughts, she catches a different expression on Hissabeth's face.

愧疚，悲伤，震惊？都不是。\
Guilt, sadness, shock? None of the above.

研究员只是收起了微笑。\
She has simply put away her smile.

**冷周六**：我明白了。\
**Hissabeth**: I see your point.

**冷周六**：还好我一直在往数据卡里备份研究资料！\
**Hissabeth**: Luckily, I've already made a copy of everything on this data card.

一个更快乐的、发自真心的笑容。\
A brighter, more genuine smile appears.

**冷周六**：我考虑了很久应该把它托付给谁，就算冒着风险把它单独用传送术式送回去，也很可能会有意外和折损。\
**Hissabeth**: I've been wondering who I should trust with it. It's not 100% safe to send back through the teleportation ritual.

**冷周六**：还好你现在回来了。\
**Hissabeth**: It's good to have you back.

薄薄的卡片再次递到她面前。\
The thin card is handed to her again.

**冷周六**：可能缺了一些内容，含章鼎，我记住他叫什么了——还没来得及做完短片剪辑。\
**Hissabeth**: The editing isn't done. Han Zhang—yeah, I can remember his name now—I didn't have time to finish his part.

**冷周六**：不过遗书这种东西也不需要多么漂亮的结尾，对吧？\
**Hissabeth**: But who has time to edit a suicide note?

**冷周六**：要点是，必须托付给一个会认真对待它的人。\
**Hissabeth**: The only thing that matters is that it's in the hands of someone who will take it seriously.

**冷周六**：现在开车回去还来得及。\
**Hissabeth**: Take it and go. You can still make it back.

数据卡有轻微的热度，它大概始终被装在口袋里。\
The data card feels faintly warm. It must have been in her pocket the entire time.

**指针**：开车也来不及，油箱快空了。\
**Pointer**: *sigh* Forget it. You already told me the car's out of gas.

**指针**：让我见识下你们的成果。\
**Pointer**: So, I'll be your witness.

**冷周六**：你决定和我一起死了？\
**Hissabeth**: You sure you wanna die with us, after all?

指针并没有接话，而是靠近了一步。\
Pointer doesn't respond. She just takes a step forward.

**指针**：我只是希望这份电子遗书不会派上用场，至少不是作为遗书派上用场。\
**Pointer**: Call it a fool's wish, but I'm hoping no one is ever going to need to see this.

**指针**：说吧，你把我们的研究完善到了什么程度？\
**Pointer**: Catch me up to speed, what's the status of the project?

**冷周六**：目前只能实现定点传送，而且会造成不可避免的压力，带来眩晕、呕吐，和严重晕车类似——\
**Hissabeth**: We've managed to refine the teleportation to pinpoint a fixed position, but there are still some serious side effects: dizziness, nausea, like the world's worst case of carsickness.

**指针**：无所谓。等我读完研究资料，就会着手解决这些副作用。\
**Pointer**: It'll have to suffice for now. I think I can work that out after I finish reading your progress.

**冷周六**：期待你的好消息！\
**Hissabeth**: Cool, I'll look forward to that.

她指了指门口。\
She points to the door.

**冷周六**：你的实验室谁都没再进去过，也没动过里面的东西。我的实验室倒是变得乱七八糟。\
**Hissabeth**: Your office should be the same as you left it, besides a layer of dust. Be grateful though. You should see the state of mine.

**冷周六**：在这里用传送软盘不太安全，万一你把发射台一起带走，或者哪台机器出了故障，我们就完蛋啦。\
**Hissabeth**: Oh, and don't activate the teleportation anywhere around here. If it takes out the single critical component, we'll be screwed completely.

**指针**：我当然知道。\
**Pointer**: Like I don't know.

**指针**：不需要更多帮手了？我可以留下帮忙。\
**Pointer**: You need a hand here? I can help.

**冷周六**：我以为那天我们已经决定好了分工方式，你留在绝对安全的地方保护资料。\
**Hissabeth**: I thought we already figured out our roles? You need to stay at a safe distance to protect the data.

她难以分辨其中是否有嘲讽的成分。\
She can't quite tell if there's mockery in her words.

但她也不需要对此追根究底。语言就是这样模糊而缥缈，被说出的话都会折损意义。\
But she doesn't need to get to the bottom of it. Language is vague and fleeting. Words lose meaning the moment they're spoken.

**指针**：那就这样。\
**Pointer**: That's it.

临转身前，她顿了顿，顺手将头发别到耳后。\
Before turning around, she pauses and tucks her hair behind her ear.

数据接口与机械装置折射着实验室的冷光。\
Her data ports and mechanical components reflect in the sterile light of the lab.

**指针**：我本以为机器无法忤逆自己的程序。它教导我以保护周围的生命为先。\
**Pointer**: Ha. I always thought I wasn't able to act against my safety programming.

**指针**：但我们还是在这里见面了。\
**Pointer**: Yet here we are.

又是一个少见的表情。指针的数据库得出了分析结果，对方感到惊讶。但这种情绪也并未在冷周六脸上停留太久。\
Another rare expression on Hissabeth's face. Pointer's database logs it as a surprise, but the emotion doesn't linger long.

**冷周六**：你能尝出普通食物的味道？\
**Hissabeth**: Do you have a sense of taste?

指针以为自己的表情数据已经不会再被奇妙的问题干扰。但她的微笑指数依然上升了0.35度。\
Pointer once thought her facial expression metrics could no longer be thrown off by strange inputs. Yet her smile is off its index by 0.35 degrees.

**指针**：我的设计目的之一就是尽可能地仿真。\
**Pointer**: Yeah. I was designed to simulate all aspects of life.

**冷周六**：仿真？谁规定人类和神秘学家是“真实”的标准？\
**Hissabeth**: Really? But whose life? Who decided whether it should be a human's or arcanist's life?

**冷周六**：按他们那套分类，你大概算是“意识唤醒者”，就像乌尔里希研究员和露西女士。\
**Hissabeth**: I suppose you are probably another Awakened arcanist, like Ulrich and Madam Lucy.

**指针**：可能不太一样。不过，还是等事情顺利结束后再说这些吧。\
**Pointer**: Not exactly. But the details can wait.

**指针**：看来多精密的计算也无法准确预估所有事。就像我本以为在这样的时刻，你会鼓励你的朋友。\
**Pointer**: I thought you would be more encouraging at such a vital moment. Guess my prediction matrix is not quite as perfect as I've let on.

**冷周六**：我的确在鼓励你。我在试着证明你的存在性……\
**Hissabeth**: I am encouraging you. I'm trying to prove your existence matters.

面对稍微偏过头、神情疑惑的研究员，指针的微笑指数再次上升。\
Faced with Hissabeth tilting her head in confusion, Pointer's smile registers even higher.

自她离开发射基地以来，这是她最为轻松的一刻。\
Since leaving the Cosmodrome, this is the lightest she's felt.

**指针**：我该走了。多保重。\
**Pointer**: Well, I should go. Take care.

**冷周六**：……好吧，我也得继续做准备，多确认几次情况，保证别出岔子。\
**Hissabeth**: Time for another double-check. Everything needs to be flawless.

这条走廊早就刻在了指针的脑子里，闭着眼都能摸清楚方向。\
This hallway is etched into Pointer's memory. She could navigate it without any sensors.

快到转角时，她听见了呼喊声。\
As she turns, Hissabeth calls out to her.

**冷周六**：——指针！\
**Hissabeth**: Pointer!

**冷周六**：我刚来普列谢茨克的时候，跟你简单解释过我的种族，但那真的很简略！\
**Hissabeth**: You know, I should have mentioned something before, something I wanted you to see.

**冷周六**：吕西尼昂的大街小巷都有关于蛇发女妖的雕像！\
**Hissabeth**: There are Melusine statues everywhere in Lusignan!

**冷周六**：我很早就离开了那里，但我相信它们还在，即使被“暴雨”冲刷也会在那儿，因为它的历史还算长！\
**Hissabeth**: I left a long time ago, but they should still be there. Even the "Storm" can't wash them away. They've been there for ages!

**冷周六**：你可以去看看！\
**Hissabeth**: Go take a look if you ever get the time!

**指针**：去那里根本找不到理由报销差旅费。\
**Pointer**: I don't think Laplace would cover that as a scientific excursion.

她没有停下脚步，也没有回头，只是比了个手势。\
She doesn't stop or turn back, but gives Hissabeth a gesture.

指针。拉普拉斯科算中心普列谢茨克分部研究员，前航天小组成员。\
The name is Pointer. Researcher in LSCC Plesetsk Branch. Former team member on the Space Monitor Project.

退出计划的原因，得有人为坏结局做好准备，帮忙收场。\
The reason I quit? Because someone must be prepared for the worst-case scenario.

另外，那碗面真的很难吃。\
And because I was tired of freeze-dried noodles.

这儿也有两位朋友在进行简单的告别。\
Two other friends have come to say a quiet goodbye.

尽管无法依靠语言交换祝愿，她们还是尽量做着尝试。\
Though they can't quite exchange wishes through speech, they still try.

远旅还不太能控制好这支记号笔。但她写得非常缓慢，非常耐心。\
Voyager struggles to control the marker, but she writes, and Kiperina waits patiently.

手掌上的笔迹组成一个复杂难辨的图形，它的几何构成非常精巧，它的含义也仍旧不可识读。\
The markings on her palm form a complex, indecipherable pattern—precise in geometry, yet unreadable in meaning.

**远旅**：阿涅娅。回家。\
**Voyager**: Alia. Come home.

小宇航员的注意力暂时从图案上离开。她接连来了几次深呼吸，确认自己没有听错。\
The little astronaut pulls her focus away from the pattern. She takes a few deep breaths, just to be sure she heard it right.

**库珀花环**：你居然说了这么长的话！\
**Kiperina**: That was three whole words!

**库珀花环**：如果你能学会更长的句子，就能告诉我你的家乡在哪里了。\
**Kiperina**: Maybe once you learn a few more, you can tell me where you're really from.

**远旅**：……\
**Voyager**: ...

鞋面上增加了微不可察的丁点重量。\
There's a shift of weight on her shoe.

库珀花环低下头，一条小蛇也正抬头瞧她。\
Kiperina lowers her head. A familiar little snake looks back up at her.

**小蛇Ⅷ**：姐姐让我来提醒你，该登上飞船了。\
**Snake VIII**: My sister sent me to tell you it's time.

**小蛇Ⅷ**：别害怕。我们九个都觉得你很厉害。\
**Snake VIII**: And that you shouldn't be afraid. You'll make one cool astronaut, ask any of us.

**库珀花环**：我完全没有害怕。\
**Kiperina**: I'm not afraid.

**库珀花环**：等我回来就给你们做特色果酱。是马戏团里的秘方。\
**Kiperina**: When I return, remind me to show you Natalya's famous jam recipe.

也许是那个图形真有什么奇妙的效果，又或者是对未来平添的几分期待。\
Maybe the pattern really does hold some kind of magic, or maybe it's just the feeling of looking forward to the future.

她的脚步确实轻快了起来。\
But either way, her steps feel lighter.

**库珀花环**：登船检测完毕，没有问题。\
**Kiperina**: Final diagnostics completed.

**库珀花环**：预计一分钟后正式进入发射准备。\
**Kiperina**: We're clear for launch in T-minus one minute.

**库珀花环**：有让人始终保持冷静的好办法吗？\
**Kiperina**: Is there anything else I have to remember?

**冷周六**：有。坚持呼吸。\
**Hissabeth**: Yes: keep breathing.

**库珀花环**：这是一句提醒，还是一个玩笑？\
**Kiperina**: Really, a joke now? Or are you serious?

**冷周六**：算是祝福。\
**Hissabeth**: It can be both things.

**冷周六**：抓紧时间就位。一路顺风。\
**Hissabeth**: Now get ready, and have a safe flight.

通讯结束。冷周六环视过发射室里的每张面孔，同伴们的神色令她稍感放松。\
The transmission ends. Hissabeth scans each face in the launch bay, the confidence in her teammates putting her at ease.

这里没有想要退缩的人。她将手掌覆上那枚按钮。\
She knows that everyone here is committed to the end. She places her hand on the button.

**冷周六**：三。\
**Hissabeth**: Three.

**冷周六**：二。\
**Hissabeth**: Two.

**冷周六**：一。\
**Hissabeth**: One.

**冷周六**：发射。\
**Hissabeth**: Ignition.

## CO-18 墓志铭 / Epitaph

**库珀花环**：高度在上升，一切正常。\
**Kiperina**: Altitude rising. All systems normal.

**冷周六**：好，保持通信。\
**Hissabeth**: Cool. Stay on comms.

她望向舷窗之外，清晰地感受到地面在远离，而天空在迫近。\
She looks out the porthole, watching as the ground falls away and the sky closes in.

恰恰与她从钢丝上摔落时相反。\
It feels like falling in reverse.

宇航员站起身来，按照重复过无数次的训练流程打开储物箱。\
The little astronaut stands up and opens the storage box, following the procedure she has rehearsed countless times.

监测器的摄像头亮起，它愉快地朝前方打了个招呼。\
The monitor's camera lights up.

**监测器**：欢迎来到拉普拉斯。更正，欢迎来到……\
