**Monitor**: Welcome to Laplace! Error, new coordinates detected. Correction: Welcome to ...

**监测器**：数据库未收录该坐标。混蛋，数据错误！混蛋！\
**Monitor**: Location coordinates not found! Reconfirming ... S**t! Location not found! S**t!

**库珀花环**：跳过二次确认流程，载入预设程序。\
**Kiperina**: Cancel the location process. Load preset program.

**库珀花环**：启用“暴雨”监测系统。\
**Kiperina**: Activate the "Storm" surveillance system.

**监测器**：声纹识别通过。信息识别通过。虹膜识别通过。身份已验证，操作权限开放。\
**Monitor**: Voice authorization approved. Iris recognition recognized. Operator identified. Operation access granted.

**监测器**：祝你拥有好运。特别提示，禁止向器械泼洒酒精，否则后果自负。\
**Monitor**: Good luck. Special Warning: Mind all liquids in the vicinity of machinery, especially alcohol!

这点幽默并没有得到回应，它被搁在舱室的地板上，识时务地进入了自检模式。\
The humorous warning gathers no reply. Left on the floor of the cabin, the monitor sensibly begins a diagnostic check on itself.

在宇航员为它扣上安全绳时，它倒没有忘记道谢。\
And when the little astronaut fastens its safety tether, it remembers to say thanks to her.

**库珀花环**：已顺利到达目标位置。\
**Kiperina**: We've reached our target altitude.

**库珀花环**：我将按计划开启舱门，校正星体坐标，投放监测器。\
**Kiperina**: Now, I will open the hatch, adjust the celestial coordinates, and deploy the monitor as planned.

**冷周六**：收到。\
**Hissabeth**: Copy that.

氧气含量充足。倒计时十五分钟。\
Oxygen level sufficient. Countdown at 15 minutes.

**监测器**：记住，轻拿轻放！\
**Monitor**: Excuse me! Please handle me with care!

她尽量扶稳身旁的监测器，拉下把手，在舱门打开前深呼吸。\
She steadies the monitor beside her, pulls the lever, and takes a deep breath before the hatch opens.

一片黑暗。\
Darkness.

没有前后、上下、远近，没有声音和光线。只有隔着航天服传来的坚实触感。\
No forward or backward, no up or down, no sound or light. Only the solid touch that seeps through her spacesuit.

再一次眨眼后，宇宙在她眼前展开，如同……玩具盒子。\
When she blinks again, the universe unfolds before her, like a toy box.

**库珀花环**：——！\
**Kiperina**: ...!

**库珀花环**：……报告，确认观测到“暴雨”影响。\
**Kiperina**: Report, the effects of the "Storm" are now being observed.

没有回应。她不知道自己是否准确传达了这一结果。\
No response. She has no way of knowing if her signal got through.

她感到头晕目眩，也感到自己的心脏就要冲出胸腔。\
She's disoriented, and her heart pounds through her chest.

这些星球以令人恐惧的美丽回报了她的勇气。\
These planets repay her courage with a terrifying kind of beauty.

为她献上掌声。\
Applause, for her.

**监测器**：警告！神秘术波动超过阈值！超过阈值！\
**Monitor**: Warning! Warning! Arcane energy fluctuations approaching safety thresholds!

**监测器**：强光！关上窗户！焊接作业时请戴上护目镜！混蛋！混蛋！\
**Monitor**: Extreme light warning! Close the blinds! Remember to wear your safety goggles when arc welding! S**t! S**t!

意识逐渐远去，躯体变得沉重，紧接着又轻盈地浮起。\
Her consciousness drifts. Her body feels heavy, then lifts again.

轻如一道呼吸。\
Light as a breath.

库珀花环很快从晕眩中找回了平衡。\
Kiperina regains her balance, steadying herself against the dizziness.

周围的景色彻底变了样，变得更加熟悉……也更加难以捉摸。\
The view around her has changed entirely. It feels more familiar and yet even harder to grasp.

**库珀花环**：我……在这里？我还没有启动传送术式……\
**Kiperina**: Why am I here? I haven't activated the teleportation ritual yet.

**库珀花环**：难道任务已经结束了……？\
**Kiperina**: Is the mission over?

她转过头，自己的手中牵着一个可笑的小东西。\
She turns her head. In her hand, she's holding something strange and almost silly.

**玩偶**：‘@#%￥！&#%！\
**Doll**: ‘@#%￥！&#%！

**库珀花环**：我听不懂您想说什么！请重复一遍——\
**Kiperina**: I don't understand! Please repeat!

**库珀花环**：请重复一遍，您说的几乎是一串乱码——\
**Kiperina**: Please repeat! I can't understand what's going on.

**监测器**：危险！波动已严重超过阈值！危险！\
**Monitor**: Warning! Energy fluctuations are now exceeding safety thresholds!

**含章鼎**：通讯信号被干扰了，她没有回复！\
**Han Zhang**: There's too much interference in the signal. We've got no response!

基金会职员在屏幕上敲下另一串密码，试图切入新的线路。\
Name Day types in another string of passwords, trying to break into a new channel.

第一次，第二次。闪烁的红光依旧刺目。\
The first time, the second time. The blinking red light remains blinding.

**冷周六**：立刻尝试远程连接监测器。\
**Hissabeth**: Connect to the monitor directly.

她注意到自己和玩偶之间有一根绳索。就像她练习时常用的那样。\
She notices a rope between her and the doll. It's a familiar style, like the ones she used to practice on.

在确认状况之前，视野里闪过的亮色先吸引了她的注意。\
She tries to orient herself, only for a flash of brightness to grab her attention first.

**库珀花环**：这是……星球。\
**Kiperina**: This is a planet.

**库珀花环**：简直可以看清地表起伏，多精致的道具……\
**Kiperina**: I can see the rise and fall of the landscape. It's so strange here.

**玩偶**：‘@#%￥！&#%！\
**Doll**: ‘@#%￥！&#%！

**库珀花环**：别往前跑，还没确认这里的安全！\
**Kiperina**: Come back. I need to record what I'm seeing here.

她拽住了那条绳索，紧接着，她不得不站在原地。\
She grabs the rope, but she's forced to stop in her tracks.

像碰翻了弹珠盒子，星球在几次震颤后崩毁，声音清脆。它爆发出绚烂但短暂的亮光。\
Like knocking over a box of marbles, planets shatter after a few tremors, bursting into radiant, fleeting flashes of light.

**库珀花环**：周围是不是变得更暗了……？\
**Kiperina**: Are those lights getting dimmer?

**库珀花环**：我得往前走才行。\
**Kiperina**: I need to keep going.

她踢到了什么东西。\
She kicks something.

**库珀花环**：一个小雕像？\
**Kiperina**: A figurine?

它很重，也很粗糙，陷在地面的黑暗之中。\
It's heavy and rough, embedded in the darkness of the ground.

带上它对前进并无助益。\
Bringing it along would only slow her down.

**库珀花环**：我能带上它，我还有力气。\
**Kiperina**: I think I need to take this with me.

她伸出手，试图把这条小蛇从未知的暗处抢过来。\
She reaches out, trying to snatch the figurine from whatever darkness it's caught in.

**库珀花环**：光线在逐渐消失。我得走快些。\
**Kiperina**: The lights are fading out. I need to move faster.

她没有需要切割的东西，也无需对谁挥动刀刃。\
She has nothing she needs to cut, no one to swing the blade at.

但她还是弯下腰。周围依旧寂静，似乎自亘古以来就是如此。\
Even so, she bends down to pick it up. The silence around her feels ancient, as if it's always been there.

**库珀花环**：只有这条路了。\
**Kiperina**: The only path left.

**库珀花环**：我知道怎么保持平衡，这应该是我最擅长的事。\
**Kiperina**: This won't be a problem. I've lived my whole life keeping balanced on a thin wire.

一小炉香灰。\
A small burner of incense ash.

生锈的尺规。\
A rusted calibrator.

被抱在怀里的东西越来越多，她的脚步也跟着变慢。绳索还牵在她的右手里，但玩偶已经隐没在几乎贴近鼻尖的黑暗中。\
Her arms are filling up, and her steps slowing under the weight. The rope is still in her right hand, but the doll has vanished into the darkness, inches from her nose.

**库珀花环**：……\
**Kiperina**: ...

她腾不出手来，只能勉强捏住小人的帽子，试图把它们也捎带上。\
She has no free hand left, barely able to pinch the circus figurines' hats, trying to take them along too.

这已经是她能做的最大努力。\
This is the most she can manage.

**命名日**：还有七分钟。监测器远程连接稳定。\
**Name Day**: Seven minutes left. The connection to the monitor is stable.

**冷周六**：进行倒计时播送，重复三次后启动监测器的自动程序。\
**Hissabeth**: Start the countdown. We'll try it another three times. If we still don't get a response after that, we'll need to activate the monitor's auto return program.

**冷周六**：虽然那玩意基本上只会闷头往前冲，但总得试试。\
**Hissabeth**: I don't have a lot of hope in that basket case of a monitor, but if it's our only option ...

**冷周六**：继续尝试联系她。我不相信库珀花环会在这时候就失败。\
**Hissabeth**: Just keep hailing her. We have to put our trust in Kiperina.

**玩偶**：‘@#%￥！&#%！\
**Doll**: ‘@#%￥！&#%！

**库珀花环**：你要去哪里？那很危险！\
**Kiperina**: Where are you going? It's dangerous there!

绳索瞬间绷紧，将她往远处拉扯。她不得不使出全身的力气，双手将笨拙的玩偶往回拽。\
The rope goes taut, yanking her backward. She has to use every ounce of strength, hauling the strange doll back with both hands.

想要兼顾所有事是不可能的。\
Trying to hold onto everything at once is impossible.

**库珀花环**：——！不、我没想这样！\
**Kiperina**: No! Not like this!

她怀抱的东西都轻易地消散了，像坠入海面的几滴水珠。\
The objects in her arms scatter outwards, drifting like mist before vanishing into the sea.

宇宙诞生之初，一切都是尘埃。往后也是如此。\
At the dawn of the universe, all things were dust. So it remains.

任何东西在宇宙的尺度都会变得微不足道，去探究它又有什么意义？\
All things become insignificant when examined on a cosmic scale. What meaning is there in chasing it?

时间或许是只对人起作用的概念。\
Maybe time is a concept that only holds meaning for humanity.

一生二，二生三，三生万物。\
Out of one, two is born; out of two, three; out of three, everything.

从一粒原子开始。\
It all started from an atom.

你一生的故事都在其中。\
Your entire life story is in there.

她感到四周忽然安静了下来，耳边只能听到头盔内自己的呼吸声。\
There's no sound anymore. Just her breathing inside the helmet and the beat of her heart in her ears.

**库珀花环**：我的确是渺小的、短暂的存在。\
有许许多多像我这样渺小而短暂的存在，始终在向这个世界寻求一个答案。\
**Kiperina**: My existence will be small and short. There are many, many others like me, searching for answers from the universe.

**库珀花环**：但我们没有发现……宇宙并没有为我们准备好那个答案。\
是我们自己赋予了万物意义。\
**Kiperina**: But there is no answer to be found. No answers but the ones we choose for ourselves.

**库珀花环**：一直都是我们自己。\
**Kiperina**: It's been our choice the whole time.

**库珀花环**：我不想否认已经度过的日子，也不想去揣测未来会变成什么样。没时间用来遗憾。\
**Kiperina**: The past is in the past, and the future will wait for us. There is no time to be spared on regrets in the moment.

**库珀花环**：无论消失的事物会不会回来，我都要往前走，去确认存在于远方的一切。\
**Kiperina**: I must keep going, venture further into this world to uncover what's in the distance, to know whether things that vanish come back or not.

**库珀花环**：直到我一生的结束。\
**Kiperina**: I must keep going or die trying.

**监测器**：成功到达指定坐标。\
**Monitor**: We have reached our designated coordinates.

## CO-19 你并不孤单 / You Are Not Alone

**库珀花环**：我成功了吗……？\
**Kiperina**: I made it?

耳机里没有传来任何声音。电子设备在一些时候远比肉体脆弱。\
No sound comes through the headset. Electronic devices can sometimes be more fragile than flesh.

**库珀花环**：监测装置亮着灯，看上去和之前训练里一样。\
**Kiperina**: The indicator light is on, just like in my training.

**库珀花环**：坐标也没有太大误差。好……\
**Kiperina**: The coordinates are, well, close enough. Good.

**库珀花环**：就只是这样。\
**Kiperina**: The rest is simple.

旅行者一号在离开太阳系之前调转镜头，最后注视了一次自己的来处。\
Before leaving the solar system, Voyager 1 turns its camera around, taking one final look at where it came from,

一枚0.12像素大小的光点。\
a 0.12-pixel speck of light,

使其上的生命明白了天地广袤。\
letting the life contained within it know just how vast the heavens truly are.

返回舱内之前，宇航员最后望了一眼漫无边际的星空。\
Before returning to the cabin, the little astronaut takes one last look at the boundless stars.

组成万物的每颗原子都诞生于这片黑暗。\
Every atom of everything was born in this darkness.

连接自己与地球的只是肉眼无法看到的信号，连接自己与监测器的只是一根绳索。\
All that links her to Earth is a signal invisible to the naked eye. All that links her to the monitor is a single rope.

如果松开手，就会永远地漂浮在庞大的宇宙中，被它包围。这无声息的、近乎永恒的沉默。\
If she lets go, she'll drift forever through the vastness of the universe, surrounded by it. Soundless, eternal silence.

曾踏出的一步，我们再也无法重现。永恒的花朵，完整的天空。前方空无一物，仅有一句承诺。 ——曼德尔施塔姆 《给娜塔雅·施坦碧尔》\
That which was movement once shall be removed …Flowers are immortal, the sky is all-embracing,And what will be is no more than a promise. Poems to Natalya Shtempel —Osip Mandelstam

她知道眼前所见会被抹去。自己的国家、故乡，曾拥有的身份、尝过的食物、结识的友人，最终都只会刻在记忆里。\
She knows what she sees will be wiped away. Her country, her home, her past identity, the food she's tasted, the friends she's known—eventually they'll only live in memory.

然而记忆的保质期可称短暂。群星回馈给这些短暂之物的也只有寂静。\
And memory, too, has a notoriously short shelf life. The stars remember nothing.

恒星的消亡尚且无声，一片土地，抑或一个词语的离去又怎么可能足够响亮呢？\
The universe does not mourn the death of a star. How could the loss of a country, a person, or a single word be truly remembered?

对于一位年轻宇航员的消失，宇宙自然也应当无动于衷。\
The disappearance of a young astronaut deserves no more reaction from the universe than that.

**库珀花环**：我该抓紧时间，回到地面……\
**Kiperina**: I need to get back. I need to get back to Earth.

**库珀花环**：我……\
**Kiperina**: I ...

幻觉带来的影响尚未完全消退，她耳后的血管仍然一阵阵抽动着发痛。\
The aftereffects of the hallucination haven't completely faded. The veins behind her ears pulse with pain.

死亡是一粒果核。她怀揣的小小的死亡，此刻无限地贴近皮肤表面。\
Death is a fruit pit. The small death she carries is now pressed close to the surface of her skin.

她松开手掌，在脑海里勾勒出那道笔迹。它可能已经被汗水融成了模糊的红色。\
She opens her palm and sketches the pattern into her mind. It's likely it's already been blurred by her sweat.

**库珀花环**：我能应对一切……只要先……\
**Kiperina**: I can have this handled. First, I need to ...

先站稳。在一根纤细的钢丝上找到立足之地。\
Steady yourself. Find your footing on a strand-thin wire.

它真的存在吗？\
Is it even there?

**库珀花环**：……\
**Kiperina**: ...

**含章鼎**：信号彻底中断了！\
**Han Zhang**: We lost the signal!

**命名日**：切了第二条线路，再试。\
**Name Day**: Switch to line two and try again.

**含章鼎**：备用线路测试。二号失联。三号失联……四号……失联。\
**Han Zhang**: Testing comm backup line. Line two, lost. Line three, lost. Line four, lost.

操作台上亮起四盏红灯，显示屏提醒着最后的四分钟倒计时。\
Four red lights blink on the console. The display shows the final four-minute countdown.

**冷周六**：再次尝试通讯。\
**Hissabeth**: Keep trying to reconnect.

**库珀花环**：……\
**Kiperina**: ...

**库珀花环**：再次尝试通讯……\
**Kiperina**: Reconnecting ...

**库珀花环**：通讯失败。\
**Kiperina**: Connection lost.

她无法及时回到舱内，安全绳上的卡扣锁死了。\
She won't be able to get back inside the cabin in time. The buckle on the safety tether has locked in place.

检测到超标的神秘术波动或者特殊环境，卡扣自动锁紧避免滑脱。这本来是贴心的防护措施，但设计者没有预料到有人使用它就是为了更好地解开。\
When detecting excess arcane fluctuations or hazardous environment, the buckle will automatically lock to prevent slippage. It was meant to be a thoughtful safety feature, but its designer never imagined someone would want to unlock it on purpose.

**库珀花环**：我应该想到的！这不是我在马戏团用的普通的绳索……\
**Kiperina**: I should have thought this through! This isn't like the rope I used in the circus.

**库珀花环**：不行，这样下去监测装置会被拖离轨道。\
**Kiperina**: No, if I do that, the monitor will be pulled out of sync.

还有多久？还能做些什么？松开手，面对失败？\
How much longer do I have? What else can I do? Should I just let go and accept my failure?

为了近在眼前的成就牺牲？他们会在墓碑上称我为英雄？\
Has what I've done so far been enough? Will they call me a hero when they write my name over an empty tomb?

会吗？更可能是乌特恩亚亚的孩子，拉普拉斯编外成员，理线学学徒……\
Face it. I won't die a hero. I'll just be a circus girl from Utrennyaya, a temporary Laplace Employee, or an apprentice Ley Line Hunter.

近乎静止的几分钟后，冷周六敲下了按键。\
After a few minutes near motionless, Hissabeth presses the button.

**冷周六**：停止测试，保持主线路通讯。\
**Hissabeth**: Okay, forget the backups. Switch to the main connection.

**冷周六**：立刻做撤离准备。五十秒之后我会启动返航程序。\
**Hissabeth**: Start evacuation preparations now. I'll activate the return program in fifty seconds.

**命名日**：我们怎么确认她已经进了返回舱？！\
**Name Day**: But how will we know if she's in the return capsule?

**冷周六**：四十秒。不追上时间，她就没有一点希望。\
**Hissabeth**: Forty seconds—We won't. Either she makes it, or she doesn't. It's out of our hands.

**冷周六**：只有在“暴雨”降临的临界线上，神秘术才能得到足够的增幅，才能实现这么远距离的定点传送。\
**Hissabeth**: The teleportation ritual won't have enough energy if it isn't at the exact critical moment of the "Storm."

**冷周六**：我相信她一定会尽最大的努力准时回家。\
**Hissabeth**: I have faith in her. She'll come home.

阿涅娅。回家。\
Alia. Come home.

**库珀花环**：我必须回去。还有人在地面等着我。\
**Kiperina**: I have to go home. People are waiting for me down there.

**库珀花环**：时间应该不多了……我需要……\
**Kiperina**: But I don't have much time. I need something.

一把刀。\
剧情场景-温室实验室

**冷周六**：如果你能帮我把这些文件变成一把刀，我会很感激你。\
**Hissabeth**: Maybe you can turn them into a knife or something.

**冷周六**：虽然派不上大用场，至少它们还能拿来切切水果。\
**Hissabeth**: A knife would be more useful at this point. You know, to cut fruit or whatever.

**命名日**：这个不行。你桌上废弃的名片可以。\
**Name Day**: Actually, that card there on the table would work better for that.

**冷周六**：有什么特别的？\
**Hissabeth**: Why is that?

**命名日**：材质。金属名片不算常见，它们做武器会比用于自我介绍更好。\
**Name Day**: It's all about the material. Metal makes a better edge than paper. Never quite understood why you made them like that.

**冷周六**：那是我之前研制的新型材料。北方哨歌和指针的名片也都是我做的，受热就会变锋利，在手里捏一会儿能当拆信刀用……\
**Hissabeth**: Oh. I was testing out the new alloy. I used it to make Windsong's and Pointer's cards. It gets harder and sharper when heated. Give it a rub with your hands, and you can use it as a letter opener.

拆信刀。\
A letter opener.

她习惯性地把那张来自北方哨歌的名片贴身携带，现在它也在宇航服的口袋里。\
She always keeps that name card from Windsong close at hand. It's in her space suit pocket now.

她也知道怎么穿着这身衣服使用自己的神秘术。这是她主要的训练任务。\
She learned how to cast her arcane skill while suited up. It had been a core part of her training.

**库珀花环**：——理线学万岁！\
**Kiperina**: Ley Lines, of course! Thank you, Ms. Windsong!

感谢新型材料的锋利，感谢安全绳没有坚不可摧，感谢理线学。\
Thanks to the sharpness of the new material, thanks to the safety tether not being unbreakable, thanks to the study of ley lines.

三十秒。\
Thirty seconds.

基金会职员最后确认了输入的坐标。\
Name Day confirms the final coordinates.

二十秒。\
Twenty seconds.

**含章鼎**：虽然我一直不想说但现在应该抓紧机会认识你们还是很荣幸的如果活下来找我进货可以打折！\
**Han Zhang**: It was a pleasure working with all of you. If we survive this, I'm giving you permanent discounts at my store. Provided we survive.

**冷周六**：任何材料都打折？！我死也会记住！\
**Hissabeth**: How big are these discounts? Tell me now. I need to know how much I will live!

她没忘记抓住旁边还在好奇地端详设备的女孩儿。\
She doesn't forget to grab Voyager beside her, who would otherwise have stayed there examining the equipment.

**冷周六**：收起来，小提琴是易碎物品——\
**Hissabeth**: Stay away, please. Your violin is fragile.

十秒。\
Ten seconds.

**命名日**：我希望死后的世界有双休！\
**Name Day**: I hope there will still be weekends in the afterlife.

**冷周六**：三倍加班费！！\
**Hissabeth**: If there is anything after this, then we deserve overtime pay for all eternity.

**含章鼎**：我真的讨厌工作狂！！！\
**Han Zhang**: How can you be thinking of work right now!

一秒。\
One second.

舱门在她身后关闭。\
The hatch seals shut behind her.

**系统提示音Ⅰ**：返回舱分离准备已完毕。坐标校验完毕。\
**Notification I**: The return capsule is ready to detach. Coordinate calibration complete.

**系统提示音Ⅰ**：请及时回到座位。\
**Notification I**: Please return to your seat.

**库珀花环**：看来大家的进展很顺利。\
**Kiperina**: It looks like everything worked out smoothly.

陷在座椅里，捏紧软盘，她闭上眼睛。\
She sinks into the seat, grips the disk tightly, and shuts her eyes.

**库珀花环**：我会成功的。这是最后的、最简单的一步了。\
**Kiperina**: Yes, I will make it. This is the last step. The simplest one.

**库珀花环**：……回家。\
**Kiperina**: Take me home.

**拉普拉斯职员Ⅲ**：——！\
**Laplace Staff Member III**: ...!

**拉普拉斯职员Ⅱ**：我听错了吗？这是——\
**Laplace Staff Member II**: Is it me, or?

**系统提示音Ⅱ**：成像数据回传结束。\
**Notification II**: Imaging data transmission complete.

**系统提示音Ⅱ**：二次确认坐标，赤经：14h，49m，09.55s……\
**Notification II**: Reconfirming coordinates. RA: 14h, 49m, 09.55s ...

比起突然出现在地板上倒作一堆的人，电子播报音先吸引了研究员们的注意。\
More fascinating than the figures who suddenly collapsed in a heap on their floor, it's the voice of the system that first grabs the staff members' attention.

实验事故在拉普拉斯算不上稀奇事。但惊人的成果总能赢得掌声。\
Experimental accidents aren't unusual at Laplace. But astonishing results always earn attention.

**拉普拉斯职员Ⅲ**：你瞧，那是冷周六。我说过她头上的蛇的确有独立意识，有一条没有晕过去。\
**Laplace Staff Member III**: Look, that's Hissabeth. See the snakes on her head? Seems like one of them's still awake. Told you they have independent minds.

**拉普拉斯职员Ⅱ**：和她一起的怎么像那群灰白格子……我们已经沦落到要去仓库抢材料了么？\
**Laplace Staff Member II**: Hold on. Those two work with the Foundation.

**指针**：别挡在这里！去申请紧急医疗援助，快点！\
**Pointer**: Out of the way! Go get medical support now!

**拉普拉斯职员Ⅱ**：哦哦，指针这家伙我倒认识。她这么着急，这群家伙……那个航天小组，对。他们又失败了？\
**Laplace Staff Member II**: That's Miss Pointer, isn't it? So then this must be the team from the Space Monitor Project. Have they failed again?

**拉普拉斯职员Ⅲ**：不，他们……如果这真的是从太空回传的数据……\
**Laplace Staff Member III**: Hold on. Check it out! If this data is really from the space monitor ...

**系统提示音Ⅱ**：赤纬：-102°，05'，45.82"。\
**Notification II**: DEC: –102°, 05m, 45.82s.

**拉普拉斯广播**：“暴雨”降临。请注意避险。\
重复，“暴雨”降临……\
**Laplace Broadcast**: The "Storm" is here. Please take precautions. Repeat, the "Storm" is here.

**拉普拉斯职员Ⅱ**：他们成功了……他们成功了！\
**Laplace Staff Member II**: It's all here. They really did it. They did it!

……\
...

播报声毫无准备地灌入耳中。\
The voice of a broadcast floods into her awareness.

**电台节目**：“工程师们正寻找有效手段，以缓解高压、高温的极端环境带来的影响……”\
**Radio**: "Our engineers are currently developing measures to minimize the effects of the high pressure and temperature ..."

**库珀花环**：……？我……\
**Kiperina**: I ...

**库珀花环**：我回到了……地面。\
**Kiperina**: I'm on Earth.

**电台节目**：“1970年至今，钻探工作已持续七年，即将超越伯沙罗杰斯钻洞的9583米深度纪录……”\
**Radio**: "Beginning in 1970, the current drilling project has been a labor of the past seven years. Its depth is predicted to soon surpass that of the Bertha Rogers Hole at 9583 meters ..."

**库珀花环**：这时候……科兹洛夫先生刚收养我。\
**Kiperina**: 1977, that was the year that Mr. Kozlov found me.

**库珀花环**：我是不是还能见到他们？\
**Kiperina**: Could that mean that I will be able to see them again?

有许多人怀揣着同样的疑问。也有许多事在这场雨之后改变了。\
Many people had the same questions she did as they awoke. Many things changed after that "Storm."

一只手轻轻拍了拍她的肩膀。\
A hand grips her shoulder.

**维拉**：你要先照顾好自己，孩子。\
**Vila**: You'll need to take care of yourself first, little astronaut.

**维拉**：想重建生活，需要足够健康的身体。那些关心你的人，一定希望见面时你看起来过得很好。\
**Vila**: Rebuilding a life requires a healthy body first. But I'm certain you are in good hands here.

**库珀花环**：谢谢您。您是……\
**Kiperina**: Thank you, but who are ...

**北方哨歌**：维拉，我的朋友。一位最亲切的同志。\
**Windsong**: This is my friend, Vila. My dearest, bravest comrade.

**北方哨歌**：这是库珀花环，我的学生。我能这样介绍吗？\
**Windsong**: And this is Kiperina. Would you mind if I introduced you as my apprentice?

**库珀花环**：当然……我已经做好了决定。\
**Kiperina**: Not at all. I've made up my mind.

**库珀花环**：我想继续学习理线学。\
**Kiperina**: I want to keep learning The Study of Ley Lines.

**北方哨歌**：这是我今天听到的第二个好消息。\
**Windsong**: That's the second-best news I've heard today.

**北方哨歌**：冷周六、命名日和含章鼎也都还在病房里躺着，指针急得够呛，刚才还说要等他们彻底康复再把他们挨个揍进急诊室……\
**Windsong**: Hissabeth, Name Day, and Han Zhang are all still recovering in bed. You should've seen Pointer. She was mad as all hell. Claimed she'd be waiting for them to recover so she could whoop them back into the recovery ward.

**北方哨歌**：我就从那边溜了，来看看自己的学生。\
**Windsong**: Anyways, I thought I'd best avoid that scene and pay a visit to my new apprentice.

**库珀花环**：第一个好消息是我们成功了，对不对？\
**Kiperina**: So, then the best news you had today—we did it, right?

**北方哨歌**：我想这算是件好事，但没有那么重要。\
**Windsong**: That's good news for sure. But still not the best.

隔着病床柔软的被单，另一只手捉住了库珀花环的手掌。\
Beneath the soft sheets of the hospital bed, another hand clasps Kiperina's.

**远旅**：……\
**Voyager**: ...

这是最好的消息。\
This is the best news.

欢迎回家。\
Welcome home.

## CO-20 宇宙无事发生 / As If Nothing Happened up There

白色石墙将世界分隔成里侧与外侧，同时也带来了长久的寂静。\
A white stonewall divides the world into inside and outside.

逐渐靠近的脚步声与说话声令这份寂静骤然消散。\
Footsteps and voices draw closer, abruptly breaking the silence of the courtyard.

**基金会职员Ⅰ**：拉普拉斯说要研究的那东西怎么样了？\
**Foundation Staff Member I**: Did we get that progress report on the Laplace teleportation project?

**基金会职员Ⅱ**：你说传送软盘吗？上次会议里提到过，它很快就会登上外勤物资申请单。\
**Foundation Staff Member II**: The teleport disk? Yeah, I guess it was a big success. They're already working on the field mission applications.

**基金会职员Ⅱ**：如果它能彻底普及开，让我每天下班直接传送回宿舍，我愿意称它是最伟大的发明。\
**Foundation Staff Member II**: Imagine if they could put it into mass production. I'd use it to commute straight to work. No more traffic.

**基金会职员Ⅰ**：算了吧，万一反过来缩短我们的集合时间呢？真这样方便，你不就得随叫随到了吗？\
**Foundation Staff Member I**: You'd better hope not. They'll start using it to summon us straight from home. It'll be like being on-call 24/7.

**基金会职员Ⅱ**：天哪，你说得对！我受不了了，拉普拉斯那群工作狂——\
**Foundation Staff Member II**: Holy moly! I didn't think of that. Worse still, those Laplace workaholics would probably enjoy it.

**基金会职员Ⅰ**：起码他们真搞到了“暴雨”相关的数据，这可是件大活儿。\
**Foundation Staff Member I**: Well, it's not all bad. We got the data—real-time observation of the universe during the "Storm" from outer space. That's huge.

**基金会职员Ⅰ**：全宇宙都会被回溯，还挺公平嘛……至少不是只有地球倒霉。\
**Foundation Staff Member I**: I'll say, looks like the whole universe is getting reversed, though. I mean, at least it's nice to know we aren't alone.

**基金会职员Ⅱ**：哈，兄弟，我就欣赏你这份乐观。\
**Foundation Staff Member II**: That's the spirit, man. Look for the silver lining.

**基金会职员Ⅱ**：为什么那个航天小队不是公开招募？谁不想去宇宙里瞧瞧呢？换成我，我恨不得在宿舍门口拉上横幅，到时候还要把这事迹刻在墓碑上！\
**Foundation Staff Member II**: Why on earth wasn't that project an open volunteer call? Who wouldn't want to go to space? If I got the chance to spacewalk, I'd never let anyone forget it. You'd see it on my tombstone.

**基金会职员Ⅰ**：万一有下次机会呢？说起来，拉普拉斯的人我不熟，但我认识他们队里基金会的小子。可惜命名日好像又去跑外勤了，到时候可以约他喝酒，打探点新鲜消息。\
**Foundation Staff Member I**: I know someone on their team, Name Day. I'll ask him about it next time we're out for a drink. Too bad he is already out on another field mission.

**基金会职员Ⅰ**：他还是航天小队的成员，意味着他要打两份工，哇哦。\
**Foundation Staff Member I**: He's working for Laplace now too. Working two jobs at once, wow!

**基金会职员Ⅱ**：你怎么认识那么多工作狂？我要重新审视你了！\
**Foundation Staff Member II**: Is that admiration I hear? I thought you didn't like workaholics.

**基金会职员Ⅱ**：但日子确实好起来了。我们会解决“暴雨”，我相信这不过是眨眼的事……\
**Foundation Staff Member II**: I just don't want to be one. Still, things are going better now. We'll have this little "Storm" problem solved soon enough.

**基金会职员Ⅰ**：嘘……阿尔文，你听到没有？\
**Foundation Staff Member I**: Shh, Alvin, did you hear that?

**基金会职员Ⅱ**：你说啥……哦。\
**Foundation Staff Member II**: What? Oh.

这里不常有琴声。忙碌的职员们最近才重新拾起一些过去的爱好。\
Music is rare in this place. But recently the ever-busy staff have felt in the right spirit to revisit old hobbies.

这是一支相当有名的曲子，它曾与另外二十六支歌曲共同穿越茫茫群星，至今也仍在途中。\
This is a well-known piece, one that once traveled with 26 other songs across the star fields, and still drifts there today.

**远旅**：……\
**Voyager**: ...

当陈旧的岁月淹没了这一代人，你仍将栖息在人群之中，为人的朋友。\
When old age shall this generation waste,Thou shalt remain, in midst of other woe.

**冷周六**：我知道这支曲子，指针经常在办公室播那盘录音带。她说是金唱片母带的翻录。\
**Hissabeth**: I know the piece. Pointer often plays that record in her office. She said it's a track from the Golden Record.

**冷周六**：就是旅行者一号带着的那张。\
**Hissabeth**: The same record that Voyager 1 carries.

**命名日**：1987年它在哪儿呢？已经到太阳系边缘了吗？\
**Name Day**: Where would it have been in 1987? At the edge of the solar system?

**冷周六**：它的动力要到2025年才耗尽，我说的是没有发生“暴雨”的那个2025。\
**Hissabeth**: Its power won't run out until 2025, so long as there's no "Storm" to stop it.

**库珀花环**：耗尽动力会怎么样？它会停下？或者损坏？\
**Kiperina**: What will happen to it when it runs out? Will it stop? Or be destroyed?

**冷周六**：没那么严重，只是我们不会再得知它的下落。\
**Hissabeth**: No, nothing quite so bad. It just won't be able to send signals back to us.

**冷周六**：它会一直在宇宙中前行，继续它的旅程。如果真有外星文明，也许会在什么时候发现它。\
**Hissabeth**: It will keep flying forward in space, continuing its endless journey. And if there is some alien life out there in the universe, they might find it some day.

**冷周六**：可能那时候地球已经不复存在。\
**Hissabeth**: Perhaps many millions of years after the Earth is gone, swallowed up by the Sun or the "Storm."

**冷周六**：等得太久了，花了太多时间和资源，又无法得到回应。听上去比我们这群人的神秘术还要没用。\
**Hissabeth**: To spend so much time and resources on something that won't respond to us after such a short time on a universal scale. It sounds even more useless than our arcane skills.

在注视头顶闪烁的光点时，人们很难想象自己脚下的星球也不过是宇宙中的一个小点。\
When staring at the flickering lights above, it's hard to imagine that the planet beneath our feet is nothing more than a speck in the universe.

你会遇上另一些哀愁，并对人说起真实的美丽。\
Than ours, a friend to man, to whom thou say'st,"Beauty is truth, truth beauty."

**含章鼎**：这本就是一封并不期待回应的信件。\
**Han Zhang**: They didn't send it out expecting to get a quick response.

**冷周六**：啊，我想是的。我觉得它只是一个招呼，一句问候。\
**Hissabeth**: You're right. I suppose it's just like a friendly greeting.

一种象征。\
A symbol.

**冷周六**：“嗨，你们好。这里是地球，这里有过文明。我们尝试活着，或许会成功地战胜时间。”\
**Hissabeth**: "Hi there. This is a gift from Earth, a place where life existed. We're trying to survive, but we may be defeated in time."

**冷周六**：或许等不到结果，但我个人相信会有谁听见这句问候。\
**Hissabeth**: Aliens or not, it's likely that it will just drift in space forever, but personally, I want to believe that someone's going to listen to that record one day.

**命名日**：库珀花环小姐说不定能带回答案。如果你在宇宙里见到了上帝，帮我问问他最喜欢什么音乐。\
**Name Day**: Maybe Ms. Kiperina can help us. If you see God up there in space, be sure to ask him what's his favorite piece on the record.

**库珀花环**：我想这该算是付费服务，请考虑把你的骨碟收藏分给我。\
**Kiperina**: That kind of service is going to cost you. You'll have to pay up with your rib collection.

**含章鼎**：总之我们要先抵达九九年之后的世界，才有机会搞清楚金唱片的下落。\
**Han Zhang**: Before we start thinking about that, we will still need to cross the year 1999, then we can figure out where that record will end up.

远旅认真地听着每一句话，有些她能理解，有些她还无法完全弄清。\
Voyager listens intently to every word. Some she understands; many others lie beyond her reach.

但她也有想要与朋友们分享的东西。\
But she has something she wants to share with her friends.

这是为小队的友人们奏响的曲调，是为勇敢的小宇航员送去的祝福与鼓励。\
A melody played for her teammates. A blessing and encouragement for a brave little astronaut.

是来自64亿光年外的回答。\
A reply from 6.4 billion light-years away.

信件送达了。收件人是一颗会唱歌的星星。\
The message has been delivered. The recipient: a star that sings.

这就是全部。你们在尘世所知晓，且应知晓的事物。 ——济慈 《希腊古瓮颂》\
That is all.Ye know on earth, and all ye need to know. Ode on a Grecian Urn —John Keats

**众人**：三。\
**All**: Three.

**众人**：二。\
**All**: Two.

**众人**：一。\
**All**: One.

她的种族并不具备地球生物理解中的“听觉”。但她有自己的方式理解其上承载的信息。\
Her species lacks what earth creatures call "hearing." But she has her own way of interpreting auditory information.

那是她从未想象过，从未感受过的……旋律。\
It's a melody unlike anything she's ever imagined—never felt before.

它来自那个黯淡的蓝色光点。\
It comes from that faint blue dot:

地球。\
Earth.

Невероятно.不可思议的。\
Невероятно.Unbelievable.

Вечный.永恒的。\
Вечный.Eternal.

Красивая.美丽的。\
Красивая.Beautiful.

**基金会职员Ⅰ**：这首歌还挺好听。\
**Foundation Staff Member I**: Hmm, it sounds nice.

**基金会职员Ⅱ**：那就多听一会儿——等等，你要去哪儿？\
**Foundation Staff Member II**: Then keep listening. Wait, where are you going?

**基金会职员Ⅰ**：我们走吧，别打扰其他人。\
**Foundation Staff Member I**: Just let them do their thing. We should go now. We've got more work waiting for us.

**基金会职员Ⅰ**：手上还有活儿要干呢，你之前说的传送软盘领用申请，要怎么提交来着？\
**Foundation Staff Member I**: By the way, you were talking about those disks being prepared for field service, right?

**基金会职员Ⅱ**：具体事项还不清楚，过几天指针女士应该会进行相关内容的宣讲……\
**Foundation Staff Member II**: Yeah, but I told you everything I know. Ms. Pointer should give us the details in a few days.

**基金会职员Ⅰ**：冷周六小姐这么忙吗？怪不得那天的庆祝会她只派几条蛇露了个面。北方哨歌女士和维拉女士倒是留到了最后，噢，还有被那群孩子包围的库珀花环小姐……\
**Foundation Staff Member I**: Not Ms. Hissabeth, huh? She seems real busy. I guess that's why she only sent one of her snakes to the victory party? I saw Windsong and Vila, though. Oh, and Kiperina was there surrounded by a bunch of kids, and they all stuck around right till the end.

**基金会职员Ⅰ**：芝诺的家伙听见有酒喝就肯定到场，那位年轻飞行员和一条蝾螈划拳拼酒……\
**Foundation Staff Member I**: There were a few Zeno guys there too. Whenever there's booze, you can count on them showing up. I think I saw one of their pilots having a drinking contest with a newt. Crazy!

**基金会职员Ⅰ**：后来乌尔里希先生也过去看，再后来我听到命名日在劝兔毛手袋别站在桌上发表总统就任演讲。\
**Foundation Staff Member I**: They even roped in Mr. Ulrich. I caught Name Day desperately stopping Medicine Pocket from climbing up on a table to recite a speech.

**基金会职员Ⅰ**：虽然最后合影时那上头挤满了人。\
**Foundation Staff Member I**: It was good fun. They even snapped a picture of it by the end.

**基金会职员Ⅱ**：我错过得太多了！不是说路德维希先生很关注职员的心理状态，鼓励他们放松吗？下次活动到底在什么时候——一定还有下次吧？！\
**Foundation Staff Member II**: It's a shame I missed it. I heard Mr. Ludwig values employees' mental health, so at least he'll be hosting more of those parties soon, right? RIGHT?

脚步声与话语声逐渐远去，琴声也随之止息。\
The footsteps and voices fade away, and the sound of the violin comes to an end.

星星用好奇的闪烁打量着这片土地。遥远的蓝色星球。京兆分之一的奇迹。\
The star looks down on this land with curious twinkles. This distant blue planet. A one-in-ten-quadrillion miracle.

她得到了金色的、珍贵的声音，于是也在这儿留下自己的声音。\
She has received golden, precious sounds and now leaves behind a voice of her own.

**远旅**：*一段轻快的哼唱*\
**Voyager**: *humming*

她学会的第一首歌。\
The first song she learned.

为那些在普列谢茨克的日子，为今后的岁月，为她所认识与铭记的。\
For the days at Plesetsk. For the days to come. For those she knew and remembers.

为文明的遥远回声。\
For the distant echoes of civilization.

**远旅**：请……听。\
**Voyager**: Please listen.

在这颗星球上，她目睹了前所未见的景象。\
On this planet, she has witnessed sights she never knew existed.

朋友。\
Friends

勇敢的访客。\
Brave visitors.

四季的更替，海岸线的蜿蜒，温暖或寒冷，和平或纷争。\
The changing seasons, winding coastlines, warmth and cold, peace and conflict.

贫穷与富裕，卑劣与高尚。文明的衰落与崛起，雨燕划过天空的轨迹。\
Poverty and wealth, cruelty and nobility. The rise and fall of civilizations, the birds slicing through the sky.

在银河系中的一粒微尘之上。\
All on a single speck of dust in the Milky Way.

**远旅**：多美丽啊……群星。\
**Voyager**: How beautiful ... the stars are.

看似无用的探索改变了一切。正如遥远的星星改变了你。\
One seemingly useless exploration changes everything.Just as a star from afar changes you.

1987 宇宙组曲\
1987 Cosmic Overture
